const TZ = 'Asia/Seoul';
const STUDENT_QR_GPS_LAT = 37.6593055556;
const STUDENT_QR_GPS_LNG = 126.6248333333;
const STUDENT_QR_GPS_RADIUS_M = 30;
const TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME = '자투리 출석부 생성';
const CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME = '자투리 당월 출석부 수정';
const LOG_SHEET_NAME = '자투리 로그';
const SETTINGS_SHEET_NAME = '자투리 설정';
const DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME = '자투리 시스템 일별점수';
const ADMIN_PASSWORD = '17752';
const ROSTER_ROW_COUNT = 60;
const HEADER_ROW = 1;
const FIRST_DATA_ROW = 2;
const SPECIAL_SEATS = ['폐쇄10', '폐쇄29', '폐쇄30', '폐쇄31', '폐쇄32', '폐쇄33', '폐쇄34', '폐쇄35', '폐쇄36', '개방19', '개방20', '개방23', '개방24'];

const DASHBOARD_CACHE_KEY = 'dashboard_payload_v2';

function invalidateDashboardCache_() {
  try { CacheService.getScriptCache().remove(DASHBOARD_CACHE_KEY); } catch (e) {}
}

function appendRowWithScriptLock_(sheet, row, timeoutMs) {
  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(timeoutMs || 10000)) throw new Error('접속이 몰려 처리 대기 중입니다. 잠시 후 다시 시도해 주세요.');
  try {
    const nextRow = Math.max(1, sheet.getLastRow() + 1);
    sheet.getRange(nextRow, 1, 1, row.length).setValues([row]);
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}


function normalizeDateKey_(value) {
  if (!value) return '';
  if (value instanceof Date) return Utilities.formatDate(value, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const text = String(value).trim();
  if (!text) return '';
  const m = text.match(/(\d{4})[-./](\d{1,2})[-./](\d{1,2})/);
  if (m) return `${m[1]}-${String(Number(m[2])).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(Number(m[3])).padStart(2, '0')}`;
  return text;
}

function getAliasMap_() {
  return JSON.parse(PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties().getProperty('ID_ALIAS_MAP') || '{}');
}

function getIdVariantsMapForIds_(ids) {
  const aliasMap = getAliasMap_();
  const result = {};
  ids.forEach(rawId => {
    const currentId = String(rawId || '').trim();
    if (!currentId) return;
    const visited = {};
    const queue = [currentId];
    while (queue.length > 0) {
      const id = queue.shift();
      if (visited[id]) continue;
      visited[id] = true;
      Object.keys(aliasMap).forEach(oldId => {
        if (String(aliasMap[oldId]) === id && !visited[oldId]) queue.push(oldId);
      });
    }
    result[currentId] = Object.keys(visited);
  });
  return result;
}

function buildDailyScoreSummary_(dateKeys, currentMonth) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  const byDate = {};
  const byMonth = {};
  const allowed = {};
  dateKeys.forEach(k => { allowed[k] = true; });
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return { byDate: byDate, byMonth: byMonth };

  const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
  data.forEach(row => {
    const dateKey = normalizeDateKey_(row[0]);
    const month = Number(row[1]);
    const id = String(row[2] || '').trim();
    const score = parseNumber_(row[3]);
    if (!id) return;
    if (allowed[dateKey]) {
      if (!byDate[dateKey]) byDate[dateKey] = {};
      byDate[dateKey][id] = (byDate[dateKey][id] || 0) + score;
    }
    if (month === Number(currentMonth)) {
      byMonth[id] = (byMonth[id] || 0) + score;
    }
  });
  return { byDate: byDate, byMonth: byMonth };
}

function buildPastTotalsById_(currentMonth) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const totals = {};
  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const month = parseJaturiMonthFromName_(sheet.getName());
    if (!month || month >= currentMonth) return;
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (!data.length) return;
    const totalIdx = data[0].indexOf('총점');
    if (totalIdx === -1) return;
    for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
      const id = String(data[r][1] || '').trim();
      if (!id) continue;
      totals[id] = (totals[id] || 0) + parseNumber_(data[r][totalIdx]);
    }
  });
  return totals;
}

function sumByVariants_(mapObj, variants) {
  let total = 0;
  variants.forEach(id => {
    total += parseNumber_(mapObj && mapObj[String(id)]);
  });
  return total;
}

}

  ensureNightCoreSheets_();
  ensureWungjiCoreSheets_();
  rebuildDailyScoresFromJaturiSheets_();
  syncCurrentEditSheetFromCurrentMonth_();
  recalcCurrentMonthTotalsFromDailyScore_();
  invalidateDashboardCache_();

}

}

  initializeAttendanceSystem();
  return 'OK';
}

const APP_TITLE = '자기주도학습 통합관리 시스템';
const APP_ICON_URL = 'https://ryujee79.github.io/self-study-icon/icon-192.png';

function doGet() {
  return HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('index')
    .setTitle(APP_TITLE)
    .setFaviconUrl(APP_ICON_URL)
    .addMetaTag('viewport', 'width=device-width, initial-scale=1')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
}

function onEdit(e) {
  try {
    if (!e || !e.range) return;

    const sheet = e.range.getSheet();
    const sheetName = sheet.getName();
    const a1 = e.range.getA1Notation();

    if (sheetName === TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME) {
      if (a1 === 'G2' && e.value === 'TRUE') {
        try {
          createSelectedMonthSheets_();
        } finally {
          sheet.getRange('G2').setValue(false);
        }
        return;
      }

      if (a1 === 'G3' && e.value === 'TRUE') {
        try {
          deleteSelectedMonthSheets_();
        } finally {
          sheet.getRange('G3').setValue(false);
        }
        return;
      }
      return;
    }

    if (sheetName === NIGHT_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME) {
      if (a1 === 'Q2' && e.value === 'TRUE') {
        try {
          createSelectedNightMonthSheets_();
        } finally {
          sheet.getRange('Q2').setValue(false);
        }
        return;
      }

      if (a1 === 'Q3' && e.value === 'TRUE') {
        try {
          deleteSelectedNightMonthSheets_();
        } finally {
          sheet.getRange('Q3').setValue(false);
        }
        return;
      }
      return;
    }

    if (sheetName === NIGHT_CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME) {
      if (a1 === 'Q3' && e.value === 'TRUE') {
        try {
          moveNightStudentSeatCurrentMonth_();
        } finally {
          sheet.getRange('Q3').setValue(false);
        }
        return;
      }

      if (isNightRosterEditRange_(e.range)) {
        syncNightCurrentEditChangesToCurrentMonth_();
      }
      return;
    }



    const nightDataMatch = sheetName.match(/^야간데이터\((\d{1,2})월\)$/);
    if (nightDataMatch) {
      const month = Number(nightDataMatch[1]);
      const rowStart = e.range.getRow();
      const rowEnd = rowStart + e.range.getNumRows() - 1;
      const colStart = e.range.getColumn();
      const colEnd = colStart + e.range.getNumColumns() - 1;

      const touchesNightRoster = rowEnd >= HEADER_ROW && rowStart <= FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1 &&
        colEnd >= 1 && colStart <= NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS;

      if (touchesNightRoster) {
        refreshNightStudySheetFromSchedule_(month);
        if (month === getCurrentMonthNumber_()) {
          syncNightCurrentEditSheetFromCurrentMonth_();
        }
        invalidateDashboardCache_();
      }
      return;
    }

    if (sheetName === CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME) {
      if (a1 === 'G3' && e.value === 'TRUE') {
        try {
          moveStudentSeatCurrentMonth_();
        } finally {
          sheet.getRange('G3').setValue(false);
        }
        return;
      }

      if (isRosterEditRange_(e.range)) {
        syncCurrentEditChangesToCurrentMonth_();
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast('오류: ' + error.message, '오류', 5);
  }
}

function verifyAdmin(password) {
  return password === ADMIN_PASSWORD;
}

function setTodayPassword(adminPw, newTodayPw) {
  if (adminPw !== ADMIN_PASSWORD) return '❌ 관리자 비밀번호가 틀렸습니다.';
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SETTINGS_SHEET_NAME) || ss.insertSheet(SETTINGS_SHEET_NAME);
  configSheet.getRange('B1').setValue(newTodayPw);
  return '✅ 오늘의 암호가 성공적으로 변경되었습니다.';
}

function getAllStatus() {
  try {
    const dataSheet = getCurrentDataSheet_();
    if (!dataSheet) return [];

    const data = dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 5).getValues();
    const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const results = [];

    data.forEach(row => {
      const seat = row[0];
      const id = row[1];
      const name = row[2];
      const status = row[3];
      const updatedAt = row[4];
      if (!id) return;

      let currentStatus = '미입실';
      if (updatedAt) {
        const updatedStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(updatedAt), TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        if (updatedStr === todayStr && status === '입실') {
          currentStatus = '입실';
        }
      }

      results.push({ seat: seat, id: id, name: name, status: currentStatus });
    });

    return results;
  } catch (e) {
    return [];
  }
}

function checkStudentStatus(id, name) {
  try {
    const sheet = getCurrentDataSheet_();
    if (!sheet) return 'ERROR';

    const data = sheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 5).getValues();
    const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      if (String(row[1]) === String(id) && String(row[2]) === String(name)) {
        const lastUpdated = row[4];
        if (lastUpdated) {
          const lastStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(lastUpdated), TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
          if (lastStr === todayStr && String(row[3]) === '입실') {
            return '오늘입실완료';
          }
        }
        return '미입실';
      }
    }
    return 'NOT_FOUND';
  } catch (e) {
    return 'ERROR';
  }
}

function processJaturiAttendanceById_(id, status) {
  try {
    const normalizedId = String(id || '').trim();
    if (!/^\d{4}$/.test(normalizedId)) {
      return '❌ 학번 4자리를 정확히 입력하세요.';
    }

    const dataSheet = getCurrentDataSheet_();
    const jSheet = getCurrentJaturiSheet_();
    if (!dataSheet || !jSheet) return '❌ 현재 월 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.';

    const data = dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 5).getValues();

    const matches = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      if (String(row[1] || '').trim() === normalizedId) {
        matches.push({
          rowNumber: FIRST_DATA_ROW + i,
          seatNum: String(row[0] || '').trim(),
          id: String(row[1] || '').trim(),
          name: String(row[2] || '').trim(),
          currentStatus: String(row[3] || ''),
          lastUpdated: row[4]
        });
      }
    }

    if (matches.length === 0) {
      return '❌ 등록되지 않은 학번입니다.';
    }

    if (matches.length > 1) {
      return '❌ 동일한 학번이 2명 이상 등록되어 있습니다. 교사에게 문의하세요.';
    }

    const student = matches[0];
    if (!student.name) {
      return '❌ 해당 학번의 이름 정보가 비어 있습니다. 교사에게 문의하세요.';
    }

    const now = new Date();
    const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

    if (student.currentStatus === status && student.lastUpdated) {
      const lastStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(student.lastUpdated), TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      if (lastStr === todayStr) {
        return '⚠️ 이미 오늘 입실 처리가 완료되었습니다.';
      }
    }

    dataSheet.getRange(student.rowNumber, 4).setValue(status);
    dataSheet.getRange(student.rowNumber, 5).setValue(now);
    appendLog_(todayStr, student.id, student.name, status, now, student.seatNum);

    const timeStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, TZ, 'HH:mm');
    setTodayAttendanceOnJaturiRow_(jSheet, student.rowNumber, timeStr);
    setDailyScoreForDate_(todayStr, student.id, getScoreFromTime(timeStr, student.seatNum));
    recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRow_(jSheet, student.rowNumber);
    invalidateDashboardCache_();

    return '✅ ' + student.name + ' 학생 입실 완료!';
  } catch (e) {
    return '⚠️ 시스템 오류가 발생했습니다: ' + e.toString();
  }
}

function adminProcessAttendance(id, name, timeStr) {
  try {
    const dataSheet = getCurrentDataSheet_();
    const jSheet = getCurrentJaturiSheet_();
    if (!dataSheet || !jSheet) return '❌ 현재 월 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.';

    const data = dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 5).getValues();
    let foundRow = -1;
    let seatNum = '';

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      if (String(row[1]) === String(id) && String(row[2]) === String(name)) {
        foundRow = FIRST_DATA_ROW + i;
        seatNum = String(row[0] || '').trim();
        break;
      }
    }

    if (foundRow === -1) return '❌ 등록되지 않은 학생입니다.';
    if (!/^([0-1]?\d|2[0-3]):[0-5]\d$/.test(String(timeStr || ''))) return '❌ 시간 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.';

    const now = new Date();
    const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const parts = String(timeStr).split(':');
    const manualDate = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), now.getDate(), Number(parts[0]), Number(parts[1]), 0);

    dataSheet.getRange(foundRow, 4).setValue('입실');
    dataSheet.getRange(foundRow, 5).setValue(manualDate);
    appendLog_(todayStr, id, name, '입실', manualDate, seatNum);

    setTodayAttendanceOnJaturiRow_(jSheet, foundRow, timeStr);
    setDailyScoreForDate_(todayStr, id, getScoreFromTime(timeStr, seatNum));
    recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRow_(jSheet, foundRow);
    invalidateDashboardCache_();

    return '✅ ' + name + ' 학생 ' + timeStr + ' 수동 입실 완료!';
  } catch (e) {
    return '⚠️ 수동 입실 중 오류 발생: ' + e.toString();
  }
}

function cancelAttendance(id, name) {
  try {
    const dataSheet = getCurrentDataSheet_();
    const jSheet = getCurrentJaturiSheet_();
    if (!dataSheet || !jSheet) return '❌ 현재 월 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.';

    const data = dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 5).getValues();
    let foundRow = -1;

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      if (String(row[1]) === String(id) && String(row[2]) === String(name)) {
        foundRow = FIRST_DATA_ROW + i;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (foundRow === -1) return '❌ 해당 학생을 찾을 수 없습니다.';

    const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    dataSheet.getRange(foundRow, 4).setValue('미입실');
    dataSheet.getRange(foundRow, 5).clearContent();
    deleteLatestLog_(id, name);

    clearTodayAttendanceOnJaturiRow_(jSheet, foundRow);
    clearDailyScoreForDate_(todayStr, id);
    recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRow_(jSheet, foundRow);
    invalidateDashboardCache_();

    return '✅ ' + name + ' 학생의 출석이 취소되고 점수가 정상 반영되었습니다.';
  } catch (e) {
    return '⚠️ 취소 중 오류 발생: ' + e.toString();
  }
}



/** =========================
 *  통합 학생 입실 분기
 *  06:00~08:40 자투리 / 08:55~16:40 일과 중 학생 직접 출결 차단 / 17:01~21:30 야간
 *  일과 중 웅지실 출결은 학생 QR이 아니라 교사 화면에서만 처리합니다.
 *  GPS 확인과 동일 브라우저 1학생 제한은 기존 학생 로그인 흐름 그대로 유지합니다.
 *  ========================= */
function processAttendanceById(id, status, gpsPayload) {
  const normalizedId = normalizeAttendanceStudentId_(id);
  if (!/^\d{4}$/.test(normalizedId)) return '❌ 학번 4자리를 정확히 입력하세요.';
  const gpsCheck = verifyStudentQrGps_(gpsPayload);
  if (!gpsCheck.ok) return gpsCheck.message;
  const now = new Date();
  const minutes = now.getHours() * 60 + now.getMinutes();

  if (minutes >= 6 * 60 && minutes <= 8 * 60 + 40) {
    return processJaturiAttendanceById_(normalizedId, '입실');
  }

  if (minutes >= 8 * 60 + 55 && minutes <= 16 * 60 + 40) {
    return '❌ 일과 중 웅지실 출결은 학생이 직접 등록할 수 없습니다.<br>담당 교사가 웅지실 화면에서 처리합니다.';
  }

  if (minutes >= 17 * 60 + 1 && minutes <= 21 * 60 + 30) {
    return processNightAttendanceById_(normalizedId);
  }

  return '❌ 현재는 출석 등록 시간이 아닙니다.';
}


function verifyStudentQrGps_(payload) {
  const lat = Number(payload && payload.lat);
  const lng = Number(payload && payload.lng);
  if (!isFinite(lat) || !isFinite(lng)) {
    return { ok: false, message: '❌ 위치 확인 실패했습니다.<br>담당 선생님께 말씀드리세요.' };
  }
  const distance = getDistanceMeters_(lat, lng, STUDENT_QR_GPS_LAT, STUDENT_QR_GPS_LNG);
  if (distance > STUDENT_QR_GPS_RADIUS_M) {
    return { ok: false, message: '❌ 지정된 장소에서만 출석할 수 있습니다.<br>담당 선생님께 말씀드리세요.' };
  }
  return { ok: true, distance: distance };
}

function getDistanceMeters_(lat1, lng1, lat2, lng2) {
  const R = 6371000;
  const toRad = Math.PI / 180;
  const dLat = (lat2 - lat1) * toRad;
  const dLng = (lng2 - lng1) * toRad;
  const a = Math.sin(dLat / 2) * Math.sin(dLat / 2) +
    Math.cos(lat1 * toRad) * Math.cos(lat2 * toRad) *
    Math.sin(dLng / 2) * Math.sin(dLng / 2);
  return R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1 - a));
}

function normalizeAttendanceStudentId_(value) {
  return String(value == null ? '' : value)
    .replace(/[０-９]/g, function(ch) { return String(ch.charCodeAt(0) - 65248); })
    .replace(/[^0-9]/g, '')
    .trim();
}

/** =========================
 *  야간 자기주도학습 전용 설정
 *  ========================= */
const NIGHT_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME = '야간 출석부 생성';
const NIGHT_CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME = '야간 당월 출석부 수정';
const NIGHT_LOG_SHEET_NAME = '야간로그';
const NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS = 14;
const NIGHT_FIRST_TIME_COL = 4;
const NIGHT_DAY_LABELS = ['월', '화', '수', '목', '금'];
const NIGHT_TIME_LABELS = ['1타임', '2타임'];
const NIGHT_STATUS_PRESENT = '출석';
const NIGHT_STATUS_LATE = '지각';

function ensureNightCoreSheets_() {
  normalizeNightStudySheetNames_();
  ensureNightTemplateSheet_();
  ensureNightCurrentEditSheet_();
  ensureNightLogSheet_();
  syncNightCurrentEditSheetFromCurrentMonth_();
  refreshCurrentNightStudySheetFromSchedule_();
  cleanupNightSheets_();
  arrangeIntegratedSheets_();
}

function ensureNightTemplateSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME) || ss.insertSheet(NIGHT_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  setupNightRosterHeaders_(sheet);
  setupNightTemplateControls_(sheet);
}

function ensureNightCurrentEditSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME) || ss.insertSheet(NIGHT_CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
  setupNightRosterHeaders_(sheet);
  setupNightCurrentEditControls_(sheet);
}

function ensureNightLogSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_LOG_SHEET_NAME) || ss.insertSheet(NIGHT_LOG_SHEET_NAME);
  const headers = ['날짜', '월', '학번', '이름', '좌석', '타임', '상태', '시간', '처리구분'];
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
  sheet.hideSheet();
}

function cleanupNightSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const hiddenNames = [NIGHT_LOG_SHEET_NAME, LOG_SHEET_NAME, DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME, SETTINGS_SHEET_NAME];
  hiddenNames.forEach(name => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (sheet) sheet.hideSheet();
  });
  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    if (/^야간데이터\(\d{1,2}월\)$/.test(sheet.getName())) sheet.hideSheet();
  });
}

function setupNightRosterHeaders_(sheet) {
  const headers = [
    '좌석', '학번', '이름',
    '(월) 1타임', '(월) 2타임',
    '(화) 1타임', '(화) 2타임',
    '(수) 1타임', '(수) 2타임',
    '(목) 1타임', '(목) 2타임',
    '(금) 1타임', '(금) 2타임',
    '비고'
  ];
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
  sheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 1).setValues(getSeatList_().map(seat => [seat]));
}

function setupNightTemplateControls_(sheet) {
  sheet.getRange('P1').setValue('출석부 적용 월 선택');
  sheet.getRange('P2').setValue('출석부 완료, 출석부 생성');
  sheet.getRange('P3').setValue('출석부 생성 취소, 전체 초기화');

  const monthRule = SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()
    .requireValueInList(['1월', '2월', '3월', '4월', '5월', '6월', '7월', '8월', '9월', '10월', '11월', '12월'], true)
    .setAllowInvalid(false)
    .build();
  sheet.getRange('Q1').setDataValidation(monthRule);
  if (!sheet.getRange('Q1').getValue()) sheet.getRange('Q1').setValue(getCurrentMonthNumber_() + '월');
  sheet.getRange('Q2').insertCheckboxes();
  sheet.getRange('Q3').insertCheckboxes();
}

function createSelectedNightMonthSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const template = ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  const month = parseMonthValue_(template.getRange('Q1').getValue());
  if (!month) {
    ss.toast('Q1에서 월을 먼저 선택하세요.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }

  if (getNightDataSheet_(month) || getNightStudySheet_(month)) {
    ss.toast('이미 해당 월 야간 시트가 존재합니다.', '안내', 2);
    return;
  }

  createNightMonthSheetsFromSource_(month, NIGHT_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  ss.toast("'" + month + "월' 야간 출석부 생성이 완료되었습니다.", '완료', 2);
}

function deleteSelectedNightMonthSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const template = ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  const month = parseMonthValue_(template.getRange('Q1').getValue());
  if (!month) {
    ss.toast('Q1에서 월을 먼저 선택하세요.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }

  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const answer = ui.alert("'" + month + "월' 야간 출석부 생성을 취소하시겠습니까?", ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO);
  if (answer !== ui.Button.YES) return;

  const dataSheet = getNightDataSheet_(month);
  const studySheet = getNightStudySheet_(month);
  let deleted = false;
  if (dataSheet) { ss.deleteSheet(dataSheet); deleted = true; }
  if (studySheet) { ss.deleteSheet(studySheet); deleted = true; }

  ss.toast(deleted ? "'" + month + "월' 야간 출석부 생성이 취소되었습니다." : '삭제할 해당 월 야간 시트가 없습니다.', '안내', 2);
}

function createNightMonthSheetsFromSource_(month, sourceSheetName) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const source = ss.getSheetByName(sourceSheetName);
  if (!source) throw new Error(sourceSheetName + ' 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.');

  const dataSheet = ss.insertSheet(getNightDataSheetName_(month));
  source.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS)
    .copyTo(
      dataSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS),
      SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL,
      false
    );
  dataSheet.hideSheet();

  const studySheet = ss.insertSheet(getNightStudySheetName_(month));
  const base = dataSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3).getValues();
  studySheet.getRange(1, 1, base.length, 3).setValues(base);

  const dates = getWeekdayDatesForMonth_(month);
  const headers = [];
  dates.forEach(date => {
    const display = Utilities.formatDate(date, TZ, 'M/d') + '(' + ['일','월','화','수','목','금','토'][date.getDay()] + ')';
    headers.push(display + ' 1타임');
    headers.push(display + ' 2타임');
  });
  if (headers.length) studySheet.getRange(1, 4, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);

  refreshNightStudySheetFromSchedule_(month);
  formatNightStudySheet_(studySheet, month);
  invalidateDashboardCache_();
}

function formatNightStudySheet_(sheet, month) {
  if (!sheet) return;
  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 4);
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol)
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle')
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setWrapStrategy(SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.CLIP);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).setFontWeight('bold');
}

function getNightDataSheetName_(month) {
  return '야간데이터(' + month + '월)';
}

function getNightStudySheetName_(month) {
  return '야간 출석부(' + month + '월)';
}

function getNightDataSheet_(month) {
  return SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(getNightDataSheetName_(month));
}

function getNightStudySheet_(month) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const preferred = ss.getSheetByName(getNightStudySheetName_(month));
  if (preferred) return preferred;

  const legacy = ss.getSheetByName('야간자습(' + month + '월)');
  if (legacy) {
    const newName = getNightStudySheetName_(month);
    if (!ss.getSheetByName(newName)) {
      legacy.setName(newName);
      return legacy;
    }
    return legacy;
  }

  return null;
}

function getCurrentNightDataSheet_() {
  return getNightDataSheet_(getCurrentMonthNumber_());
}

function getCurrentNightStudySheet_() {
  return getNightStudySheet_(getCurrentMonthNumber_());
}

function classifyNightTime_(dateObj, requestedTime) {
  const d = dateObj || new Date();
  const minutes = d.getHours() * 60 + d.getMinutes();

  if (requestedTime) {
    const t = Number(requestedTime);
    return { timeNo: t, status: NIGHT_STATUS_PRESENT, ok: true };
  }

  if (minutes >= 18 * 60 + 10 && minutes <= 18 * 60 + 30) return { timeNo: 1, status: NIGHT_STATUS_PRESENT, ok: true };
  if (minutes >= 18 * 60 + 31 && minutes <= 20 * 60) return { timeNo: 1, status: NIGHT_STATUS_LATE, ok: true };
  if (minutes >= 20 * 60 + 10 && minutes <= 20 * 60 + 30) return { timeNo: 2, status: NIGHT_STATUS_PRESENT, ok: true };
  if (minutes >= 20 * 60 + 31 && minutes <= 21 * 60 + 45) return { timeNo: 2, status: NIGHT_STATUS_LATE, ok: true };

  if (minutes >= 20 * 60 + 1 && minutes <= 20 * 60 + 9) {
    return { ok: false, message: '❌ 2타임 출석 체크는 20:10부터 가능합니다.' };
  }

  return { ok: false, message: '❌ 야간 자기주도학습 출석 처리 시간이 아닙니다.' };
}

function processNightAttendanceById_(id) {
  const normalizedId = String(id || '').trim();
  if (!/^\d{4}$/.test(normalizedId)) return '❌ 학번 4자리를 정확히 입력하세요.';

  const now = new Date();
  const classified = classifyNightTime_(now);
  if (!classified.ok) return classified.message;

  const found = findNightStudentById_(normalizedId);
  if (!found) return '❌ 야간 출석부에 등록되지 않은 학번입니다.';

  return setNightAttendance_(found, classified.timeNo, classified.status, now, '학생QR');
}

function findNightStudentById_(id) {
  const sheet = getCurrentNightDataSheet_();
  if (!sheet) return null;
  const values = sheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS).getValues();
  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    const row = values[i];
    if (String(row[1] || '').trim() === String(id)) {
      return {
        rowIndex: FIRST_DATA_ROW + i,
        seat: String(row[0] || '').trim(),
        id: String(row[1] || '').trim(),
        name: String(row[2] || '').trim(),
        schedule: row.slice(3, 13),
        note: row[13]
      };
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function getNightScheduleCell_(student, dateObj, timeNo) {
  const day = dateObj.getDay();
  if (day < 1 || day > 5) return 'x';
  const dayIdx = day - 1;
  const relIdx = dayIdx * 2 + (Number(timeNo) - 1);
  return student.schedule[relIdx];
}

function getNightScheduleState_(cellValue) {
  if (cellValue instanceof Date) return { type: 'early', time: Utilities.formatDate(cellValue, TZ, 'HH:mm') };
  const text = String(cellValue == null ? '' : cellValue).trim();
  if (!text) return { type: 'scheduled' };
  if (text.toLowerCase() === 'x') return { type: 'off' };
  if (/^([01]?\d|2[0-3]):[0-5]\d$/.test(text)) return { type: 'early', time: normalizeNightTimeText_(text) };
  return { type: 'scheduled' };
}

function normalizeNightTimeText_(text) {
  const m = String(text || '').match(/([01]?\d|2[0-3]):([0-5]\d)/);
  if (!m) return '';
  return String(Number(m[1])).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + m[2];
}

function formatNightScheduleCellForStudy_(cellValue, displayValue) {
  const displayText = String(displayValue == null ? '' : displayValue).trim();
  const normalizedDisplayTime = normalizeNightTimeText_(displayText);
  if (normalizedDisplayTime) return normalizedDisplayTime;
  if (cellValue instanceof Date) return Utilities.formatDate(cellValue, TZ, 'HH:mm');
  return String(cellValue == null ? '' : cellValue).trim();
}

function extractNightTimeFromText_(text) {
  return normalizeNightTimeText_(text);
}

function parseNightDataHeader_(headerText, fallbackRelIndex) {
  const fallbackLabels = [
    { dayLabel: '월', timeNo: 1 }, { dayLabel: '월', timeNo: 2 },
    { dayLabel: '화', timeNo: 1 }, { dayLabel: '화', timeNo: 2 },
    { dayLabel: '수', timeNo: 1 }, { dayLabel: '수', timeNo: 2 },
    { dayLabel: '목', timeNo: 1 }, { dayLabel: '목', timeNo: 2 },
    { dayLabel: '금', timeNo: 1 }, { dayLabel: '금', timeNo: 2 }
  ];

  const text = String(headerText || '').trim();
  const dayMatch = text.match(/[월화수목금]/);
  const timeMatch = text.match(/([12])\s*타임|([12])\s*$/);

  if (dayMatch && timeMatch) {
    return {
      dayLabel: dayMatch[0],
      timeNo: Number(timeMatch[1] || timeMatch[2])
    };
  }

  return fallbackLabels[fallbackRelIndex] || null;
}

function buildNightDataScheduleIndexMap_(dataSheet) {
  const headers = dataSheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, NIGHT_FIRST_TIME_COL, 1, NIGHT_TIME_LABELS.length * NIGHT_DAY_LABELS.length).getDisplayValues()[0];
  const map = {};
  headers.forEach((header, relIdx) => {
    const parsed = parseNightDataHeader_(header, relIdx);
    if (!parsed) return;
    map[parsed.dayLabel + '_' + parsed.timeNo] = relIdx;
  });
  return map;
}


function setNightAttendance_(student, timeNo, status, dateObj, source) {
  const studySheet = getCurrentNightStudySheet_();
  if (!studySheet) return '❌ 현재 월 야간자습 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.';

  // 신청 여부와 관계없이 별도 초과 상태를 만들지 않습니다.
  // QR 출석 시각에 따라 이미 classifyNightTime_에서 출석/지각이 결정됩니다.
  const finalStatus = status;
  const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const timeStr = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, TZ, 'HH:mm');
  const col = getNightStudyColumnForDateTime_(studySheet, dateObj, timeNo);
  if (col === -1) return '❌ 해당 날짜의 야간자습 열을 찾지 못했습니다.';

  const range = studySheet.getRange(student.rowIndex, col);
  range.setValue(finalStatus);
  applyNightCellStyle_(range, finalStatus);
  appendNightLog_(dateKey, student.id, student.name, student.seat, timeNo, finalStatus, timeStr, source);
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  invalidateDashboardCache_();

  return '✅ ' + student.name + ' 학생 ' + timeNo + '타임 ' + finalStatus + ' 처리 완료';
}

function clearNightAttendance_(student, timeNo, dateObj, source) {
  const studySheet = getCurrentNightStudySheet_();
  if (!studySheet) return '❌ 현재 월 야간자습 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.';
  const col = getNightStudyColumnForDateTime_(studySheet, dateObj, timeNo);
  if (col === -1) return '❌ 해당 날짜의 야간자습 열을 찾지 못했습니다.';

  const range = studySheet.getRange(student.rowIndex, col);
  range.clearContent();

  const scheduleState = getNightScheduleState_(getNightScheduleCell_(student, dateObj, timeNo));
  if (scheduleState.type === 'off') {
    range.setValue('미신청');
    range.setBackground('#434343');
  } else {
    range.setBackground('#ea9999');
  }

  const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const timeStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, 'HH:mm');
  appendNightLog_(dateKey, student.id, student.name, student.seat, timeNo, '출석취소', timeStr, source || '교사수동');
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  invalidateDashboardCache_();
  return '✅ ' + student.name + ' 학생 ' + timeNo + '타임 출석 취소 완료';
}

function getNightStudyColumnForDateTime_(sheet, dateObj, timeNo) {
  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getDisplayValues()[0];
  const display = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, TZ, 'M/d') + '(' + ['일','월','화','수','목','금','토'][dateObj.getDay()] + ') ' + timeNo + '타임';
  const idx = headers.indexOf(display);
  return idx === -1 ? -1 : idx + 1;
}

function applyNightCellStyle_(range, status) {
  const color = status === NIGHT_STATUS_PRESENT ? '#ffd966'
    : status === NIGHT_STATUS_LATE ? '#b7b7b7'
    : '#ea9999';
  range.setBackground(color);
}

function appendNightLog_(dateStr, id, name, seat, timeNo, status, timeStr, source) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_LOG_SHEET_NAME) || ss.insertSheet(NIGHT_LOG_SHEET_NAME);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() === 0) sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 9).setValues([['날짜', '월', '학번', '이름', '좌석', '타임', '상태', '시간', '처리구분']]);
  appendRowWithScriptLock_(sheet, [dateStr, Number(dateStr.slice(5, 7)), id, name, seat, timeNo + '타임', status, timeStr, source || ''], 12000);
  try { sheet.hideSheet(); } catch (_) {}
}

function adminProcessNightAttendance(id, name, timeNos) {
  const student = findNightStudentById_(id);
  if (!student) return '❌ 야간 출석부에서 학생을 찾지 못했습니다.';
  const times = (timeNos || []).map(Number).filter(v => v === 1 || v === 2);
  if (!times.length) return '❌ 타임을 선택해 주세요.';

  const now = new Date();
  const results = times.map(t => setNightAttendance_(student, t, NIGHT_STATUS_PRESENT, now, '교사수동'));
  return results.join('\n');
}

function cancelNightAttendance(id, name, timeNos) {
  const student = findNightStudentById_(id);
  if (!student) return '❌ 야간 출석부에서 학생을 찾지 못했습니다.';
  const times = (timeNos || []).map(Number).filter(v => v === 1 || v === 2);
  if (!times.length) return '❌ 타임을 선택해 주세요.';

  const now = new Date();
  const results = times.map(t => clearNightAttendance_(student, t, now, '교사수동'));
  return results.join('\n');
}

function updateNightAttendanceState(id, name, t1State, t2State) {
  const student = findNightStudentById_(id);
  if (!student) return '❌ 야간 출석부에서 학생을 찾지 못했습니다.';

  const now = new Date();
  const studySheet = getCurrentNightStudySheet_();
  if (!studySheet) return '❌ 현재 월 야간자습 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.';

  const requests = [
    { timeNo: 1, state: String(t1State || '').trim() },
    { timeNo: 2, state: String(t2State || '').trim() }
  ];

  const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(now, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const timeStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, TZ, 'HH:mm');
  const messages = [];

  requests.forEach(req => {
    if (req.state !== 'present' && req.state !== 'absent') return;

    const col = getNightStudyColumnForDateTime_(studySheet, now, req.timeNo);
    if (col === -1) {
      messages.push(req.timeNo + '타임 열 없음');
      return;
    }

    const range = studySheet.getRange(student.rowIndex, col);

    if (req.state === 'present') {
      // 교사가 팝업에서 '출석'으로 직접 수정한 경우에는 시간대와 신청 여부와 관계없이 노란색 '출석'으로 처리합니다.
      const finalStatus = NIGHT_STATUS_PRESENT;
      range.setValue(finalStatus);
      applyNightCellStyle_(range, finalStatus);
      appendNightLog_(dateKey, student.id, student.name, student.seat, req.timeNo, finalStatus, timeStr, '교사수정');
      messages.push(req.timeNo + '타임 출석');
    } else {
      range.clearContent();
      const scheduleState = getNightScheduleState_(getNightScheduleCell_(student, now, req.timeNo));
      if (scheduleState.type === 'off') {
        range.setValue('미신청');
        range.setBackground('#434343');
      } else {
        range.setBackground('#ea9999');
      }
      appendNightLog_(dateKey, student.id, student.name, student.seat, req.timeNo, '미출석', timeStr, '교사수정');
      messages.push(req.timeNo + '타임 미출석');
    }
  });

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  invalidateDashboardCache_();

  return '✅ ' + student.name + ' 학생 출석 상황 변경 완료: ' + messages.join(', ');
}


function getNightStudyDisplayMatrixForDate_(studySheet, dateObj) {
  const lastCol = studySheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastCol < 4) return { rows: [], t1ColIndex: -1, t2ColIndex: -1 };

  const headers = studySheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getDisplayValues()[0];
  const display = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, TZ, 'M/d') + '(' + ['일','월','화','수','목','금','토'][dateObj.getDay()] + ')';
  const t1AbsCol = headers.indexOf(display + ' 1타임');
  const t2AbsCol = headers.indexOf(display + ' 2타임');
  const bodyCols = lastCol - 3;
  const rows = studySheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 4, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, bodyCols).getDisplayValues();

  return {
    rows: rows,
    t1ColIndex: t1AbsCol === -1 ? -1 : t1AbsCol - 3,
    t2ColIndex: t2AbsCol === -1 ? -1 : t2AbsCol - 3
  };
}

function getNightScheduleValueFromRow_(row, scheduleIndexMap, dateObj, timeNo) {
  const dayLabel = ['일','월','화','수','목','금','토'][dateObj.getDay()];
  const relIdx = scheduleIndexMap[dayLabel + '_' + Number(timeNo)];
  if (relIdx == null) return '';
  return row[NIGHT_FIRST_TIME_COL - 1 + relIdx];
}

function getNightTimeDisplayStateFromValues_(scheduleValue, studyValue) {
  const scheduleState = getNightScheduleState_(scheduleValue);
  const scheduledTime = scheduleState.type === 'early' ? scheduleState.time : '';
  const value = String(studyValue || '').trim();

  // 웹앱 좌석 이름 아래에는 출석 처리 시각을 표시하지 않습니다.
  // 야간데이터에 미리 입력된 조퇴/하원 시간만 표시합니다.
  if (value.indexOf(NIGHT_STATUS_LATE) !== -1) return { state: 'late', text: '지각', time: scheduledTime };
  if (value.indexOf(NIGHT_STATUS_PRESENT) !== -1) return { state: 'present', text: '출석', time: scheduledTime };

  if (scheduleState.type === 'off') return { state: 'off', text: '미신청', time: '' };
  return { state: 'absent', text: '미출석', time: scheduledTime };
}

function getNightStatus() {
  const dataSheet = getCurrentNightDataSheet_();
  const studySheet = getCurrentNightStudySheet_();
  if (!dataSheet || !studySheet) return [];

  const today = new Date();
  const dataValues = dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS).getValues();
  const scheduleIndexMap = buildNightDataScheduleIndexMap_(dataSheet);
  const studyValues = getNightStudyDisplayMatrixForDate_(studySheet, today);

  return dataValues.map((row, idx) => {
    const seat = String(row[0] || '').trim();
    const id = String(row[1] || '').trim();
    const name = String(row[2] || '').trim();
    if (!id) return null;

    const t1Schedule = getNightScheduleValueFromRow_(row, scheduleIndexMap, today, 1);
    const t2Schedule = getNightScheduleValueFromRow_(row, scheduleIndexMap, today, 2);
    const t1Value = studyValues.t1ColIndex === -1 ? '' : String((studyValues.rows[idx] || [])[studyValues.t1ColIndex] || '').trim();
    const t2Value = studyValues.t2ColIndex === -1 ? '' : String((studyValues.rows[idx] || [])[studyValues.t2ColIndex] || '').trim();

    return {
      seat, id, name,
      t1: getNightTimeDisplayStateFromValues_(t1Schedule, t1Value),
      t2: getNightTimeDisplayStateFromValues_(t2Schedule, t2Value)
    };
  }).filter(Boolean);
}

function getNightTimeDisplayState_(studySheet, student, dateObj, timeNo) {
  const scheduleValue = getNightScheduleCell_(student, dateObj, timeNo);
  const col = getNightStudyColumnForDateTime_(studySheet, dateObj, timeNo);
  const value = col === -1 ? '' : String(studySheet.getRange(student.rowIndex, col).getDisplayValue() || '').trim();
  return getNightTimeDisplayStateFromValues_(scheduleValue, value);
}

function getNightAbsenceStatus() {
  const today = new Date();
  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

  // 감독표 E열(3학년)에 실제 감독교사가 있는 날만 야간자율학습 미출결을 계산합니다.
  // 3학년 감독교사가 없거나 회색/행사/공휴일이면 미출결 인원은 없는 것으로 봅니다.
  try {
    const supervisorSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(NIGHT_SUPERVISOR_SPREADSHEET_ID);
    if (!isNightStudyDateBySupervisor_(supervisorSs, new Date(today), {})) return [];
  } catch (e) {
    // 감독표 확인에 실패하면 기존 출석부 기준으로 계산합니다.
  }

  const statusRows = getNightStatus();
  if (!statusRows || !statusRows.length) return [];

  const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(today, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const dateLabel = Utilities.formatDate(today, TZ, 'MM/dd') + '(' + ['일','월','화','수','목','금','토'][today.getDay()] + ')';

  const results = [];

  statusRows.forEach(student => {
    const seat = String(student.seat || '').trim();
    const id = String(student.id || '').trim();
    const name = String(student.name || '').trim();
    if (!id) return;

    const missingTimes = [];
    const t1State = student.t1 && student.t1.state ? String(student.t1.state).trim() : '';
    const t2State = student.t2 && student.t2.state ? String(student.t2.state).trim() : '';

    if (t1State === 'absent') missingTimes.push(1);
    if (t2State === 'absent') missingTimes.push(2);

    if (!missingTimes.length) return;

    const timeText = missingTimes.length === 1
      ? missingTimes[0] + '타임'
      : missingTimes.join(', ') + '타임';

    results.push({
      seat,
      id,
      name,
      dateKey,
      dateTime: dateLabel + ' ' + timeText
    });
  });

  results.sort((a, b) => {
    const idCompare = String(a.id).localeCompare(String(b.id), 'ko', { numeric: true });
    if (idCompare !== 0) return idCompare;
    return String(a.dateTime).localeCompare(String(b.dateTime), 'ko', { numeric: true });
  });

  return results;
}



function buildNightLogStatusMapForDate_(dateKey) {
  const map = {};
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(NIGHT_LOG_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return map;

  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
  values.forEach(row => {
    const rawDate = row[0];
    const logDate = rawDate instanceof Date ? Utilities.formatDate(rawDate, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd') : normalizeDateKey_(rawDate);
    if (logDate !== dateKey) return;

    const id = String(row[2] || '').trim();
    const timeText = String(row[5] || '').trim();
    const statusText = String(row[6] || '').trim();
    if (!id) return;

    const timeMatch = timeText.match(/([12])\s*타임/);
    if (!timeMatch) return;
    const timeNo = Number(timeMatch[1]);

    let normalized = '';
    if (statusText.indexOf('출석취소') !== -1 || statusText.indexOf('미출석') !== -1 || statusText.indexOf('결석') !== -1) {
      normalized = 'absent';
    } else if (statusText.indexOf('출석') !== -1 || statusText.indexOf('지각') !== -1) {
      normalized = 'present';
    } else {
      return;
    }

    // 야간로그는 아래 행이 최신이므로 순서대로 덮어써서 최종 상태만 남깁니다.
    map[id + '_' + timeNo] = {
      status: normalized,
      rawStatus: statusText
    };
  });

  return map;
}


function getNightAbsenceStatusForDate_(targetDate) {
  try {
    const month = targetDate.getMonth() + 1;
    const dataSheet = getNightDataSheet_(month);
    const studySheet = getNightStudySheet_(month);
    if (!dataSheet || !studySheet) return null;

    const studyValues = getNightStudyDisplayMatrixForDate_(studySheet, targetDate);
    if (studyValues.t1ColIndex === -1 && studyValues.t2ColIndex === -1) return null;

    const dataValues = dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS).getValues();
    const scheduleIndexMap = buildNightDataScheduleIndexMap_(dataSheet);
    const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(targetDate, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const dateLabel = Utilities.formatDate(targetDate, TZ, 'MM/dd') + '(' + ['일','월','화','수','목','금','토'][targetDate.getDay()] + ')';
    const logStatusMap = buildNightLogStatusMapForDate_(dateKey);

    const results = [];
    let hasOperationTarget = false;

    dataValues.forEach((row, idx) => {
      const seat = String(row[0] || '').trim();
      const id = String(row[1] || '').trim();
      const name = String(row[2] || '').trim();
      if (!id) return;

      const missingTimes = [];

      [1, 2].forEach(timeNo => {
        const scheduleValue = getNightScheduleValueFromRow_(row, scheduleIndexMap, targetDate, timeNo);
        const scheduleState = getNightScheduleState_(scheduleValue);
        if (scheduleState.type === 'off') return;

        const colIndex = timeNo === 1 ? studyValues.t1ColIndex : studyValues.t2ColIndex;
        if (colIndex === -1) return;

        hasOperationTarget = true;
        const logState = logStatusMap[id + '_' + timeNo];

        // 야간로그에 해당 날짜·학생·타임 최종 기록이 있으면 로그를 우선합니다.
        // 과거 onOpen 재정리 문제로 출석부 셀이 지워진 날도 로그의 마지막 상태가 출석/지각이면 미출결에서 제외됩니다.
        if (logState && logState.status === 'present') return;
        if (logState && logState.status === 'absent') {
          missingTimes.push(timeNo);
          return;
        }

        // 로그가 없을 때만 야간 출석부 셀 값을 보조 기준으로 사용합니다.
        const studyValue = String((studyValues.rows[idx] || [])[colIndex] || '').trim();
        const displayState = getNightTimeDisplayStateFromValues_(scheduleValue, studyValue);
        if (displayState.state === 'absent') missingTimes.push(timeNo);
      });

      if (!missingTimes.length) return;

      const timeText = missingTimes.length === 1
        ? missingTimes[0] + '타임'
        : missingTimes.join(', ') + '타임';

      results.push({
        seat,
        id,
        name,
        dateKey,
        dateLabel,
        dateTime: dateLabel + ' ' + timeText
      });
    });

    return {
      isOperatingDate: hasOperationTarget,
      dateKey,
      dateLabel,
      rows: results.sort((a, b) => {
        const idCompare = String(a.id).localeCompare(String(b.id), 'ko', { numeric: true });
        if (idCompare !== 0) return idCompare;
        return String(a.seat).localeCompare(String(b.seat), 'ko', { numeric: true });
      })
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return null;
  }
}


function getPreviousNightAbsenceStatus() {
  try {
    const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    const now = new Date();
    const todayKey = Utilities.formatDate(now, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const minutes = now.getHours() * 60 + now.getMinutes();
    const phaseKey = minutes >= (20 * 60 + 1) ? 'after2001' : 'before2001';

    // v9: 로그인 화면도 야간자습 미출결 현황과 같은 기준을 사용합니다.
    // 20:01 전에는 직전 3학년 야간자율학습 시행일, 20:01부터는 오늘이 시행일이면 오늘 데이터입니다.
    // 오늘 3학년 감독교사가 없으면 20:01 이후에도 직전 시행일을 유지합니다.
    // 미출결 계산은 야간로그 최종 기록을 우선합니다.
    const cacheKey = 'previous_night_absence_v9_' + todayKey + '_' + phaseKey;
    const cached = cache.get(cacheKey);
    if (cached) {
      try { return JSON.parse(cached); } catch (e) {}
    }

    const targetDate = getPreviousNightStudyDateFromSupervisor_();
    if (targetDate) {
      const payload = getNightAbsenceStatusForDate_(new Date(targetDate));
      const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(targetDate, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      const dateLabel = Utilities.formatDate(targetDate, TZ, 'MM/dd') + '(' + ['일','월','화','수','목','금','토'][targetDate.getDay()] + ')';
      const result = {
        ok: true,
        dateKey: payload ? payload.dateKey : dateKey,
        dateLabel: payload ? payload.dateLabel : dateLabel,
        rows: payload ? (payload.rows || []) : [],
        message: payload ? '' : '해당 날짜의 야간 출석부 데이터를 찾지 못했습니다.'
      };
      try { cache.put(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(result), 120); } catch (e) {}
      return result;
    }

    const result = {
      ok: true,
      dateKey: '',
      dateLabel: '',
      rows: [],
      message: '감독표에서 표시할 3학년 야간자율학습 시행일을 찾지 못했습니다.'
    };
    try { cache.put(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(result), 120); } catch (e) {}
    return result;
  } catch (e) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      dateKey: '',
      dateLabel: '',
      rows: [],
      message: '미출결 현황을 불러오는 중 오류가 발생했습니다: ' + e.message
    };
  }
}


function getPreviousNightStudyDateFromSupervisor_() {
  const today = new Date();
  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

  let ss;
  try {
    ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(NIGHT_SUPERVISOR_SPREADSHEET_ID);
  } catch (e) {
    return null;
  }

  const monthCache = {};
  const now = new Date();
  const minutes = now.getHours() * 60 + now.getMinutes();

  // 20:01부터는 오늘이 3학년 야간자율학습 시행일이면 오늘 데이터를 보여줍니다.
  // 오늘이 시행일이 아니면 계속 직전 시행일을 보여줍니다.
  if (minutes >= 20 * 60 + 1 && isNightStudyDateBySupervisor_(ss, new Date(today), monthCache)) {
    return new Date(today);
  }

  const cursor = new Date(today);
  cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() - 1);

  for (let i = 0; i < 90; i++) {
    const day = cursor.getDay();
    if (day !== 0 && day !== 6) {
      if (isNightStudyDateBySupervisor_(ss, new Date(cursor), monthCache)) {
        return new Date(cursor);
      }
    }
    cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() - 1);
  }

  return null;
}

function isNightStudyDateBySupervisor_(ss, targetDate, monthCache) {
  const month = targetDate.getMonth() + 1;
  if (!monthCache[month]) {
    const sheet = getSupervisorMonthSheet_(ss, month);
    if (!sheet) {
      monthCache[month] = { rows: [] };
    } else {
      const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
      if (lastRow < 1) {
        monthCache[month] = { rows: [] };
      } else {
        const range = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, 5);
        monthCache[month] = {
          values: range.getValues(),
          displays: range.getDisplayValues(),
          backgrounds: range.getBackgrounds()
        };
      }
    }
  }

  const cached = monthCache[month];
  const values = cached.values || [];
  const displays = cached.displays || [];
  const backgrounds = cached.backgrounds || [];
  const targetKey = Utilities.formatDate(targetDate, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

  for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) {
    const dateObj = parseSupervisorDate_(values[r][0], displays[r][0], targetDate.getFullYear(), targetDate.getMonth());
    if (!dateObj) continue;

    const rowKey = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    if (rowKey !== targetKey) continue;

    const grade3Raw = String((displays[r] || [])[4] || '').trim();
    const grade3Bg = String(((backgrounds[r] || [])[4]) || '').toLowerCase();

    // 3학년 칸이 회색이면 운영 없음, 비어 있거나 행사명/시험명 등이면 운영 없음.
    return !isSupervisorGray_(grade3Bg) && isTeacherNameLike_(grade3Raw);
  }

  return false;
}

function getRecentWeekdayDatesExcludeToday_(count) {
  const dates = [];
  const cursor = new Date();
  cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() - 1);
  cursor.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  while (dates.length < count) {
    const day = cursor.getDay();
    if (day !== 0 && day !== 6) dates.push(new Date(cursor));
    cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() - 1);
  }
  return dates.reverse();
}

function getCumulativeStatus() {
  ensureDailyScoreSheet_();
  if (isDailyScoreSheetEmpty_()) rebuildDailyScoresFromJaturiSheets_();

  const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
  const cached = cache.get(DASHBOARD_CACHE_KEY);
  if (cached) {
    try {
      return JSON.parse(cached);
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  const baseSheet = getCurrentJaturiSheet_() || getCurrentDataSheet_() || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!baseSheet) return { dates: [], records: [] };

  const targetDates = getRecentWeekdayDates_(3);
  const dateKeys = targetDates.map(d => Utilities.formatDate(d, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd'));
  const students = baseSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 3).getValues();
  const currentMonth = getCurrentMonthNumber_();

  const ids = students.map(r => normalizeString_(r[1])).filter(Boolean);
  const idVariantsMap = getIdVariantsMapForIds_(ids);
  const dailySummary = buildDailyScoreSummary_(dateKeys, currentMonth);
  const pastTotals = buildPastTotalsById_(currentMonth);

  const monthInfoMap = {};
  targetDates.forEach(date => {
    const month = date.getMonth() + 1;
    const sheetName = getJaturiSheetName_(month);
    if (!monthInfoMap[sheetName]) {
      const sheet = getSheetByMonth_('자투리', month);
      monthInfoMap[sheetName] = sheet ? buildJaturiSheetInfo_(sheet) : null;
    }
  });

  const records = students.map(row => {
    const seat = row[0];
    const id = normalizeString_(row[1]);
    const name = row[2];
    if (!id) return null;

    const variants = idVariantsMap[id] || [id];
    const attendance = {};
    let sixDayScore = 0;

    targetDates.forEach(date => {
      const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(date, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      const info = monthInfoMap[getJaturiSheetName_(date.getMonth() + 1)];
      attendance[dateKey] = info ? getAttendanceTimeByIdVariants_(info, variants, dateKey) : '-';
      sixDayScore += sumByVariants_(dailySummary.byDate[dateKey], variants);
    });

    const totalScore = sumByVariants_(pastTotals, variants) + sumByVariants_(dailySummary.byMonth, variants);

    return {
      seat: seat,
      rawId: id,
      rawName: name,
      attendance: attendance,
      totalScore: totalScore,
      sixDayScore: sixDayScore,
      isSpecial: SPECIAL_SEATS.indexOf(String(seat).trim()) !== -1
    };
  }).filter(Boolean);

  const result = {
    dates: targetDates.map(d => ({
      full: Utilities.formatDate(d, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd'),
      display: (d.getMonth() + 1) + '/' + d.getDate() + '(' + ['일', '월', '화', '수', '목', '금', '토'][d.getDay()] + ')'
    })),
    records: records
  };

  try { cache.put(DASHBOARD_CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify(result), 20); } catch (e) {}
  return result;
}

function recalculateAllScores() {
  ensureDailyScoreSheet_();
  rebuildDailyScoresFromJaturiSheets_();
  recalcCurrentMonthTotalsFromDailyScore_();
  invalidateDashboardCache_();
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('✅ 현재월 총점 재계산이 완료되었습니다.');
}

function ensureCoreSheets_() {
  normalizeLegacySheets_();
  ensureTemplateSheet_();
  ensureCurrentEditSheet_();
  ensureDailyScoreSheet_();
  cleanupExistingSheetStructures_();
  runOneTimeCurrentMonthTemplateMigration_();
  syncCurrentEditSheetFromCurrentMonth_();
}

function normalizeLegacySheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const currentMonth = getCurrentMonthNumber_();

  const renamePairs = [
    ['출석부 생성', TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME],
    ['당월 출석부 수정', CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME],
    ['로그', LOG_SHEET_NAME],
    ['시스템_일별점수', DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME],
    ['설정', SETTINGS_SHEET_NAME]
  ];

  renamePairs.forEach(pair => {
    const oldSheet = ss.getSheetByName(pair[0]);
    const newSheet = ss.getSheetByName(pair[1]);
    if (oldSheet && !newSheet) oldSheet.setName(pair[1]);
  });

  const oldData = ss.getSheetByName('데이터');
  const currentDataName = getDataSheetName_(currentMonth);
  if (oldData && !ss.getSheetByName(currentDataName)) oldData.setName(currentDataName);

  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const name = sheet.getName();

    let match = name.match(/^데이터\((\d{1,2})월\)$/);
    if (match) {
      const newName = getDataSheetName_(Number(match[1]));
      if (!ss.getSheetByName(newName)) sheet.setName(newName);
      return;
    }

    match = name.match(/^자투리(\d{1,2})월$/);
    if (match) {
      const newName = getJaturiSheetName_(Number(match[1]));
      if (!ss.getSheetByName(newName)) sheet.setName(newName);
      return;
    }

    if (name === '원본' && !ss.getSheetByName(TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME)) {
      sheet.setName(TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
    }
  });
}


function runOneTimeCurrentMonthTemplateMigration_() {
  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  if (props.getProperty('CURRENT_MONTH_TEMPLATE_MIGRATED') === 'true') return;

  const template = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  const dataSheet = getCurrentDataSheet_();
  const jSheet = getCurrentJaturiSheet_();
  if (!template || !dataSheet || !jSheet) {
    props.setProperty('CURRENT_MONTH_TEMPLATE_MIGRATED', 'true');
    return;
  }

  template.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3)
    .copyTo(dataSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);
  template.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3)
    .copyTo(jSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);
  dataSheet.hideSheet();
  props.setProperty('CURRENT_MONTH_TEMPLATE_MIGRATED', 'true');
}

function ensureTemplateSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME) || ss.insertSheet(TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  setupRosterHeadersAndSeats_(sheet);
  setupTemplateControls_(sheet);
}

function ensureCurrentEditSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME) || ss.insertSheet(CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
  setupRosterHeadersAndSeats_(sheet);
  setupCurrentEditControls_(sheet);
}

function ensureDailyScoreSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME) || ss.insertSheet(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() === 0 || sheet.getRange('A1').getValue() !== '날짜') {
    sheet.clear();
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['날짜', '월', '학번', '점수']]);
  }
  sheet.hideSheet();
}

function cleanupExistingSheetStructures_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const name = sheet.getName();
    if (/^(자투리 )?데이터\(\d{1,2}월\)$/.test(name)) {
      normalizeDataSheetStructure_(sheet);
      sheet.hideSheet();
    }
    if (/^자투리\(\d{1,2}월\)$/.test(name)) {
      normalizeJaturiSheetStructure_(sheet);
    }
    if (name === LOG_SHEET_NAME) {
      normalizeLogSheetStructure_(sheet);
    }
  });
}

function normalizeDataSheetStructure_(sheet) {
  sheet.getRange('D1').setValue('상태');
  sheet.getRange('E1').setValue('최종업데이트');
  while (sheet.getLastColumn() > 5) sheet.deleteColumn(6);
}

function normalizeJaturiSheetStructure_(sheet) {
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastCol < 4) return;
  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0];
  if (headers.indexOf('총점') === -1) sheet.getRange(1, lastCol + 1).setValue('총점');
}

function normalizeLogSheetStructure_(sheet) {
  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 5)).getValues()[0];
  const baseHeaders = ['날짜', '학번', '이름', '상태', '시간'];
  if (headers.slice(0, 5).join('|') !== baseHeaders.join('|')) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([baseHeaders]);
  }
  if (sheet.getLastColumn() > 5) {
    // keep extra columns untouched to avoid user data loss
  }
}

function setupRosterHeadersAndSeats_(sheet) {
  sheet.getRange('A1').setValue('좌석');
  sheet.getRange('B1').setValue('학번');
  sheet.getRange('C1').setValue('이름');
  sheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 1).setValues(getSeatList_().map(seat => [seat]));
}

function setupTemplateControls_(sheet) {
  sheet.getRange('F1').setValue('출석부 적용 월 선택');
  sheet.getRange('F2').setValue('출석부 완료, 출석부 생성');
  sheet.getRange('F3').setValue('출석부 생성 취소, 전체 초기화');

  const monthRule = SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()
    .requireValueInList(['1월', '2월', '3월', '4월', '5월', '6월', '7월', '8월', '9월', '10월', '11월', '12월'], true)
    .setAllowInvalid(false)
    .build();
  sheet.getRange('G1').setDataValidation(monthRule);
  if (!sheet.getRange('G1').getValue()) sheet.getRange('G1').setValue(getCurrentMonthNumber_() + '월');
  sheet.getRange('G2').insertCheckboxes();
  sheet.getRange('G3').insertCheckboxes();
}

function setupCurrentEditControls_(sheet) {
  sheet.getRange('F1').setValue('이동할 학생 학번');
  sheet.getRange('F2').setValue('새 좌석');
  sheet.getRange('F3').setValue('좌석 이동 실행');
  sheet.getRange('F5').setValue('좌석 이동은 G1~G3 사용');
  sheet.getRange('F6').setValue('학번 정정은 이름을 먼저 동일하게 맞춘 뒤 학번 수정');

  const seatRule = SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()
    .requireValueInList(getSeatList_(), true)
    .setAllowInvalid(false)
    .build();
  sheet.getRange('G2').setDataValidation(seatRule);
  sheet.getRange('G3').insertCheckboxes();
}

function syncCurrentEditSheetFromCurrentMonth_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const currentEdit = ss.getSheetByName(CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!currentEdit) return;

  const source = getCurrentDataSheet_() || ss.getSheetByName(TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!source) return;

  source.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3)
    .copyTo(currentEdit.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);
  normalizeCurrentEditSeats_(currentEdit);
  setupCurrentEditControls_(currentEdit);
}

function syncCurrentEditChangesToCurrentMonth_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const editSheet = ss.getSheetByName(CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!editSheet) return;

  normalizeCurrentEditSeats_(editSheet);
  const newRoster = editSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 3).getValues();
  const duplicateIds = getDuplicateIdsFromRoster_(newRoster);
  if (duplicateIds.length > 0) {
    ss.toast('중복 학번이 있어 적용하지 않았습니다: ' + duplicateIds.join(', '), '중복 학번', 5);
    syncCurrentEditSheetFromCurrentMonth_();
    return;
  }

  let dataSheet = getCurrentDataSheet_();
  let jSheet = getCurrentJaturiSheet_();
  if (!dataSheet || !jSheet) {
    createMonthSheetsFromSource_(getCurrentMonthNumber_(), CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
    dataSheet = getCurrentDataSheet_();
    jSheet = getCurrentJaturiSheet_();
  }

  const oldRoster = dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 3).getValues();
  const movedIds = getMovedIdsBetweenRosters_(oldRoster, newRoster);
  if (movedIds.length > 0) {
    ss.toast('좌석 이동은 G1~G3로만 처리하세요. 수동 행 이동은 적용하지 않았습니다.', '좌석 이동 제한', 5);
    syncCurrentEditSheetFromCurrentMonth_();
    return;
  }

  for (let i = 0; i < ROSTER_ROW_COUNT; i++) {
    const rowNum = FIRST_DATA_ROW + i;
    const oldRow = oldRoster[i];
    const newRow = newRoster[i];

    const oldId = normalizeString_(oldRow[1]);
    const oldName = normalizeString_(oldRow[2]);
    const newId = normalizeString_(newRow[1]);
    const newName = normalizeString_(newRow[2]);

    if (!oldId && !newId) {
      clearCurrentMonthOperationalCells_(dataSheet, jSheet, rowNum, false);
      continue;
    }

    if (oldId && !newId) {
      clearCurrentMonthDailyScoresById_(oldId);
      clearCurrentMonthOperationalCells_(dataSheet, jSheet, rowNum, false);
      continue;
    }

    if (!oldId && newId) {
      clearCurrentMonthOperationalCells_(dataSheet, jSheet, rowNum, false);
      continue;
    }

    if (oldId === newId) {
      if (oldName !== newName) replaceLogNameById_(oldId, newName);
      continue;
    }

    if (oldName && newName && oldName === newName) {
      registerIdAlias_(oldId, newId);
      moveCurrentMonthDailyScoresToNewId_(oldId, newId);
      replaceLogIdentity_(oldId, oldName, newId, newName);
      continue;
    }

    clearCurrentMonthDailyScoresById_(oldId);
    clearCurrentMonthOperationalCells_(dataSheet, jSheet, rowNum, false);
  }

  editSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3)
    .copyTo(dataSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);
  editSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3)
    .copyTo(jSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);

  for (let i = 0; i < ROSTER_ROW_COUNT; i++) {
    const rowNum = FIRST_DATA_ROW + i;
    const id = normalizeString_(jSheet.getRange(rowNum, 2).getValue());
    if (!id) clearCurrentMonthOperationalCells_(dataSheet, jSheet, rowNum, true);
    recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRow_(jSheet, rowNum);
  }

  dataSheet.hideSheet();
  invalidateDashboardCache_();
}

function createSelectedMonthSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const template = ss.getSheetByName(TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  const month = parseMonthValue_(template.getRange('G1').getValue());
  if (!month) {
    ss.toast('G1에서 월을 먼저 선택하세요.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }

  if (getSheetByMonth_('데이터', month) || getSheetByMonth_('자투리', month)) {
    ss.toast('이미 해당 월 시트가 존재합니다.', '안내', 2);
    return;
  }

  createMonthSheetsFromSource_(month, TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  ss.toast("'" + month + "월' 출석부 생성이 완료되었습니다.", '완료', 2);
}

function deleteSelectedMonthSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const template = ss.getSheetByName(TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  const month = parseMonthValue_(template.getRange('G1').getValue());
  if (!month) {
    ss.toast('G1에서 월을 먼저 선택하세요.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }

  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const answer = ui.alert("'" + month + "월' 출석부 생성을 취소하시겠습니까?", ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO);
  if (answer !== ui.Button.YES) return;

  const deleted = deleteMonthSheets_(month);
  if (deleted) {
    rebuildDailyScoresFromJaturiSheets_();
    recalcCurrentMonthTotalsFromDailyScore_();
    invalidateDashboardCache_();
    ss.toast("'" + month + "월' 출석부 생성이 취소되었습니다.", '완료', 2);
  } else {
    ss.toast('삭제할 해당 월 시트가 없습니다.', '안내', 2);
  }
}

function createMonthSheetsFromSource_(month, sourceSheetName) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const source = ss.getSheetByName(sourceSheetName);
  if (!source) throw new Error(sourceSheetName + ' 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.');
  if (getSheetByMonth_('데이터', month) || getSheetByMonth_('자투리', month)) {
    throw new Error('이미 해당 월 시트가 존재합니다.');
  }

  const dataSheet = ss.insertSheet(getDataSheetName_(month));
  source.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3)
    .copyTo(dataSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);
  dataSheet.getRange('D1').setValue('상태');
  dataSheet.getRange('E1').setValue('최종업데이트');
  dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 4, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 2).clearContent();
  normalizeDataSheetStructure_(dataSheet);
  dataSheet.hideSheet();

  const jSheet = ss.insertSheet(getJaturiSheetName_(month));
  source.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3)
    .copyTo(jSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);

  const weekdays = getWeekdayDatesForMonth_(month);
  const headers = weekdays.slice();
  headers.push('총점');
  if (headers.length > 0) jSheet.getRange(1, 4, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
  normalizeJaturiSheetStructure_(jSheet);

  for (let i = 0; i < ROSTER_ROW_COUNT; i++) {
    recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRowBySheetAndMonth_(jSheet, FIRST_DATA_ROW + i, month);
  }
  invalidateDashboardCache_();
}

function deleteMonthSheets_(month) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dataSheet = getSheetByMonth_('데이터', month);
  const jSheet = getSheetByMonth_('자투리', month);
  let deleted = false;

  if (dataSheet) {
    ss.deleteSheet(dataSheet);
    deleted = true;
  }
  if (jSheet) {
    ss.deleteSheet(jSheet);
    deleted = true;
  }
  return deleted;
}

function moveStudentSeatCurrentMonth_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const rosterSheet = ss.getSheetByName(CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
  const dataSheet = getCurrentDataSheet_();
  const jSheet = getCurrentJaturiSheet_();
  if (!rosterSheet || !dataSheet || !jSheet) return;

  const studentId = normalizeString_(rosterSheet.getRange('G1').getValue());
  const targetSeat = normalizeString_(rosterSheet.getRange('G2').getValue());
  if (!studentId || !targetSeat) {
    ss.toast('G1에 학생 학번, G2에 새 좌석을 입력하세요.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }

  const rosterValues = rosterSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 3).getValues();
  let sourceRow = -1;
  let targetRow = -1;

  rosterValues.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const actualRow = FIRST_DATA_ROW + idx;
    if (normalizeString_(row[1]) === studentId) sourceRow = actualRow;
    if (normalizeString_(row[0]) === targetSeat) targetRow = actualRow;
  });

  if (sourceRow === -1) {
    ss.toast('해당 학번 학생을 찾지 못했습니다.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }
  if (targetRow === -1) {
    ss.toast('새 좌석을 찾지 못했습니다.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }
  if (sourceRow === targetRow) {
    ss.toast('현재 좌석과 동일합니다.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }

  swapRangeValues_(rosterSheet, sourceRow, targetRow, 2, 2);
  swapRangeValues_(dataSheet, sourceRow, targetRow, 2, 4);
  swapRangeValues_(jSheet, sourceRow, targetRow, 2, jSheet.getLastColumn() - 1);

  rosterSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3)
    .copyTo(dataSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);
  rosterSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3)
    .copyTo(jSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, 3), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);

  recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRow_(jSheet, sourceRow);
  recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRow_(jSheet, targetRow);

  rosterSheet.getRange('G1:G3').clearContent();
  rosterSheet.getRange('G3').insertCheckboxes().setValue(false);
  dataSheet.hideSheet();
  invalidateDashboardCache_();
  ss.toast('좌석 이동이 완료되었습니다.', '완료', 2);
}

function swapRangeValues_(sheet, row1, row2, startCol, numCols) {
  const range1 = sheet.getRange(row1, startCol, 1, numCols);
  const range2 = sheet.getRange(row2, startCol, 1, numCols);
  const values1 = range1.getValues();
  const values2 = range2.getValues();
  range1.setValues(values2);
  range2.setValues(values1);
}

function setTodayAttendanceOnJaturiRow_(sheet, row, timeStr) {
  const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const dateCol = getDateColumnIndex_(sheet, todayStr);
  if (dateCol === -1) return;
  sheet.getRange(row, dateCol).setValue(timeStr);
}

function clearTodayAttendanceOnJaturiRow_(sheet, row) {
  const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const dateCol = getDateColumnIndex_(sheet, todayStr);
  if (dateCol === -1) return;
  sheet.getRange(row, dateCol).clearContent();
}

function clearCurrentMonthOperationalCells_(dataSheet, jSheet, row, clearOnlyIfNoId) {
  const id = normalizeString_(dataSheet.getRange(row, 2).getValue());
  if (clearOnlyIfNoId && id) return;

  dataSheet.getRange(row, 4, 1, 2).clearContent();
  const lastCol = jSheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastCol >= 4) jSheet.getRange(row, 4, 1, lastCol - 3).clearContent();
}

function appendLog_(dateStr, id, name, status, timeValue, seat) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let logSheet = ss.getSheetByName(LOG_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!logSheet) {
    logSheet = ss.insertSheet(LOG_SHEET_NAME);
    logSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([['날짜', '학번', '이름', '상태', '시간']]);
  }
  appendRowWithScriptLock_(logSheet, [dateStr, id, name, status, timeValue], 12000);
}

function deleteLatestLog_(id, name) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const logSheet = ss.getSheetByName(LOG_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!logSheet) return;

  const logData = logSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  for (let i = logData.length - 1; i >= 1; i--) {
    const logDate = logData[i][0];
    const logDateStr = logDate instanceof Date ? Utilities.formatDate(logDate, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd') : String(logDate);
    if (logDateStr === todayStr && String(logData[i][1]) === String(id) && String(logData[i][2]) === String(name)) {
      logSheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
      break;
    }
  }
}

function replaceLogIdentity_(oldId, oldName, newId, newName) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const logSheet = ss.getSheetByName(LOG_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!logSheet) return;

  const range = logSheet.getDataRange();
  const values = range.getValues();
  let changed = false;
  for (let i = 1; i < values.length; i++) {
    if (normalizeString_(values[i][1]) === normalizeString_(oldId) && normalizeString_(values[i][2]) === normalizeString_(oldName)) {
      values[i][1] = newId;
      values[i][2] = newName;
      changed = true;
    }
  }
  if (changed) range.setValues(values);
}

function replaceLogNameById_(id, newName) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const logSheet = ss.getSheetByName(LOG_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!logSheet) return;

  const range = logSheet.getDataRange();
  const values = range.getValues();
  let changed = false;
  for (let i = 1; i < values.length; i++) {
    if (normalizeString_(values[i][1]) === normalizeString_(id)) {
      values[i][2] = newName;
      changed = true;
    }
  }
  if (changed) range.setValues(values);
}

function rebuildDailyScoresFromJaturiSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dailySheet = ss.getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!dailySheet) return;

  const rows = [['날짜', '월', '학번', '점수']];
  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const month = parseJaturiMonthFromName_(sheet.getName());
    if (!month) return;

    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < FIRST_DATA_ROW) return;
    const headers = data[0];

    for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
      const row = data[r];
      const seat = row[0];
      const id = row[1];
      if (!id) continue;

      for (let c = 3; c < headers.length; c++) {
        const header = headers[c];
        if (header === '총점') break;
        if (!(header instanceof Date)) continue;

        const timeVal = row[c];
        const timeStr = normalizeTimeValue_(timeVal);
        if (timeStr === '-') continue;

        const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(header, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        rows.push([dateKey, month, id, getScoreFromTime(timeStr, seat)]);
      }
    }
  });

  dailySheet.clearContents();
  dailySheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 4).setValues(rows);
  dailySheet.hideSheet();
}

function isDailyScoreSheetEmpty_() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  return !sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1;
}

function setDailyScoreForDate_(dateKey, studentId, score) {
  ensureDailyScoreSheet_();
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  const month = Number(String(dateKey).split('-')[1]);
  const normalizedDate = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey);
  const normalizedId = String(studentId || '').trim();

  if (!normalizedDate || !normalizedId) return;

  // 같은 날짜+같은 학번 점수는 반드시 1개만 유지합니다.
  // 학생 QR 출석 후 취소, 교사 재출석을 해도 이전 점수가 누적되지 않게 합니다.
  clearDailyScoreForDate_(normalizedDate, normalizedId);

  sheet.appendRow([normalizedDate, month, normalizedId, score]);
  sheet.hideSheet();
}

function clearDailyScoreForDate_(dateKey, studentId) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;

  const normalizedDate = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey);
  const normalizedId = String(studentId || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedDate || !normalizedId) return;

  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  for (let i = data.length - 1; i >= 1; i--) {
    const rowDate = normalizeDateKey_(data[i][0]);
    const rowId = String(data[i][2] || '').trim();
    if (rowDate === normalizedDate && rowId === normalizedId) {
      sheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
    }
  }
}

function clearCurrentMonthDailyScoresById_(studentId) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;

  const currentMonth = getCurrentMonthNumber_();
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  for (let i = data.length - 1; i >= 1; i--) {
    if (Number(data[i][1]) === currentMonth && String(data[i][2]) === String(studentId)) {
      sheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
    }
  }
}

function moveCurrentMonthDailyScoresToNewId_(oldId, newId) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;

  const currentMonth = getCurrentMonthNumber_();
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();

  const maxByDate = {};
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    const month = Number(data[i][1]);
    const id = String(data[i][2]);
    const dateKey = String(data[i][0]);
    const score = parseNumber_(data[i][3]);
    if (month !== currentMonth) continue;

    if (id === String(newId)) {
      maxByDate[dateKey] = Math.max(maxByDate[dateKey] || 0, score);
    }
    if (id === String(oldId)) {
      maxByDate[dateKey] = Math.max(maxByDate[dateKey] || 0, score);
    }
  }

  for (let i = data.length - 1; i >= 1; i--) {
    const month = Number(data[i][1]);
    const id = String(data[i][2]);
    if (month === currentMonth && (id === String(oldId) || id === String(newId))) {
      sheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
    }
  }

  Object.keys(maxByDate).sort().forEach(dateKey => {
    sheet.appendRow([dateKey, currentMonth, newId, maxByDate[dateKey]]);
  });
  sheet.hideSheet();
}


function buildDailyScoreIndex_(dateKeys) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  const index = {};
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return index;

  const allowed = {};
  dateKeys.forEach(key => { allowed[key] = true; });

  const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
  data.forEach(row => {
    const dateKey = normalizeDateKey_(row[0]);
    const id = String(row[2] || '').trim();
    const score = parseNumber_(row[3]);
    if (!allowed[dateKey] || !id) return;
    if (!index[dateKey]) index[dateKey] = {};
    index[dateKey][id] = (index[dateKey][id] || 0) + score;
  });

  return index;
}

function getDailyScoreByVariantsFromIndex_(index, dateKey, idVariants) {
  if (!index[dateKey]) return 0;
  let total = 0;
  idVariants.forEach(id => {
    total += parseNumber_(index[dateKey][String(id)]);
  });
  return total;
}

function getCurrentMonthDailyScoreTotalById_(studentId) {
  return getMonthDailyScoreTotalById_(studentId, getCurrentMonthNumber_());
}

function recalcCurrentMonthTotalsFromDailyScore_() {
  const sheet = getCurrentJaturiSheet_();
  if (!sheet) return;
  for (let row = FIRST_DATA_ROW; row < FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT; row++) {
    recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRow_(sheet, row);
  }
}

function recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRow_(jSheet, row) {
  recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRowBySheetAndMonth_(jSheet, row, getCurrentMonthNumber_());
}

function recalcCurrentMonthTotalForRowBySheetAndMonth_(jSheet, row, month) {
  const totalCol = getTotalColumnIndex_(jSheet);
  if (totalCol === -1) return;

  const id = normalizeString_(jSheet.getRange(row, 2).getValue());
  if (!id) {
    jSheet.getRange(row, totalCol).clearContent();
    return;
  }

  const total = getFixedPastTotalById_(id, month) + getMonthDailyScoreTotalById_(id, month);
  jSheet.getRange(row, totalCol).setValue(total);
}

function getMonthDailyScoreTotalById_(studentId, month) {
  const idVariants = getIdVariantsForCurrentId_(studentId);
  const variantMap = {};
  idVariants.forEach(id => { variantMap[String(id)] = true; });

  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return 0;

  const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
  let total = 0;
  data.forEach(row => {
    if (Number(row[1]) === Number(month) && variantMap[String(row[2])]) {
      total += parseNumber_(row[3]);
    }
  });
  return total;
}

function getFixedPastTotalById_(studentId, targetMonth) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const variants = getIdVariantsForCurrentId_(studentId);
  const variantMap = {};
  variants.forEach(id => { variantMap[String(id)] = true; });

  let total = 0;
  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
