    const month = parseJaturiMonthFromName_(sheet.getName());
    if (!month || month >= targetMonth) return;

    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length === 0) return;
    const headers = data[0];
    const totalIdx = headers.indexOf('총점');
    if (totalIdx === -1) return;

    for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
      const id = String(data[r][1]);
      if (variantMap[id]) {
        total += parseNumber_(data[r][totalIdx]);
        break;
      }
    }
  });
  return total;
}

function registerIdAlias_(oldId, newId) {
  oldId = normalizeString_(oldId);
  newId = normalizeString_(newId);
  if (!oldId || !newId || oldId === newId) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const map = JSON.parse(props.getProperty('ID_ALIAS_MAP') || '{}');
  map[oldId] = newId;
  props.setProperty('ID_ALIAS_MAP', JSON.stringify(map));
}

function getIdVariantsForCurrentId_(currentId) {
  const result = {};
  const queue = [String(currentId)];
  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const map = JSON.parse(props.getProperty('ID_ALIAS_MAP') || '{}');

  while (queue.length > 0) {
    const id = queue.shift();
    if (result[id]) continue;
    result[id] = true;

    Object.keys(map).forEach(oldId => {
      if (String(map[oldId]) === String(id) && !result[oldId]) queue.push(oldId);
    });
  }

  return Object.keys(result);
}

function getAttendanceTimeByIdVariants_(info, idVariants, dateKey) {
  const colIdx = info.cols[dateKey];
  if (colIdx === undefined) return '-';

  for (let i = 0; i < idVariants.length; i++) {
    const rowIndex = info.rowMap[String(idVariants[i])];
    if (rowIndex === undefined) continue;
    return normalizeTimeValue_(info.data[rowIndex][colIdx]);
  }
  return '-';
}

function getDuplicateIdsFromRoster_(roster) {
  const seen = {};
  const duplicates = {};
  roster.forEach(row => {
    const id = normalizeString_(row[1]);
    if (!id) return;
    if (seen[id]) duplicates[id] = true;
    seen[id] = true;
  });
  return Object.keys(duplicates);
}

function getMovedIdsBetweenRosters_(oldRoster, newRoster) {
  const oldMap = {};
  const newMap = {};
  oldRoster.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const id = normalizeString_(row[1]);
    if (id) oldMap[id] = idx;
  });
  newRoster.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const id = normalizeString_(row[1]);
    if (id) newMap[id] = idx;
  });

  const moved = [];
  Object.keys(newMap).forEach(id => {
    if (oldMap[id] !== undefined && oldMap[id] !== newMap[id]) moved.push(id);
  });
  return moved;
}

function normalizeCurrentEditSeats_(sheet) {
  sheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 1).setValues(getSeatList_().map(seat => [seat]));
}

function isRosterEditRange_(range) {
  return range.getRow() >= 1 &&
    range.getRow() <= FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1 &&
    range.getColumn() >= 1 &&
    range.getColumn() <= 3;
}

function getDateColumnIndex_(sheet, dateKey) {
  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
    if (headers[i] instanceof Date && Utilities.formatDate(headers[i], TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd') === dateKey) {
      return i + 1;
    }
  }
  return -1;
}

function getTotalColumnIndex_(sheet) {
  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const idx = headers.indexOf('총점');
  return idx === -1 ? -1 : idx + 1;
}

function getScoreFromTime(timeVal, seatNum) {
  if (!timeVal) return 0;
  const timeStr = timeVal instanceof Date ? Utilities.formatDate(timeVal, TZ, 'HH:mm') : String(timeVal);
  const match = timeStr.match(/(\d{1,2}):(\d{2})/);
  if (!match) return 0;

  const hours = Number(match[1]);
  const minutes = Number(match[2]);
  const isSpecial = SPECIAL_SEATS.indexOf(String(seatNum || '').trim()) !== -1;

  if (isSpecial) {
    if (hours < 8) return 4;
    if (hours === 8 && minutes < 25) return 3;
    if (hours === 8 && minutes < 30) return 2;
    return 0;
  }

  if (hours < 8) return 4;
  if (hours > 8) return 0;
  if (minutes <= 1) return 4;
  if (minutes <= 6) return 3;
  if (minutes <= 11) return 2;
  if (minutes <= 16) return 1;
  return 0;
}

function getSeatList_() {
  const seats = [];
  for (let i = 1; i <= 36; i++) seats.push('폐쇄' + i);
  for (let i = 1; i <= 24; i++) seats.push('개방' + i);
  return seats;
}

function getCurrentMonthNumber_() {
  return new Date().getMonth() + 1;
}

function getDataSheetName_(month) {
  return '자투리 데이터(' + month + '월)';
}

function getJaturiSheetName_(month) {
  return '자투리(' + month + '월)';
}

function getCurrentDataSheet_() {
  return getSheetByMonth_('데이터', getCurrentMonthNumber_());
}

function getCurrentJaturiSheet_() {
  return getSheetByMonth_('자투리', getCurrentMonthNumber_());
}

function getSheetByMonth_(type, month) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  if (type === '데이터') {
    return ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month))
      || ss.getSheetByName('데이터(' + month + '월)')
      || (month === getCurrentMonthNumber_() ? ss.getSheetByName('데이터') : null);
  }
  return ss.getSheetByName(getJaturiSheetName_(month)) || ss.getSheetByName('자투리' + month + '월');
}

function parseMonthValue_(value) {
  if (typeof value === 'number') return value >= 1 && value <= 12 ? value : null;
  const match = String(value || '').match(/(\d{1,2})/);
  if (!match) return null;
  const month = Number(match[1]);
  return month >= 1 && month <= 12 ? month : null;
}

function parseJaturiMonthFromName_(name) {
  let match = String(name || '').match(/^자투리\((\d{1,2})월\)$/);
  if (match) return Number(match[1]);
  match = String(name || '').match(/^자투리(\d{1,2})월$/);
  if (match) return Number(match[1]);
  return null;
}

function getWeekdayDatesForMonth_(month) {
  const year = new Date().getFullYear();
  const dates = [];
  const cursor = new Date(year, month - 1, 1);
  while (cursor.getMonth() === month - 1) {
    const day = cursor.getDay();
    if (day !== 0 && day !== 6) dates.push(new Date(cursor));
    cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() + 1);
  }
  return dates;
}

function getRecentWeekdayDates_(count) {
  const dates = [];
  const cursor = new Date();
  cursor.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  while (dates.length < count) {
    const day = cursor.getDay();
    if (day !== 0 && day !== 6) dates.push(new Date(cursor));
    cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() - 1);
  }
  return dates.reverse();
}

function buildJaturiSheetInfo_(sheet) {
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0] || [];
  const cols = {};
  headers.forEach((header, idx) => {
    if (header === '총점') cols['총점'] = idx;
    else if (header instanceof Date) cols[Utilities.formatDate(header, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd')] = idx;
  });

  const rowMap = {};
  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const id = data[r][1];
    if (id) rowMap[String(id)] = r;
  }

  return { data: data, cols: cols, rowMap: rowMap };
}

function normalizeTimeValue_(value) {
  if (!value) return '-';
  if (value instanceof Date) return Utilities.formatDate(value, TZ, 'HH:mm');
  const text = String(value).trim();
  return text ? text : '-';
}

function parseNumber_(value) {
  const num = Number(value);
  return isNaN(num) ? 0 : num;
}

function normalizeString_(value) {
  return String(value || '').trim();
}


/** =========================
 *  야간 당월 출석부 수정 → 야간데이터/야간 출석부 반영
 *  ========================= */
function setupNightCurrentEditControls_(sheet) {
  sheet.getRange('P1').setValue('이동할 학생 학번');
  sheet.getRange('P2').setValue('새 좌석');
  sheet.getRange('P3').setValue('좌석 이동 실행');
  sheet.getRange('P5').setValue('좌석 이동은 Q1~Q3 사용');
  sheet.getRange('P6').setValue('신청요일·타임·조퇴시간은 A~N에서 직접 수정');
  sheet.getRange('P7').setValue('빈칸=신청, x=미신청, 20:30=조퇴');

  const seatRule = SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()
    .requireValueInList(getSeatList_(), true)
    .setAllowInvalid(false)
    .build();
  sheet.getRange('Q2').setDataValidation(seatRule);
  sheet.getRange('Q3').insertCheckboxes();
}

function isNightRosterEditRange_(range) {
  const row = range.getRow();
  const col = range.getColumn();
  const lastRow = row + range.getNumRows() - 1;
  const lastCol = col + range.getNumColumns() - 1;
  return lastRow >= FIRST_DATA_ROW && row <= FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1 && lastCol >= 1 && col <= NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS;
}

function syncNightCurrentEditSheetFromCurrentMonth_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const editSheet = ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!editSheet) return;

  const source = getCurrentNightDataSheet_() || ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME);
  if (!source) {
    setupNightCurrentEditControls_(editSheet);
    return;
  }

  source.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS)
    .copyTo(editSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_NORMAL, false);
  setupNightCurrentEditControls_(editSheet);
}

function syncNightCurrentEditChangesToCurrentMonth_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const editSheet = ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
  let dataSheet = getCurrentNightDataSheet_();
  const month = getCurrentMonthNumber_();

  if (!editSheet) return;

  if (!dataSheet) {
    createNightMonthSheetsFromSource_(month, NIGHT_CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
    dataSheet = getCurrentNightDataSheet_();
  }
  if (!dataSheet) return;

  const values = editSheet.getRange(1, 1, FIRST_DATA_ROW + ROSTER_ROW_COUNT - 1, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS).getValues();
  dataSheet.getRange(1, 1, values.length, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS).setValues(values);
  dataSheet.hideSheet();

  refreshNightStudySheetFromSchedule_(month);
  cleanupNightSheets_();
  invalidateDashboardCache_();
}

function moveNightStudentSeatCurrentMonth_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const editSheet = ss.getSheetByName(NIGHT_CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME);
  const dataSheet = getCurrentNightDataSheet_();
  const studySheet = getCurrentNightStudySheet_();
  if (!editSheet || !dataSheet || !studySheet) {
    ss.toast('현재 월 야간 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }

  const studentId = normalizeString_(editSheet.getRange('Q1').getValue());
  const targetSeat = normalizeString_(editSheet.getRange('Q2').getValue());
  if (!studentId || !targetSeat) {
    ss.toast('Q1에 학생 학번, Q2에 새 좌석을 입력하세요.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }

  const rosterValues = editSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS).getValues();
  let sourceRow = -1;
  let targetRow = -1;

  rosterValues.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const actualRow = FIRST_DATA_ROW + idx;
    if (normalizeString_(row[1]) === studentId) sourceRow = actualRow;
    if (normalizeString_(row[0]) === targetSeat) targetRow = actualRow;
  });

  if (sourceRow === -1) {
    ss.toast('해당 학번 학생을 찾지 못했습니다.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }
  if (targetRow === -1) {
    ss.toast('새 좌석을 찾지 못했습니다.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }
  if (sourceRow === targetRow) {
    ss.toast('현재 좌석과 동일합니다.', '안내', 3);
    return;
  }

  // 좌석열(A)은 고정하고, 학생 정보·신청 요일·조퇴시간·비고(B:N)를 이동/교환합니다.
  swapRangeValues_(editSheet, sourceRow, targetRow, 2, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS - 1);
  swapRangeValues_(dataSheet, sourceRow, targetRow, 2, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS - 1);

  // 월별 야간 출석부는 좌석(A)은 고정, 학생정보 및 기존 출석 기록(B:끝)을 같이 이동/교환합니다.
  const lastCol = studySheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastCol >= 2) {
    swapRangeValues_(studySheet, sourceRow, targetRow, 2, lastCol - 1);
  }

  editSheet.getRange('Q1:Q3').clearContent();
  editSheet.getRange('Q3').insertCheckboxes().setValue(false);
  dataSheet.hideSheet();
  refreshCurrentNightStudySheetFromSchedule_();
  cleanupNightSheets_();
  arrangeIntegratedSheets_();
  invalidateDashboardCache_();
  ss.toast('야간 좌석 이동이 완료되었습니다.', '완료', 2);
}

function refreshCurrentNightStudySheetFromSchedule_() {
  const month = getCurrentMonthNumber_();
  refreshNightStudySheetFromSchedule_(month);
}

function refreshNightStudySheetFromSchedule_(month) {
  const dataSheet = getNightDataSheet_(month);
  const studySheet = getNightStudySheet_(month);
  if (!dataSheet || !studySheet) return;

  const dataValues = dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS).getValues();
  const dataDisplayValues = dataSheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, NIGHT_ROSTER_COLS).getDisplayValues();
  const scheduleIndexMap = buildNightDataScheduleIndexMap_(dataSheet);

  const base = dataValues.map(row => [row[0], row[1], row[2]]);
  studySheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 1, ROSTER_ROW_COUNT, 3).setValues(base);

  const lastCol = studySheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastCol < 4) return;

  const numRows = ROSTER_ROW_COUNT;
  const numCols = lastCol - 3;
  const headers = studySheet.getRange(1, 4, 1, numCols).getDisplayValues()[0];
  const parsedHeaders = headers.map(h => parseNightStudyHeader_(h));

  const bodyRange = studySheet.getRange(FIRST_DATA_ROW, 4, numRows, numCols);
  const values = bodyRange.getValues();
  const displayValues = bodyRange.getDisplayValues();
  const backgrounds = bodyRange.getBackgrounds();

  for (let r = 0; r < numRows; r++) {
    for (let j = 0; j < numCols; j++) {
      const parsed = parsedHeaders[j];
      if (!parsed) continue;

      const valueText = String(displayValues[r][j] || '').trim();
      const hasAttendance = /^(출석|지각)\b/.test(valueText);

      // 이미 실제 출석/지각으로 처리된 셀은 절대 덮어쓰지 않습니다.
      if (hasAttendance) {
        if (valueText.indexOf('지각') === 0) {
          backgrounds[r][j] = '#d9d9d9';
        } else {
          backgrounds[r][j] = '#fff2cc';
        }
        continue;
      }

      const mapKey = parsed.dayLabel + '_' + parsed.timeNo;
      const relIdx = scheduleIndexMap[mapKey];
      const rawValue = relIdx == null ? '' : dataValues[r][NIGHT_FIRST_TIME_COL - 1 + relIdx];
      const rawDisplay = relIdx == null ? '' : dataDisplayValues[r][NIGHT_FIRST_TIME_COL - 1 + relIdx];
      const scheduleText = formatNightScheduleCellForStudy_(rawValue, rawDisplay);
      const scheduleState = getNightScheduleState_(rawValue);

      if (scheduleState.type === 'off') {
        values[r][j] = '미신청';
        backgrounds[r][j] = '#4b5563';
      } else {
        // 일반 신청 학생과 조퇴/하원 시간이 입력된 학생은 출석 전까지 모두 미출석 상태입니다.
        // 조퇴/하원 시간은 야간데이터에서 읽어 웹앱 좌석 이름 아래에 표시하므로, 출석부 셀에는 쓰지 않습니다.
        values[r][j] = '';
        backgrounds[r][j] = '#f4cccc';
      }
    }
  }

  bodyRange.setValues(values);
  bodyRange.setBackgrounds(backgrounds);
  formatNightStudySheet_(studySheet, month);
  invalidateDashboardCache_();
}

function parseNightStudyHeader_(headerText) {
  const text = String(headerText || '').trim();
  const m = text.match(/^(\d{1,2})\/(\d{1,2})\(([^)]*)\)\s*([12])타임$/);
  if (!m) return null;
  const dayMatch = String(m[3] || '').match(/[월화수목금]/);
  return {
    month: Number(m[1]),
    day: Number(m[2]),
    dayLabel: dayMatch ? dayMatch[0] : '',
    timeNo: Number(m[4])
  };
}

function normalizeNightStudySheetNames_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const m = sheet.getName().match(/^야간자습\((\d{1,2})월\)$/);
    if (!m) return;
    const newName = getNightStudySheetName_(Number(m[1]));
    if (!ss.getSheetByName(newName)) sheet.setName(newName);
  });
}

function arrangeIntegratedSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const currentMonth = getCurrentMonthNumber_();
  const months = [];
  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const name = sheet.getName();
    let m = name.match(/^자투리\((\d{1,2})월\)$/);
    if (m) months.push(Number(m[1]));
    m = name.match(/^야간 출석부\((\d{1,2})월\)$/);
    if (m) months.push(Number(m[1]));
  });
  const monthList = [...new Set(months)].sort((a, b) => b - a);

  const orderedNames = [TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME, NIGHT_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME, CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME, NIGHT_CURRENT_EDIT_SHEET_NAME];
  monthList.forEach(month => {
    orderedNames.push(getJaturiSheetName_(month));
    orderedNames.push(getNightStudySheetName_(month));
  });

  let pos = 1;
  orderedNames.forEach(name => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (!sheet) return;
    ss.setActiveSheet(sheet);
    ss.moveActiveSheet(pos);
    pos++;
  });

  // 숨김 처리 대상은 항상 다시 숨깁니다.
  const hiddenNames = [LOG_SHEET_NAME, DAILY_SCORE_SHEET_NAME, SETTINGS_SHEET_NAME, NIGHT_LOG_SHEET_NAME];
  hiddenNames.forEach(name => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (sheet) sheet.hideSheet();
  });
  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    if (/^자투리 데이터\(\d{1,2}월\)$/.test(sheet.getName()) || /^야간데이터\(\d{1,2}월\)$/.test(sheet.getName())) {
      sheet.hideSheet();
    }
  });
}

const NIGHT_SUPERVISOR_SPREADSHEET_ID = '15Badt6rIWeN6VH0aWKghjPmFLkqjBnB-jehQbs0uaoQ';
const NIGHT_SUPERVISOR_CACHE_KEY = 'night_supervisor_schedule_v2';

function getNightSupervisorSchedule() {
  const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
  try {
    const cached = cache.get(NIGHT_SUPERVISOR_CACHE_KEY);
    if (cached) return JSON.parse(cached);
  } catch (e) {}

  const result = [];
  const today = new Date();
  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(NIGHT_SUPERVISOR_SPREADSHEET_ID);

    for (let monthOffset = 0; monthOffset < 4 && result.length < 3; monthOffset++) {
      const cursor = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() + monthOffset, 1);
      const sheet = getSupervisorMonthSheet_(ss, cursor.getMonth() + 1);
      if (!sheet) continue;

      const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
      if (lastRow < 2) continue;

      // A~E를 한 번에 읽고, C/E 색상만 판단합니다. 결과는 캐시해 반복 로딩을 줄입니다.
      const range = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, 5);
      const values = range.getValues();
      const displays = range.getDisplayValues();
      const backgrounds = range.getBackgrounds();

      for (let r = 0; r < values.length && result.length < 3; r++) {
        const dateObj = parseSupervisorDate_(values[r][0], displays[r][0], cursor.getFullYear(), cursor.getMonth());
        if (!dateObj) continue;

        dateObj.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
        if (dateObj < today) continue;

        const day = dateObj.getDay();
        if (day === 0 || day === 6) continue;

        const generalRaw = String(displays[r][2] || '').trim();
        const grade3Raw = String(displays[r][4] || '').trim();
        const generalBg = String(backgrounds[r][2] || '').toLowerCase();
        const grade3Bg = String(backgrounds[r][4] || '').toLowerCase();

        if (isSupervisorGray_(generalBg)) continue;
        if (!isTeacherNameLike_(generalRaw)) continue;

        const grade3 = (!isSupervisorGray_(grade3Bg) && isTeacherNameLike_(grade3Raw))
          ? grade3Raw
          : '없음';

        result.push({
          date: formatSupervisorDate_(dateObj),
          general: generalRaw,
          grade3: grade3
        });
      }
    }

    const payload = { ok: true, items: result };
    try { cache.put(NIGHT_SUPERVISOR_CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify(payload), 1800); } catch (e) {}
    return payload;
  } catch (e) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      message: '감독 일정 정보를 불러오지 못했습니다: ' + e.message,
      items: []
    };
  }
}

function getSupervisorMonthSheet_(ss, month) {
  const candidates = [
    month + '월',
    String(month).padStart(2, '0') + '월',
    month + '',
    String(month).padStart(2, '0')
  ];

  for (let i = 0; i < candidates.length; i++) {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(candidates[i]);
    if (sheet) return sheet;
  }

  const sheets = ss.getSheets();
  for (let i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
    const name = sheets[i].getName();
    if (name.indexOf(month + '월') !== -1) return sheets[i];
  }

  return null;
}

function parseSupervisorDate_(value, displayText, year, monthIndex) {
  if (value instanceof Date) {
    return new Date(value.getFullYear(), value.getMonth(), value.getDate());
  }

  const text = String(displayText || value || '').trim();
  if (!text) return null;

  let m = text.match(/(\d{4})[-./]\s*(\d{1,2})[-./]\s*(\d{1,2})/);
  if (m) return new Date(Number(m[1]), Number(m[2]) - 1, Number(m[3]));

  m = text.match(/(\d{1,2})\s*[-./월]\s*(\d{1,2})/);
  if (m) return new Date(Number(year), Number(m[1]) - 1, Number(m[2]));

  m = text.match(/(\d{1,2})/);
  if (m && typeof monthIndex === 'number') return new Date(Number(year), Number(monthIndex), Number(m[1]));

  return null;
}

function formatSupervisorDate_(dateObj) {
  const days = ['일', '월', '화', '수', '목', '금', '토'];
  const mm = String(dateObj.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
  const dd = String(dateObj.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  return mm + '/' + dd + '(' + days[dateObj.getDay()] + ')';
}

function isSupervisorGray_(hex) {
  const color = String(hex || '').toLowerCase();
  if (!/^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/.test(color)) return false;

  const r = parseInt(color.slice(1, 3), 16);
  const g = parseInt(color.slice(3, 5), 16);
  const b = parseInt(color.slice(5, 7), 16);
  const diff = Math.max(r, g, b) - Math.min(r, g, b);
  const avg = (r + g + b) / 3;

  return diff <= 14 && avg >= 120 && avg <= 235;
}

function isTeacherNameLike_(text) {
  const value = String(text || '').trim();
  if (!value) return false;

  const excluded = [
    '전국연합', '졸업앨범', '체육한마당', '부처님', '공휴일', '행사',
    '시험', '모의고사', '재량', '방학', '없음', '휴업', '대체공휴일',
    '현충일', '개교기념일', '수련회', '체험학습', '진로', '상담'
  ];

  for (let i = 0; i < excluded.length; i++) {
    if (value.indexOf(excluded[i]) !== -1) return false;
  }

  return /^[가-힣]{2,4}$/.test(value);
}

 */

let WD_SS_CACHE_ = null;

function wdGetSS_() {
  if (!WD_SS_CACHE_) WD_SS_CACHE_ = SpreadsheetApp.openById(WD_SPREADSHEET_ID);
  return WD_SS_CACHE_;
}

function wdSheet_(name, optional) {
  const sheet = wdGetSS_().getSheetByName(name);
  if (!sheet && !optional) throw new Error('시트를 찾을 수 없습니다: ' + name);
  return sheet;
}

function wdAllValues_(sheetName, optional) {
  const sheet = wdSheet_(sheetName, optional);
  if (!sheet) return [];
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < 1 || lastCol < 1) return [];
  return sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).getDisplayValues();
}

function wdValues_(sheetName, optional) {
  const values = wdAllValues_(sheetName, optional);
  return values.length > 1 ? values.slice(1) : [];
}

function wdCacheGet_(key) {
  const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
  const value = cache.get(key);
  if (!value) return null;
  try { return JSON.parse(value); } catch (_) { return null; }
}

function wdCachePut_(key, value, seconds) {
  try { CacheService.getScriptCache().put(key, JSON.stringify(value), seconds); } catch (_) {}
  return value;
}

function wdStaticValues_(sheetName, optional) {
  const key = 'wd6_static_' + sheetName;
  const cached = wdCacheGet_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  return wdCachePut_(key, wdValues_(sheetName, optional), WD_STATIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function wdStaticAllValues_(sheetName, optional) {
  const key = 'wd6_static_all_' + sheetName;
  const cached = wdCacheGet_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  return wdCachePut_(key, wdAllValues_(sheetName, optional), WD_STATIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function wdClearStaticCache() {
  const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
  Object.keys(WD_SHEETS).forEach(k => {
    try { cache.remove('wd6_static_' + WD_SHEETS[k]); } catch (_) {}
    try { cache.remove('wd6_static_all_' + WD_SHEETS[k]); } catch (_) {}
  });
  return { ok: true };
}

function wdEnsureLogSheet_() {
  const ss = wdGetSS_();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(WD_SHEETS.ATTENDANCE_LOG);
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet(WD_SHEETS.ATTENDANCE_LOG);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() === 0) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, WD_LOG_HEADERS.length).setValues([WD_LOG_HEADERS]);
  } else {
    const current = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, Math.max(WD_LOG_HEADERS.length, sheet.getLastColumn())).getDisplayValues()[0];
    const mismatch = WD_LOG_HEADERS.some((h, i) => current[i] !== h);
    if (mismatch) sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, WD_LOG_HEADERS.length).setValues([WD_LOG_HEADERS]);
  }
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  return sheet;
}

function wdNow_() {
  return new Date();
}

function wdDateKey_(date) {
  return Utilities.formatDate(date || wdNow_(), WD_TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
}

function wdDayNoFromDate_(date) {
  const n = Number(Utilities.formatDate(date || wdNow_(), WD_TZ, 'u'));
  return n >= 1 && n <= 5 ? n : 0;
}

function wdDayLabelFromDate_(date) {
  return WD_DAY_LABELS[wdDayNoFromDate_(date)] || '';
}

function wdTimeKey_(date) {
  return Utilities.formatDate(date || wdNow_(), WD_TZ, 'HH:mm');
}

function wdClean_(v) {
  return String(v == null ? '' : v).trim();
}

function wdNormalizeFullWidthDigits_(value) {
  return wdClean_(value).replace(/[０-９]/g, ch => String(ch.charCodeAt(0) - 65248));
}

function wdNormalizeSubjectKey_(value) {
  return wdClean_(value)
    .replace(/\s+/g, '')
    .replace(/Ⅰ/g, 'I').replace(/Ⅱ/g, 'II').replace(/Ⅲ/g, 'III')
    .replace(/Ⅳ/g, 'IV').replace(/Ⅴ/g, 'V')
    .replace(/1/g, 'I').replace(/2/g, 'II').replace(/3/g, 'III')
    .toLowerCase();
}

function wdTeacherList_(value) {
  return wdClean_(value)
    .split(/[,+/·ㆍ&]/)
    .map(s => wdClean_(s))
    .filter(Boolean);
}

function wdTeacherText_(list) {
  const map = {};
  (list || []).forEach(t => { if (t) map[t] = true; });
  return Object.keys(map).join(',');
}

function wdTeacherIncludes_(teacherListText, teacherName) {
  if (!teacherName) return false;
  return wdTeacherList_(teacherListText).indexOf(teacherName) !== -1;
}

function wdClassGroupFromStudentId_(studentId) {
  const id = wdClean_(studentId).replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
  if (id.length >= 5) return Number(id.charAt(2)) || 0;
  if (id.length >= 4) return Number(id.charAt(1)) || 0;
  return 0;
}

function wdNormalizeSeatType_(value) {
  const text = wdClean_(value);
  if (text.indexOf('개방') >= 0) return '개방';
  if (text.indexOf('폐쇄') >= 0) return '폐쇄';
  return text.replace(/형/g, '');
}

function wdMakeSeatKey_(seatType, seatNo) {
  const type = wdNormalizeSeatType_(seatType);
  const num = Number(String(seatNo || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '')) || 0;
  if (!type || !num) return '';
  return type + num;
}

function wdMakeRosterKey_(teacher, subjectKey, classGroup) {
  return [wdClean_(teacher).replace(/\s+/g, ''), wdClean_(subjectKey), Number(classGroup)].join('|');
}

function wdHomeroomRosterKey_(classGroup) {
  return '금요일창체_' + Number(classGroup || 0) + '반';
}

function wdMakeRecordKey_(dateKey, period, rosterKey, studentId) {
  return [dateKey, Number(period), wdClean_(rosterKey), wdClean_(studentId)].join('|');
}

function wdIsActiveStatus_(status) {
  const s = wdClean_(status);
  return s === WD_STATUS_PRESENT || s === WD_STATUS_WUNGJI_LEGACY;
}

function wdIsFridayHomeroomCourse_(course) {
  return Number(course && course.dayNo) === 5 && WD_FRIDAY_HOMEROOM_PERIODS.indexOf(Number(course && course.period)) !== -1;
}

function wdSpecialFridayTeacherMap_(dateKey) {
  const source = Object.assign({}, WD_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS);
  if ((dateKey || wdDateKey_()) >= '2026-08-01') {
    Object.keys(WD_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS_AFTER_202608).forEach(cls => {
      source[cls] = WD_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS_AFTER_202608[cls];
    });
  }
  const map = {};
  Object.keys(source).forEach(cls => map[String(cls)] = source[cls].slice());
  return map;
}

function wdGetHomeroomTeacherList_(classGroup, dateKey) {
  const map = wdSpecialFridayTeacherMap_(dateKey);
  return map[String(Number(classGroup))] || [];
}

function wdTeacherCanAccessCourse_(course, teacherName) {
  if (!course || !teacherName) return false;
  if (wdTeacherIncludes_(course.teacher, teacherName)) return true;
  if (!wdIsFridayHomeroomCourse_(course)) return false;
  return wdGetHomeroomTeacherList_(course.classGroup, course.dateKey).indexOf(teacherName) !== -1;
}

function wdGetTeacherNames_() {
  const names = {};
  try { wdStaticValues_(WD_SHEETS.TEACHER_SUBJECT, true).forEach(row => wdTeacherList_(row[1]).forEach(n => names[n] = true)); } catch (_) {}
  try { wdStaticValues_(WD_SHEETS.TIMETABLE, true).forEach(row => wdTeacherList_(row[6]).forEach(n => names[n] = true)); } catch (_) {}
  try { wdStaticValues_(WD_SHEETS.SUBJECT_ROSTER, true).forEach(row => wdTeacherList_(row[4]).forEach(n => names[n] = true)); } catch (_) {}
  try {
    const today = wdDateKey_();
    const hr = wdSpecialFridayTeacherMap_(today);
    Object.keys(hr).forEach(cls => (hr[cls] || []).forEach(n => names[n] = true));
  } catch (_) {}
  return Object.keys(names).filter(Boolean).sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'ko'));
}

function wdLogin(name) {
  const id = wdClean_(name);
  if (!id) return { ok: false, message: '이름을 입력하세요.' };
  const dateKey = wdDateKey_();
  const ranges = wdGetPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey);
  const currentPeriod = wdGetCurrentPeriod_(ranges);
  if (id.toLowerCase() === 'admin') {
    return {
      ok: true,
      role: 'admin',
      id: 'admin',
      displayName: '관리자',
      dateKey: dateKey,
      dayLabel: wdDayLabelFromDate_(),
      periodRanges: ranges,
      currentPeriod: currentPeriod
    };
  }

  // v6: 로그인 속도를 위해 교사명 전체 검증과 출석 집계를 로그인 단계에서 하지 않습니다.
  // 실제 수업 클릭/처리 단계에서 담당 교사 권한을 다시 확인합니다.
  const schedule = wdGetScheduleForTeacherFast_(id, dateKey);
  if (!schedule.courses.length) return { ok: false, message: '오늘 표시할 수업이 없습니다.' };
  return {
    ok: true,
    role: 'teacher',
    id: id,
    displayName: id,
    dateKey: dateKey,
    dayLabel: schedule.dayLabel,
    periodRanges: ranges,
    schedule: schedule
  };
}

function wdGetScheduleForTeacherFast_(teacherName, dateKey) {
  const dayNo = wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(dateKey);
  const courses = wdGetEffectiveCoursesForDate_(dateKey)
    .filter(c => wdTeacherCanAccessCourse_(c, teacherName))
    .sort((a, b) => Number(a.period) - Number(b.period) || Number(a.classGroup) - Number(b.classGroup))
    .map(c => Object.assign({}, c, { totalCount: '', activeCount: '' }));
  return {
    dateKey: dateKey,
    dayNo: dayNo,
    dayLabel: WD_DAY_LABELS[dayNo] || '',
    courses: courses
  };
}

function wdGetSettingsMap_() {
  const rows = wdStaticValues_(WD_SHEETS.SETTINGS, true);
  const result = {};
  rows.forEach(r => {
    const key = wdClean_(r[0]);
    if (key) result[key] = wdClean_(r[1]);
  });
  return result;
}

function wdParseTimeMinutes_(value) {
  const text = wdNormalizeTime_(value);
  const m = text.match(/^(\d{2}):(\d{2})$/);
  if (!m) return -1;
  return Number(m[1]) * 60 + Number(m[2]);
}

function wdNormalizeTime_(value) {
  const text = wdNormalizeFullWidthDigits_(value);
  if (!text) return '';
  let m = text.match(/^(\d{1,2}):(\d{2})$/);
  if (!m) {
    const digits = text.replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
    if (digits.length >= 4) m = [null, digits.slice(0, 2), digits.slice(2, 4)];
  }
  if (!m) return '';
  const hh = Number(m[1]);
  const mm = Number(m[2]);
  if (hh < 0 || hh > 23 || mm < 0 || mm > 59) return '';
  return String(hh).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(mm).padStart(2, '0');
}

function wdAddMinutes_(timeText, minutes) {
  const base = wdParseTimeMinutes_(timeText);
  if (base < 0) return '';
  const total = base + Number(minutes || 0);
  return String(Math.floor(total / 60)).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(total % 60).padStart(2, '0');
}

function wdGetPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey) {
  dateKey = dateKey || wdDateKey_();
  const cacheKey = 'wd6_ranges_' + dateKey;
  const cached = wdCacheGet_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;
  const settings = wdGetSettingsMap_();
  const duration = Number(settings.CLASS_DURATION_MINUTES) || 50;
  const ranges = {};
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) {
    const start = wdNormalizeTime_(settings['PERIOD_' + p + '_START'] || WD_DEFAULT_PERIOD_TIMES[p]);
    const end = wdNormalizeTime_(settings['PERIOD_' + p + '_END']) || wdAddMinutes_(start, duration);
    ranges[p] = { start: start, end: end };
  }
  const sheet = wdSheet_(WD_SHEETS.DATE_TIME, true);
  if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, Math.min(5, sheet.getLastColumn())).getDisplayValues().forEach(r => {
      const rowDate = wdNormalizeDateKey_(r[0]);
      const period = Number(r[1]);
      if (rowDate !== dateKey || !(period >= 1 && period <= 7)) return;
      const start = wdNormalizeTime_(r[2]);
      const end = wdNormalizeTime_(r[3]);
      if (start) ranges[period].start = start;
      if (end) ranges[period].end = end;
      else if (start) ranges[period].end = wdAddMinutes_(start, duration);
    });
  }
  return wdCachePut_(cacheKey, ranges, WD_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function wdGetCurrentPeriod_(ranges) {
  ranges = ranges || wdGetPeriodRangesForDate_(wdDateKey_());
  const now = wdNow_();
  const nowMinutes = Number(Utilities.formatDate(now, WD_TZ, 'H')) * 60 + Number(Utilities.formatDate(now, WD_TZ, 'm'));
  let closest = 1;
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) {
    const start = wdParseTimeMinutes_(ranges[p] && ranges[p].start);
    const end = wdParseTimeMinutes_(ranges[p] && ranges[p].end);
    if (start >= 0 && end >= 0 && nowMinutes >= start && nowMinutes <= end + 4) return p;
    if (start >= 0 && nowMinutes >= start) closest = p;
  }
  return closest;
}

function wdNormalizeDateKey_(value) {
  if (value instanceof Date) return Utilities.formatDate(value, WD_TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const text = wdNormalizeFullWidthDigits_(value);
  if (!text) return '';
  let m = text.match(/(\d{4})[-./](\d{1,2})[-./](\d{1,2})/);
  if (m) return m[1] + '-' + String(Number(m[2])).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(Number(m[3])).padStart(2, '0');
  return text;
}

function wdParseDate_(dateKey) {
  const key = wdNormalizeDateKey_(dateKey);
  if (!key) return null;
  const m = key.match(/^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})$/);
  if (!m) return null;
  return new Date(Number(m[1]), Number(m[2]) - 1, Number(m[3]), 12, 0, 0);
}

function wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(dateKey) {
  const parsed = wdParseDate_(dateKey);
  if (!parsed) return 0;
  let dayNo = wdDayNoFromDate_(parsed);
  const rows = wdStaticValues_(WD_SHEETS.OVERRIDE, true);
  const matches = rows.filter(r => wdNormalizeDateKey_(r[0]) === dateKey && wdClean_(r[1]) === '요일적용');
  if (matches.length) {
    const target = Number(matches[matches.length - 1][2]);
    if (target >= 1 && target <= 5) dayNo = target;
  }
  return dayNo;
}

function wdGetBaseCoursesByDay_(dayNo) {
  if (!dayNo) return [];
  return wdStaticValues_(WD_SHEETS.TIMETABLE)
    .map(row => ({
      dayNo: Number(row[0]),
      dayLabel: wdClean_(row[1]),
      period: Number(row[2]),
      classGroup: Number(row[3]),
      subject: wdClean_(row[4]),
      subjectKey: wdClean_(row[5]) || wdNormalizeSubjectKey_(row[4]),
      teacher: wdClean_(row[6]),
      raw: wdClean_(row[7])
    }))
    .filter(c => c.dayNo === Number(dayNo) && c.period && c.classGroup && c.subject && c.teacher);
}

function wdGetEffectiveCoursesForDate_(dateKey) {
  dateKey = dateKey || wdDateKey_();
  const dayNo = wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(dateKey);
  const cacheKey = 'wd6_courses_' + dateKey + '_' + dayNo;
  const cached = wdCacheGet_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;
  const bySlot = {};
  wdGetBaseCoursesByDay_(dayNo).forEach(c => {
    c.dateKey = dateKey;
    c.dayNo = dayNo;
    c.dayLabel = WD_DAY_LABELS[dayNo] || c.dayLabel;
    bySlot[c.classGroup + '|' + c.period] = c;
  });
  if (dayNo === 5) {
    Object.keys(WD_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS).forEach(cls => {
      WD_FRIDAY_HOMEROOM_PERIODS.forEach(period => {
        const teachers = wdGetHomeroomTeacherList_(cls, dateKey);
        bySlot[Number(cls) + '|' + period] = {
          dateKey: dateKey,
          dayNo: 5,
          dayLabel: '금',
          period: Number(period),
          classGroup: Number(cls),
          subject: '창체',
          subjectKey: wdNormalizeSubjectKey_('창체'),
          teacher: wdTeacherText_(teachers),
          raw: '창체(' + wdTeacherText_(teachers) + ')',
          rosterKey: wdHomeroomRosterKey_(cls),
          specialFriday: true
        };
      });
    });
  }
  const courses = Object.keys(bySlot).map(k => {
    const c = bySlot[k];
    // v6: 로그인 단계에서는 명렬키 탐색을 미룹니다. 과목 클릭/관리자 조회 시 필요한 학생 명렬만 찾습니다.
    if (c.specialFriday && !c.rosterKey) c.rosterKey = wdHomeroomRosterKey_(c.classGroup);
    c.courseKey = [c.dateKey, c.dayNo, c.period, c.classGroup, c.subjectKey, c.teacher].join('|');
    return c;
  }).sort((a, b) => Number(a.period) - Number(b.period) || Number(a.classGroup) - Number(b.classGroup) || a.subject.localeCompare(b.subject, 'ko'));
  return wdCachePut_(cacheKey, courses, WD_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function wdGetScheduleForTeacher_(teacherName, dateKey) {
  const courses = wdGetEffectiveCoursesForDate_(dateKey)
    .filter(c => wdTeacherCanAccessCourse_(c, teacherName))
    .sort((a, b) => Number(a.period) - Number(b.period) || Number(a.classGroup) - Number(b.classGroup));
  const activeMap = wdGetAttendanceMapCached_(dateKey);
  const rosterIndex = wdGetSubjectRosterIndex_();
  const applicantMap = wdGetApplicantMap_();
  const result = courses.map(c => {
    const counts = wdCountCourseStudents_(c, rosterIndex, applicantMap, activeMap, dateKey);
    return Object.assign({}, c, {
      totalCount: counts.total,
      activeCount: counts.active
    });
  });
  return { dateKey: dateKey, dayNo: wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(dateKey), dayLabel: WD_DAY_LABELS[wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(dateKey)] || '', courses: result };
}

function wdGetSubjectRosterIndex_() {
  const key = 'wd6_subject_roster_index';
  const cached = wdCacheGet_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  const byRosterKey = {};
  const byCourseKey = {};
  const byStudent = {};
  wdStaticValues_(WD_SHEETS.SUBJECT_ROSTER).forEach(row => {
    const item = {
      rosterKey: wdClean_(row[0]),
      version: wdClean_(row[1]),
      current: wdClean_(row[2]),
      teacher: wdClean_(row[4]),
      subject: wdClean_(row[5]),
      subjectKey: wdClean_(row[6]) || wdNormalizeSubjectKey_(row[5]),
      classGroup: Number(row[7]),
      studentId: wdClean_(row[8]),
      studentName: wdClean_(row[9]),
      use: wdClean_(row[10])
    };
    if (!item.rosterKey || item.current !== 'Y' || item.use !== 'Y' || !item.studentId) return;
    if (!byRosterKey[item.rosterKey]) byRosterKey[item.rosterKey] = [];
    byRosterKey[item.rosterKey].push(item);
    const courseKey = [item.subjectKey, item.classGroup].join('|');
    if (!byCourseKey[courseKey]) byCourseKey[courseKey] = [];
    byCourseKey[courseKey].push(item);
    if (!byStudent[item.studentId]) byStudent[item.studentId] = [];
    byStudent[item.studentId].push(item);
  });
  return wdCachePut_(key, { byRosterKey: byRosterKey, byCourseKey: byCourseKey, byStudent: byStudent }, WD_STATIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function wdFindRosterKeyForCourse_(course, rosterIndex) {
  rosterIndex = rosterIndex || wdGetSubjectRosterIndex_();
  if (course && course.specialFriday) return wdHomeroomRosterKey_(course.classGroup);
  const key = [course.subjectKey, course.classGroup].join('|');
  const candidates = (rosterIndex.byCourseKey[key] || []).filter(item => {
    return wdTeacherList_(course.teacher).some(t => wdTeacherIncludes_(item.teacher, t)) || wdTeacherList_(item.teacher).some(t => wdTeacherIncludes_(course.teacher, t));
  });
  if (candidates.length) return candidates[0].rosterKey;
  const loose = rosterIndex.byCourseKey[key] || [];
  return loose.length ? loose[0].rosterKey : '';
}

function wdGetApplicantMap_() {
  const rows = wdStaticValues_(WD_SHEETS.APPLICANTS);
  const map = {};
  rows.forEach(row => {
    const current = wdClean_(row[1]);
    const id = wdClean_(row[3]);
    const use = wdClean_(row[8]);
    if (current !== 'Y' || use !== 'Y' || !id) return;
    const seatType = wdNormalizeSeatType_(row[5]);
    const seatNo = Number(String(row[6] || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '')) || 0;
    const seatKey = wdClean_(row[7]) || wdMakeSeatKey_(seatType, seatNo);
    map[id] = {
      id: id,
      name: wdClean_(row[4]),
      seatType: seatType,
      seatNo: seatNo,
      seatKey: seatKey,
      classGroup: wdClassGroupFromStudentId_(id)
    };
  });
  return map;
}

function wdGetApplicantList_() {
  const map = wdGetApplicantMap_();
  return Object.keys(map).map(id => map[id]).sort(wdSortBySeat_);
}

function wdSortBySeat_(a, b) {
  const ao = wdSeatOrder_(a);
  const bo = wdSeatOrder_(b);
  if (ao !== bo) return ao - bo;
  return String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true });
}

function wdSeatOrder_(st) {
  const seat = wdClean_(st && st.seatKey);
  const m = seat.match(/^(개방|폐쇄)\s*(\d+)/);
  if (m) return (m[1] === '개방' ? 0 : 1000) + Number(m[2]);
  return 9999;
}

function wdGetAttendanceMap_(dateKey) {
  const sheet = wdEnsureLogSheet_();
  const map = {};
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return map;
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, WD_LOG_HEADERS.length).getDisplayValues();
  values.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const rowDate = wdClean_(row[1]);
    if (rowDate !== dateKey) return;
    const recordKey = wdClean_(row[0]);
    if (!recordKey) return;
    const status = wdClean_(row[12]);
    map[recordKey] = {
      rowIndex: idx + 2,
      recordKey: recordKey,
      dateKey: rowDate,
      period: Number(row[3]),
      classGroup: Number(row[4]),
      subject: wdClean_(row[5]),
      subjectKey: wdClean_(row[6]),
      teacher: wdClean_(row[7]),
      rosterKey: wdClean_(row[8]),
      studentId: wdClean_(row[9]),
      studentName: wdClean_(row[10]),
      time: wdClean_(row[11]),
      status: status,
      active: wdIsActiveStatus_(status)
    };
  });
  return map;
}

function wdGetAttendanceMapCached_(dateKey) {
  dateKey = dateKey || wdDateKey_();
  const key = 'wd6_attendance_' + dateKey;
  const cached = wdCacheGet_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  return wdCachePut_(key, wdGetAttendanceMap_(dateKey), WD_ATTENDANCE_CACHE_SECONDS);
}


function wdClearAttendanceCache_(dateKey) {
  try { CacheService.getScriptCache().remove('wd6_attendance_' + (dateKey || wdDateKey_())); } catch (_) {}
}

function wdStatsNormalize_(value) {
  return wdNormalizeFullWidthDigits_(value).replace(/\s+/g, '').trim();
}

function wdStatsDigits_(value) {
  return wdNormalizeFullWidthDigits_(value).replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
}

function wdStatsDateCandidates_(dateKey) {
  dateKey = wdClean_(dateKey) || wdDateKey_();
  const parts = dateKey.split('-');
  const y = parts[0] || Utilities.formatDate(wdNow_(), WD_TZ, 'yyyy');
  const m = Number(parts[1]) || Number(Utilities.formatDate(wdNow_(), WD_TZ, 'M'));
  const d = Number(parts[2]) || Number(Utilities.formatDate(wdNow_(), WD_TZ, 'd'));
  const mm = String(m).padStart(2, '0');
  const dd = String(d).padStart(2, '0');
  return [
    `${y}-${mm}-${dd}`, `${y}.${mm}.${dd}`, `${y}/${mm}/${dd}`,
    `${y}.${m}.${d}`, `${y}/${m}/${d}`,
    `${mm}-${dd}`, `${mm}.${dd}`, `${mm}/${dd}`,
    `${m}.${d}`, `${m}/${d}`,
    `${m}월${d}일`, `${mm}월${dd}일`,
    `${y}년${m}월${d}일`, `${y}년${mm}월${dd}일`
  ].map(wdStatsNormalize_);
}

function wdStatsTextHasDate_(text, candidates) {
  const norm = wdStatsNormalize_(text);
  if (!norm) return false;
  return (candidates || []).some(c => c && norm.indexOf(c) !== -1);
}

function wdStatsTextHasPeriod_(text, period) {
  const norm = wdStatsNormalize_(text);
  const p = String(Number(period) || '').trim();
  if (!p) return false;
  if (norm === p || norm === p + '교시') return true;
  if (norm.indexOf(p + '교시') !== -1) return true;
  if (norm.indexOf('교시' + p) !== -1) return true;
  return false;
}

function wdGetStatsSheetData_(sheet) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < 1 || lastCol < 1) return { display: [], lastRow: 0, lastCol: 0 };
  const range = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol);
  const display = range.getDisplayValues();
  range.getMergedRanges().forEach(mr => {
    const baseRow = mr.getRow();
    const baseCol = mr.getColumn();
    const value = mr.getCell(1, 1).getDisplayValue();
    for (let r = baseRow; r < baseRow + mr.getNumRows(); r++) {
      for (let c = baseCol; c < baseCol + mr.getNumColumns(); c++) {
        if (r >= 1 && r <= lastRow && c >= 1 && c <= lastCol) display[r - 1][c - 1] = value;
      }
    }
  });
  return { display: display, lastRow: lastRow, lastCol: lastCol };
}

function wdFindStatsStudentRow_(display, student) {
  const id = wdStatsDigits_(student && student.id);
  const name = wdStatsNormalize_(student && student.name);
  let nameRow = 0;
  for (let r = 0; r < display.length; r++) {
    let idHit = false;
    let nameHit = false;
    for (let c = 0; c < display[r].length; c++) {
      const text = display[r][c];
      const norm = wdStatsNormalize_(text);
      const digits = wdStatsDigits_(text);
      if (id && digits === id) idHit = true;
      if (name && norm === name) nameHit = true;
    }
    if (idHit) return r + 1;
    if (!nameRow && nameHit) nameRow = r + 1;
  }
  return nameRow;
}

function wdFindStatsStudentCol_(display, student) {
  const id = wdStatsDigits_(student && student.id);
  const name = wdStatsNormalize_(student && student.name);
  let nameCol = 0;
  const rowCount = display.length;
  const colCount = rowCount ? display[0].length : 0;
  for (let c = 0; c < colCount; c++) {
    let idHit = false;
    let nameHit = false;
    for (let r = 0; r < rowCount; r++) {
      const text = display[r][c];
      const norm = wdStatsNormalize_(text);
      const digits = wdStatsDigits_(text);
      if (id && digits === id) idHit = true;
      if (name && norm === name) nameHit = true;
    }
    if (idHit) return c + 1;
    if (!nameCol && nameHit) nameCol = c + 1;
  }
  return nameCol;
}

function wdFindStatsPeriodCol_(data, studentRow, dateKey, period) {
  const display = data.display || [];
  if (!display.length) return 0;
  const candidates = wdStatsDateCandidates_(dateKey);
  const headerRows = Math.max(1, Math.min(studentRow > 1 ? studentRow - 1 : 30, display.length, 30));
  const colCount = display[0].length;
  let periodOnlyCol = 0;
  let dateOnlyCol = 0;

  for (let c = 0; c < colCount; c++) {
    let text = '';
    let dateHit = false;
    let periodHit = false;
    for (let r = 0; r < headerRows; r++) {
      const cell = display[r][c];
      text += ' ' + cell;
      if (wdStatsTextHasDate_(cell, candidates)) dateHit = true;
      if (wdStatsTextHasPeriod_(cell, period)) periodHit = true;
    }
    if (!dateHit && wdStatsTextHasDate_(text, candidates)) dateHit = true;
    if (!periodHit && wdStatsTextHasPeriod_(text, period)) periodHit = true;
    if (dateHit && periodHit) return c + 1;
    if (periodHit && !periodOnlyCol) periodOnlyCol = c + 1;
    if (dateHit && !dateOnlyCol) dateOnlyCol = c + 1;
  }

  // 날짜가 없는 당일 전용 통계표이면 교시 열만으로 반영합니다.
  return dateOnlyCol ? 0 : periodOnlyCol;
}

function wdFindStatsPeriodRow_(data, studentCol, dateKey, period) {
  const display = data.display || [];
  if (!display.length) return 0;
  const candidates = wdStatsDateCandidates_(dateKey);
  const labelCols = Math.max(1, Math.min(studentCol > 1 ? studentCol - 1 : 10, display[0].length, 10));
  let periodOnlyRow = 0;
  let dateOnlyRow = 0;

  for (let r = 0; r < display.length; r++) {
    let text = '';
    let dateHit = false;
    let periodHit = false;
    for (let c = 0; c < labelCols; c++) {
      const cell = display[r][c];
      text += ' ' + cell;
      if (wdStatsTextHasDate_(cell, candidates)) dateHit = true;
      if (wdStatsTextHasPeriod_(cell, period)) periodHit = true;
    }
    if (!dateHit && wdStatsTextHasDate_(text, candidates)) dateHit = true;
    if (!periodHit && wdStatsTextHasPeriod_(text, period)) periodHit = true;
    if (dateHit && periodHit) return r + 1;
    if (periodHit && !periodOnlyRow) periodOnlyRow = r + 1;
    if (dateHit && !dateOnlyRow) dateOnlyRow = r + 1;
  }

  return dateOnlyRow ? 0 : periodOnlyRow;
}

function wdShouldUpdateStatsCell_(data, row, col, nextActive) {
  if (nextActive) return true;
  return wdClean_((data.display[row - 1] || [])[col - 1]) === WD_STATS_MARK_TEXT;
}

function wdAddStatsTarget_(sheet, data, targets, row, col, nextActive) {
  if (!row || !col) return false;
  if (!wdShouldUpdateStatsCell_(data, row, col, nextActive)) return false;
  targets[sheet.getRange(row, col).getA1Notation()] = true;
  return true;
}

function wdSyncPeriodStats_(course, students, nextActive, dateKey) {
  try {
    const sheet = wdSheet_(WD_SHEETS.STATS_PERIOD, true);
    if (!sheet) return { ok: false, message: '일과통계(기간) 시트를 찾지 못했습니다.', updated: 0 };
    const data = wdGetStatsSheetData_(sheet);
    if (!data.display.length) return { ok: false, message: '일과통계(기간) 시트가 비어 있습니다.', updated: 0 };

    const cleanStudents = (students || []).filter(st => wdClean_(st && st.id) || wdClean_(st && st.name));
    const targets = {};
    let missed = [];

    cleanStudents.forEach(st => {
      const row = wdFindStatsStudentRow_(data.display, st);
      const col = row ? wdFindStatsPeriodCol_(data, row, dateKey, course && course.period) : 0;
      if (wdAddStatsTarget_(sheet, data, targets, row, col, !!nextActive)) return;

      // 통계표가 가로/세로 반대 구조인 경우까지 보조 처리합니다.
      const transposedCol = wdFindStatsStudentCol_(data.display, st);
      const transposedRow = transposedCol ? wdFindStatsPeriodRow_(data, transposedCol, dateKey, course && course.period) : 0;
      if (!wdAddStatsTarget_(sheet, data, targets, transposedRow, transposedCol, !!nextActive)) {
        missed.push([wdClean_(st.id), wdClean_(st.name)].filter(Boolean).join(' '));
      }
    });

    const a1List = Object.keys(targets);
    if (a1List.length) {
      const rangeList = sheet.getRangeList(a1List);
      if (nextActive) {
        rangeList.setValue(WD_STATS_MARK_TEXT);
        rangeList.setFontColor(WD_STATS_MARK_COLOR);
      } else {
        rangeList.clearContent();
        rangeList.setFontColor(WD_STATS_DEFAULT_COLOR);
      }
    }

    return { ok: true, updated: a1List.length, missed: missed };
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('일과통계(기간) 반영 실패: ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : err));
    return { ok: false, message: err && err.message ? err.message : String(err), updated: 0 };
  }
}

function wdCountCourseStudents_(course, rosterIndex, applicantMap, activeMap, dateKey) {
  let total = 0;
  let active = 0;
  const students = wdBuildStudentsForCourse_(course, rosterIndex, applicantMap, activeMap, dateKey);
  students.forEach(st => { total++; if (st.active) active++; });
  return { total: total, active: active };
}

function wdBuildStudentsForCourse_(course, rosterIndex, applicantMap, activeMap, dateKey) {
  rosterIndex = rosterIndex || wdGetSubjectRosterIndex_();
  applicantMap = applicantMap || wdGetApplicantMap_();
  activeMap = activeMap || wdGetAttendanceMapCached_(dateKey);
  if (!course || !course.rosterKey) return [];
  let base = [];
  if (course.specialFriday || wdIsFridayHomeroomCourse_(course)) {
    base = Object.keys(applicantMap).map(id => applicantMap[id]).filter(st => Number(st.classGroup) === Number(course.classGroup));
  } else {
    const rows = rosterIndex.byRosterKey[course.rosterKey] || [];
    const seen = {};
    base = rows.filter(st => applicantMap[st.studentId]).filter(st => {
      if (seen[st.studentId]) return false;
      seen[st.studentId] = true;
      return true;
    }).map(st => {
      const app = applicantMap[st.studentId];
      return Object.assign({}, app, { name: st.studentName || app.name });
    });
  }
  return base.sort(wdSortBySeat_).map(app => {
    const recordKey = wdMakeRecordKey_(dateKey, course.period, course.rosterKey, app.id);
    const att = activeMap[recordKey];
    return {
      id: app.id,
      name: app.name,
      seatType: app.seatType,
      seatNo: app.seatNo,
      seatKey: app.seatKey,
      classGroup: app.classGroup,
      active: !!(att && att.active),
      status: att && att.active ? WD_STATUS_PRESENT : WD_STATUS_ABSENT,
      dateKey: dateKey,
      period: Number(course.period),
      rosterKey: course.rosterKey,
      subject: course.subject,
      subjectKey: course.subjectKey,
      teacher: course.teacher,
      courseLabel: course.subject + ' ' + course.classGroup + '반'
    };
  });
}

function wdGetCourseStudents(request) {
  request = request || {};
  const user = request.user || {};
  const role = wdClean_(user.role);
  const actor = wdClean_(user.id);
  if (!role || !actor) return { ok: false, message: '다시 로그인하세요.' };
  const course = wdSanitizeCourse_(request.course);
  if (!course) return { ok: false, message: '수업 정보를 찾지 못했습니다.' };
  if (role !== 'admin' && !wdTeacherCanAccessCourse_(course, actor)) return { ok: false, message: '해당 수업 담당 교사가 아닙니다.' };
  const dateKey = wdDateKey_();
  const rosterIndex = wdGetSubjectRosterIndex_();
  const applicantMap = wdGetApplicantMap_();
  const activeMap = wdGetAttendanceMapCached_(dateKey);
  if (!course.rosterKey) course.rosterKey = wdFindRosterKeyForCourse_(course, rosterIndex) || (course.specialFriday ? wdHomeroomRosterKey_(course.classGroup) : wdMakeRosterKey_(course.teacher, course.subjectKey, course.classGroup));
  const students = wdBuildStudentsForCourse_(course, rosterIndex, applicantMap, activeMap, dateKey);
  return {
    ok: true,
    dateKey: dateKey,
    course: course,
    students: students,
    summary: { total: students.length, active: students.filter(s => s.active).length }
  };
}

function wdSanitizeCourse_(course) {
  course = course || {};
  const period = Number(course.period);
  const classGroup = Number(course.classGroup);
  const subject = wdClean_(course.subject);
  const teacher = wdClean_(course.teacher);
  if (!period || !classGroup || !subject || !teacher) return null;
  return {
    dateKey: wdClean_(course.dateKey) || wdDateKey_(),
    dayNo: Number(course.dayNo) || wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(wdDateKey_()),
    dayLabel: wdClean_(course.dayLabel),
    period: period,
    classGroup: classGroup,
    subject: subject,
    subjectKey: wdClean_(course.subjectKey) || wdNormalizeSubjectKey_(subject),
    teacher: teacher,
    rosterKey: wdClean_(course.rosterKey),
    courseKey: wdClean_(course.courseKey),
    specialFriday: !!course.specialFriday
  };
}

function wdFindStudentCourseForPeriod_(studentId, period, dateKey, courses, rosterIndex) {
  const appClass = wdClassGroupFromStudentId_(studentId);
  const dayNo = wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(dateKey);
  if (dayNo === 5 && WD_FRIDAY_HOMEROOM_PERIODS.indexOf(Number(period)) !== -1) {
    const teachers = wdGetHomeroomTeacherList_(appClass, dateKey);
    return {
      dateKey: dateKey,
      dayNo: 5,
      dayLabel: '금',
      period: Number(period),
      classGroup: Number(appClass),
      subject: '창체',
      subjectKey: wdNormalizeSubjectKey_('창체'),
      teacher: wdTeacherText_(teachers),
      rosterKey: wdHomeroomRosterKey_(appClass),
      specialFriday: true,
      courseLabel: '창체 ' + appClass + '반'
    };
  }
  const periodCourses = (courses || []).filter(c => Number(c.period) === Number(period));
  for (let i = 0; i < periodCourses.length; i++) {
    const c = periodCourses[i];
    if (!c.rosterKey) c.rosterKey = wdFindRosterKeyForCourse_(c, rosterIndex) || wdMakeRosterKey_(c.teacher, c.subjectKey, c.classGroup);
    const rows = (rosterIndex.byRosterKey[c.rosterKey] || []);
    if (rows.some(st => wdClean_(st.studentId) === wdClean_(studentId))) {
      c.courseLabel = c.subject + ' ' + c.classGroup + '반';
      return c;
    }
  }
  const classCourse = periodCourses.find(c => Number(c.classGroup) === Number(appClass));
  if (classCourse) {
    if (!classCourse.rosterKey) classCourse.rosterKey = wdFindRosterKeyForCourse_(classCourse, rosterIndex) || wdMakeRosterKey_(classCourse.teacher, classCourse.subjectKey, classCourse.classGroup);
    classCourse.courseLabel = classCourse.subject + ' ' + classCourse.classGroup + '반';
    return classCourse;
  }
  return null;
}

function wdGetAdminPeriodStatus(request) {
  request = request || {};
  const user = request.user || {};
  if (wdClean_(user.role) !== 'admin' || wdClean_(user.id) !== 'admin') return { ok: false, message: '관리자만 사용할 수 있습니다.' };
  const dateKey = wdDateKey_();
  const period = Number(request.period) || wdGetCurrentPeriod_(wdGetPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey));
  const ranges = wdGetPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey);
  const courses = wdGetEffectiveCoursesForDate_(dateKey).filter(c => Number(c.period) === period);
  const rosterIndex = wdGetSubjectRosterIndex_();
  const activeMap = wdGetAttendanceMapCached_(dateKey);
  const applicants = wdGetApplicantList_();
  const students = applicants.map(app => {
    const course = wdFindStudentCourseForPeriod_(app.id, period, dateKey, courses, rosterIndex);
    const recordKey = course ? wdMakeRecordKey_(dateKey, period, course.rosterKey, app.id) : '';
    const att = recordKey ? activeMap[recordKey] : null;
    return {
      id: app.id,
      name: app.name,
      seatType: app.seatType,
      seatNo: app.seatNo,
      seatKey: app.seatKey,
      classGroup: app.classGroup,
      active: !!(att && att.active),
      status: att && att.active ? WD_STATUS_PRESENT : WD_STATUS_ABSENT,
      dateKey: dateKey,
      period: period,
      rosterKey: course ? course.rosterKey : '',
      subject: course ? course.subject : '',
      subjectKey: course ? course.subjectKey : '',
      teacher: course ? course.teacher : '',
      courseLabel: course ? course.courseLabel || (course.subject + ' ' + course.classGroup + '반') : '',
      course: course || null
    };
  }).sort(wdSortBySeat_);
  return {
    ok: true,
    dateKey: dateKey,
    dayNo: wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(dateKey),
    dayLabel: WD_DAY_LABELS[wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(dateKey)] || '',
    period: period,
    startTime: ranges[period] ? ranges[period].start : '',
    endTime: ranges[period] ? ranges[period].end : '',
    students: students,
    summary: { total: students.length, active: students.filter(s => s.active).length }
  };
}

function wdTeacherToggleStudent(request) {
  request = request || {};
  const user = request.user || {};
  const role = wdClean_(user.role);
  const actor = wdClean_(user.id);
  const course = wdSanitizeCourse_(request.course);
  const student = request.student || {};
  const studentId = wdClean_(student.id);
  const studentName = wdClean_(student.name);
  const nextActive = !!request.nextActive;
  if (role !== 'teacher' || !actor) return { ok: false, message: '교사만 사용할 수 있습니다.' };
  if (!course || !studentId) return { ok: false, message: '처리할 학생을 찾지 못했습니다.' };
  if (!wdTeacherCanAccessCourse_(course, actor)) return { ok: false, message: '해당 수업 담당 교사가 아닙니다.' };
  return wdSetStudentStatus_(course, studentId, studentName, nextActive, actor, '교사');
}

function wdAdminSetStudent(request) {
  request = request || {};
  const user = request.user || {};
  const role = wdClean_(user.role);
  const actor = wdClean_(user.id);
  const course = wdSanitizeCourse_(request.course || (request.student && request.student.course));
  const student = request.student || {};
  const studentId = wdClean_(student.id);
  const studentName = wdClean_(student.name);
  const nextActive = wdClean_(request.action) === 'present' || wdClean_(request.status) === WD_STATUS_PRESENT || wdClean_(request.status) === WD_STATUS_WUNGJI_LEGACY;
  if (role !== 'admin' || actor !== 'admin') return { ok: false, message: '관리자만 사용할 수 있습니다.' };
  if (!course || !studentId) return { ok: false, message: '수업 정보를 찾지 못했습니다.' };
  return wdSetStudentStatus_(course, studentId, studentName, nextActive, 'admin', '관리자');
}

function wdBulkSetCourseStudents(request) {
  request = request || {};
  const user = request.user || {};
  const role = wdClean_(user.role);
  const actor = wdClean_(user.id);
  const course = wdSanitizeCourse_(request.course);
  if (role !== 'teacher' || !actor) return { ok: false, message: '교사만 사용할 수 있습니다.' };
  if (!course) return { ok: false, message: '수업 정보를 찾지 못했습니다.' };
  if (!wdTeacherCanAccessCourse_(course, actor)) return { ok: false, message: '해당 수업 담당 교사가 아닙니다.' };
  const list = wdGetCourseStudents({ user: user, course: course });
  if (!list.ok) return list;
  return wdSetManyStudentStatus_(list.course, list.students, true, actor, '교사일괄');
}

function wdSetStudentStatus_(course, studentId, studentName, nextActive, actor, processPrefix) {
  return wdSetManyStudentStatus_(course, [{ id: studentId, name: studentName }], nextActive, actor, processPrefix);
}

function wdSetManyStudentStatus_(course, students, nextActive, actor, processPrefix) {
  const list = (students || []).filter(st => wdClean_(st.id));
  if (!list.length) return { ok: true, status: nextActive ? WD_STATUS_PRESENT : WD_STATUS_ABSENT, active: !!nextActive, message: '처리할 학생이 없습니다.', count: 0 };

  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(30000)) throw new Error('처리가 몰려 저장이 지연되었습니다. 화면을 새로고침해 다시 확인하세요.');

  try {
    const date = wdNow_();
    const dateKey = wdDateKey_(date);
    const dayNo = wdGetEffectiveDayNoForDate_(dateKey);
    if (!course.rosterKey) course.rosterKey = course.specialFriday ? wdHomeroomRosterKey_(course.classGroup) : wdMakeRosterKey_(course.teacher, course.subjectKey, course.classGroup);

    const sheet = wdEnsureLogSheet_();
    const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
    const keyRows = {};
    if (lastRow >= 2) {
      const keys = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 1).getDisplayValues();
      keys.forEach((r, i) => {
        const k = wdClean_(r[0]);
        if (!k) return;
        if (!keyRows[k]) keyRows[k] = [];
        keyRows[k].push(i + 2);
      });
    }

    const rowsToAppend = [];
    let count = 0;
    const time = nextActive ? wdTimeKey_(date) : '';
    const status = nextActive ? WD_STATUS_PRESENT : WD_STATUS_ABSENT;
    const processText = (processPrefix || '') + (nextActive ? '웅지실:' : '취소:') + actor;

    list.forEach(st => {
      const studentId = wdClean_(st.id);
      const studentName = wdClean_(st.name);
      const recordKey = wdMakeRecordKey_(dateKey, course.period, course.rosterKey, studentId);
      const row = [
        recordKey,
        dateKey,
        WD_DAY_LABELS[dayNo] || course.dayLabel || '',
        Number(course.period),
        Number(course.classGroup),
        course.subject,
        course.subjectKey,
        course.teacher,
        course.rosterKey,
        studentId,
        studentName,
        time,
        status,
        processText
      ];
      const existing = keyRows[recordKey] || [];
      if (existing.length) {
        // 삭제하지 않고 같은 기록키의 모든 행을 같은 최종 상태로 덮어씁니다.
        // deleteRow가 잠금을 오래 잡아먹어 되돌림 현상이 생겼기 때문입니다.
        existing.forEach(rowNo => sheet.getRange(rowNo, 1, 1, WD_LOG_HEADERS.length).setValues([row]));
      } else if (nextActive) {
        rowsToAppend.push(row);
      }
      count++;
    });

    if (rowsToAppend.length) {
      sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, rowsToAppend.length, WD_LOG_HEADERS.length).setValues(rowsToAppend);
    }

    const statsSync = wdSyncPeriodStats_(course, list, nextActive, dateKey);

    wdClearAttendanceCache_(dateKey);

    return {
      ok: true,
      status: status,
      active: !!nextActive,
      message: nextActive ? '웅지실 처리' : '취소 처리',
      count: count,
      stats: statsSync
    };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

// v5부터는 취소 시 행을 삭제하지 않습니다.
// 기존 행의 로그인시간을 비우고 상태를 미로그인으로 바꿔, 기존 앱에서도 미처리로 읽히게 합니다.
function wdSetStudentStatusUnlocked_(course, studentId, studentName, nextActive, actor, processPrefix) {
  return wdSetManyStudentStatus_(course, [{ id: studentId, name: studentName }], nextActive, actor, processPrefix);
}

  <script>
    (function() {
      var busy = false;
      function normalizeStudentId(value) {
        return String(value == null ? '' : value)
          .replace(/[０-９]/g, function(ch) { return String(ch.charCodeAt(0) - 65248); })
          .replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
      }
      function setResult(html) {
        var el = document.getElementById('attendanceResult');
        if (el) el.innerHTML = html;
      }
      const STUDENT_DEVICE_LOCK_KEY = 'selfStudyStudentDeviceLockedId_v1';
      const WUNGJI_GPS_LAT = 37.6593055556;
      const WUNGJI_GPS_LNG = 126.6248333333;
      const WUNGJI_GPS_RADIUS_M = 30;
      function finish(button) {
        busy = false;
        if (button) button.disabled = false;
      }
      function getLockedStudentId() {
        try { return localStorage.getItem(STUDENT_DEVICE_LOCK_KEY) || ''; } catch (_) { return ''; }
      }
      function lockStudentId(id) {
        try { if (id) localStorage.setItem(STUDENT_DEVICE_LOCK_KEY, id); } catch (_) {}
      }
      function distanceMeters(lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2) {
        var R = 6371000;
        var toRad = Math.PI / 180;
        var dLat = (lat2 - lat1) * toRad;
        var dLon = (lon2 - lon1) * toRad;
        var a = Math.sin(dLat / 2) * Math.sin(dLat / 2) +
          Math.cos(lat1 * toRad) * Math.cos(lat2 * toRad) *
          Math.sin(dLon / 2) * Math.sin(dLon / 2);
        return R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1 - a));
      }
      function requestStudentGps(success, failure, outside) {
        var attempts = 0;
        function once() {
          attempts++;
          if (!navigator.geolocation) {
            if (attempts < 2) {
              setResult('<span class="text-primary">위치를 다시 확인하는 중입니다.<br>잠시만 기다려 주세요.</span>');
              setTimeout(once, 800);
            } else {
              failure({ code: 'unsupported' });
            }
            return;
          }
          navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function(pos) {
            var lat = Number(pos.coords && pos.coords.latitude);
            var lng = Number(pos.coords && pos.coords.longitude);
            if (!isFinite(lat) || !isFinite(lng)) {
              if (attempts < 2) {
                setResult('<span class="text-primary">위치를 다시 확인하는 중입니다.<br>잠시만 기다려 주세요.</span>');
                setTimeout(once, 800);
              } else {
                failure({ code: 'invalid' });
              }
              return;
            }
            var dist = distanceMeters(lat, lng, WUNGJI_GPS_LAT, WUNGJI_GPS_LNG);
            var gps = {
              lat: lat,
              lng: lng,
              accuracy: Math.round(Number((pos.coords && pos.coords.accuracy) || 0)),
              distance: Math.round(dist),
              radius: WUNGJI_GPS_RADIUS_M,
              checkedAt: Date.now()
            };
            if (dist <= WUNGJI_GPS_RADIUS_M) success(gps);
            else outside(gps);
          }, function(err) {
            if (attempts < 2) {
              setResult('<span class="text-primary">위치를 다시 확인하는 중입니다.<br>잠시만 기다려 주세요.</span>');
              setTimeout(once, 900);
            } else {
              failure(err || {});
            }
          }, { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 9000, maximumAge: 0 });
        }
        once();
      }
      window.submitAttendanceCompat = function(event) {
        if (event && event.preventDefault) event.preventDefault();
        if (busy) return false;
        var input = document.getElementById('studentId');
        var button = document.getElementById('submitAttendanceBtn');
        var id = normalizeStudentId(input ? input.value : '');
        if (input) input.value = id;
        if (!/^\d{4}$/.test(id)) {
          setResult('<span class="text-danger">학번 4자리를 정확히 입력해 주세요.</span>');
          return false;
        }
        var lockedId = getLockedStudentId();
        if (lockedId && lockedId !== id) {
          setResult('<span class="text-danger">이 기기에서는 이미 다른 학번으로 로그인했습니다.<br>담당 선생님께 말씀드리세요.</span>');
          return false;
        }
        var modeEl = document.querySelector('input[name="studentAttendanceMode"]:checked');
        var attendanceMode = modeEl ? modeEl.value : 'wungji';
        if (!(window.google && google.script && google.script.run)) {
          setResult('<span class="text-danger">현재 QR 앱의 내부 브라우저에서는 연결할 수 없습니다.<br><a href="' + location.href + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Safari 또는 Chrome에서 열기</a></span>');
          return false;
        }
        busy = true;
        if (button) button.disabled = true;
        setResult('<span class="text-primary">위치를 확인하고 있습니다...</span>');
        var tryNo = 0;
        function attempt(gpsPayload) {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(msg) {
              finish(button);
              var success = String(msg || '').indexOf('✅') >= 0;
              setResult('<span class="' + (success ? 'text-success' : 'text-danger') + '">' + String(msg || '') + '</span>');
              if (success) lockStudentId(id);
              if (success && input) input.value = id;
              try {
                if (success && typeof loadPublicTop10 === 'function') loadPublicTop10();
                if (success && typeof isAdminLoggedIn !== 'undefined' && isAdminLoggedIn && typeof adminMode !== 'undefined' && adminMode === 'class' && typeof isClassAdmin_ === 'function' && isClassAdmin_() && typeof loadCurrentWungjiStatus === 'function') loadCurrentWungjiStatus();
                if (success && typeof isAdminLoggedIn !== 'undefined' && isAdminLoggedIn && typeof adminMode !== 'undefined' && adminMode === 'class' && typeof selectedWungjiCourse !== 'undefined' && selectedWungjiCourse && typeof refreshSelectedClassAttendance === 'function') refreshSelectedClassAttendance();
              } catch (_) {}
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
              var message = error && error.message ? error.message : String(error || '처리 오류');
              var transient = /동시|too many|혼잡|대기|Service invoked|Exceeded maximum|잠시 후/i.test(message);
              if (transient && tryNo < 3) {
                tryNo++;
                setResult('<span class="text-primary">접속이 몰려 자동으로 다시 시도하고 있습니다...</span>');
                setTimeout(function() { attempt(gpsPayload); }, 800 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 900) + tryNo * 500);
                return;
              }
              finish(button);
              setResult('<span class="text-danger">출석 처리에 실패했습니다.<br>Safari 또는 Chrome에서 다시 열어 주세요.</span>');
            })
            .processAttendanceById(id, attendanceMode, gpsPayload);
        }
        requestStudentGps(function(gpsPayload) {
          setResult('<span class="text-primary">출석을 처리하고 있습니다...</span>');
          attempt(gpsPayload);
        }, function() {
          finish(button);
          setResult('<span class="text-danger">위치 확인 실패했습니다.<br>담당 선생님께 말씀드리세요.</span>');
        }, function() {
          finish(button);
          setResult('<span class="text-danger">지정된 장소에서만 출석할 수 있습니다.<br>담당 선생님께 말씀드리세요.</span>');
        });
        return false;
      };
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        var form = document.getElementById('attendanceForm');
        var input = document.getElementById('studentId');
        if (form) form.onsubmit = window.submitAttendanceCompat;
        if (input) {
          input.oninput = function() { this.value = normalizeStudentId(this.value).slice(0, 4); };
          var savedStudentId = getLockedStudentId();
          if (savedStudentId && !input.value) input.value = savedStudentId;
        }
      });
    })();
  </script>

  <script defer src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/xlsx@0.18.5/dist/xlsx.full.min.js"></script>

        const mm = rawValue.substring(2, 4);
        if (parseInt(hh, 10) > 23 || parseInt(mm, 10) > 59) {
          showMessage('올바른 시간이 아닙니다. (00~23시, 00~59분)');

      });

    function getTodayFormatted() {
      const now = new Date();
      const month = String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
      const date = String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
      const days = ['일', '월', '화', '수', '목', '금', '토'];
      return `${month}/${date}(${days[now.getDay()]})`;
    }


    function formatClassDateShort_(dateKey) {
      const date = dateKey ? new Date(String(dateKey) + 'T12:00:00') : new Date();
      const month = String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
      const day = String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
      const days = ['일', '월', '화', '수', '목', '금', '토'];
      return `${month}/${day}(${days[date.getDay()]})`;
    }

    function getClassSeatOrder_(row) {
      const seat = String(row && (row.seatKey || row.seat || '') || '');
      const openMatch = seat.match(/^개방\s*(\d+)/);
      if (openMatch) return Number(openMatch[1] || 0);
      const closedMatch = seat.match(/^폐쇄\s*(\d+)/);
      if (closedMatch) return 1000 + Number(closedMatch[1] || 0);
      const type = String(row && row.seatType || '');
      const num = Number(row && row.seatNumber || 999);
      if (type.indexOf('개방') >= 0) return num;
      if (type.indexOf('폐쇄') >= 0) return 1000 + num;
      return 9999;
    }

    function sortClassRowsBySeat_(rows) {
      return (rows || []).slice().sort((a, b) => {
        const ao = getClassSeatOrder_(a);
        const bo = getClassSeatOrder_(b);
        if (ao !== bo) return ao - bo;
        return String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''), 'ko', { numeric:true });
      });
    }

    function showMessage(message) {
      document.getElementById('messageModalBody').innerText = message;
      messageModal.show();
    }

    function escapeHtml(value) {
      return String(value == null ? '' : value)
        .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
        .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
        .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
        .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
        .replace(/'/g, '&#039;');
    }

    function showConfirm(message, callback) {
      document.getElementById('confirmModalBody').innerText = message;
      confirmCallback = callback;
      confirmModal.show();
    }

    function showTimeInput(title, defaultValue, callback, okLabel, returnRaw4) {
      document.getElementById('timeInputTitle').innerText = title;
      const input = document.getElementById('manualTimeInput');
      input.value = defaultValue || '0800';
      document.getElementById('timeInputOkBtn').innerText = okLabel || '적용';
      timeInputReturnRaw4 = !!returnRaw4;
      timeInputCallback = callback;
      timeInputModal.show();
      setTimeout(function() {
        input.focus();
        input.select();
      }, 200);
    }


        function showTimeSelect(callback, t1State, t2State) {
      document.getElementById('timeSelectTitle').innerText = '학생 출석 상황을 변경합니다.';
      document.querySelectorAll('input[name="timeSelect1State"], input[name="timeSelect2State"]').forEach(function(el) {
        el.checked = false;
      });

      const t1Default = ['present', 'late'].includes(String(t1State || '')) ? 'present' : 'absent';
      const t2Default = ['present', 'late'].includes(String(t2State || '')) ? 'present' : 'absent';
      const t1Target = document.querySelector('input[name="timeSelect1State"][value="' + t1Default + '"]');
      const t2Target = document.querySelector('input[name="timeSelect2State"][value="' + t2Default + '"]');
      if (t1Target) t1Target.checked = true;
      if (t2Target) t2Target.checked = true;

      timeSelectCallback = callback;
      timeSelectModal.show();
    }

    function readAttendanceInputs() {
      const raw = document.getElementById('studentId').value;
      const id = String(raw == null ? '' : raw).replace(/[０-９]/g, ch => String(ch.charCodeAt(0) - 65248)).replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
      return { id: id };
    }

    function submitAttendance(event) {
      return window.submitAttendanceCompat ? window.submitAttendanceCompat(event) : false;
    }

    function createSeat(seatName) {
      if (adminMode === 'night') {
        return `
          <div class="seat-box night-half-seat" id="seat-${seatName}" style="cursor:pointer;">
            <div class="night-seat-halves">
              <div class="night-half left night-state-empty" id="seat-${seatName}-t1"></div>
              <div class="night-half right night-state-empty" id="seat-${seatName}-t2"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="seat-label">${seatName}</div>
            <div class="seat-name" id="name-${seatName}">-</div>
            <div class="night-seat-time" id="time-${seatName}"></div>
          </div>
        `;
      }

      return `
        <div class="seat-box" id="seat-${seatName}" style="cursor:pointer;">
          <div class="seat-label">${seatName}</div>
          <div class="seat-name" id="name-${seatName}">-</div>
        </div>
      `;
    }

    function renderSeatingLayout() {
      if (seatingLayoutRendered) return;

      const area = document.getElementById('seatingChartArea');
      let html = `<div class="room-container">`;

      html += `<div class="open-section">`;
      for (let b = 0; b < 3; b++) {
        html += `<div class="open-block">`;
        for (let c = 1; c <= 4; c++) html += createSeat(`개방${b * 8 + c}`);
        for (let c = 5; c <= 8; c++) html += createSeat(`개방${b * 8 + c}`);
        html += `</div>`;
      }
      html += `</div>`;

      html += `<div class="center-aisle">중앙복도</div>`;
      html += `<div class="closed-section">`;
      html += `<div class="closed-block">`;
      for (let r = 0; r < 9; r++) {
        html += createSeat(`폐쇄${28 + r}`);
        html += createSeat(`폐쇄${19 + r}`);
      }
      html += `</div>`;
      html += `<div class="closed-block">`;
      for (let r = 0; r < 9; r++) {
        html += createSeat(`폐쇄${10 + r}`);
        html += createSeat(`폐쇄${1 + r}`);
      }
      html += `</div>`;
      html += `</div>`;
      html += `</div>`;

      area.innerHTML = html;
      seatingLayoutRendered = true;
      
      // 도면이 완전히 그려진 후 스크롤바 세팅 계산
      setTimeout(refreshHorizontalScrollbars, 100);
    }

    function confirmCancelAttendance(id, name) {
      if (!isAdminLoggedIn) return;

      if (adminMode === 'night') {
        promptManualAttendance(id, name);
        return;
      }

      showConfirm('출석을 취소하시겠습니까?', function() {
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
            showMessage(result);
