            manualRefreshSeating();
            loadCumulativeStatus();
            loadPublicTop10();
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
            showMessage('오류가 발생했습니다: ' + error.message);
          })
          .cancelAttendance(id, name);
      });
    }

        function promptManualAttendance(id, name, t1State, t2State) {
      if (adminMode === 'night') {
        showTimeSelect(function(selection) {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
              showMessage(result);
              manualRefreshSeating();
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
              showMessage('오류 발생: ' + error.message);
            })
            .updateNightAttendanceState(id, name, selection.t1, selection.t2);
        }, t1State, t2State);
        return;
      }

      showTimeInput(`${name} 학생의 수동 입실 시간을 입력하세요.`, '0800', function(timeStr) {
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
            showMessage(result);
            manualRefreshSeating();
            loadCumulativeStatus();
            loadPublicTop10();
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
            showMessage('오류 발생: ' + error.message);
          })
          .adminProcessAttendance(id, name, timeStr);
      });
    }


    function isGrade2StudentId_(id) {
      return String(id == null ? '' : id).trim().startsWith('2');
    }

    function applyGrade2NameColor_(nameEl, id) {
      if (!nameEl) return;
      const isGrade2 = isGrade2StudentId_(id);
      nameEl.classList.toggle('grade2-name', isGrade2);
      if (isGrade2) {
        nameEl.style.setProperty('color', '#2957ff', 'important');
      } else {
        nameEl.style.removeProperty('color');
      }
    }

    function grade2NameClass_(id) {
      return isGrade2StudentId_(id) ? ' grade2-name' : '';
    }

    function updateSeatingData() {
      if (adminMode === 'night') {
        updateNightSeatingData();
        return;
      }

      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
        if (!data) return;

        let totalStudents = 0;
        let presentStudents = 0;

        data.forEach(function(student) {
          if (!student.seat) return;
          if (student.name && String(student.name).trim() !== '') {
            totalStudents++;
            if (student.status === '입실') presentStudents++;
          }

          const seatEl = document.getElementById(`seat-${student.seat}`);
          const nameEl = document.getElementById(`name-${student.seat}`);
          if (!seatEl || !nameEl) return;

          nameEl.innerText = student.name || '-';
          applyGrade2NameColor_(nameEl, student.id);
          seatEl.classList.remove('seat-occupied', 'seat-special');
          seatEl.onclick = null;

          // 야간자기주도학습에서는 스페셜 좌석 빨간 글씨를 적용하지 않습니다.

          if (student.status === '입실') {
            seatEl.classList.add('seat-occupied');
            seatEl.onclick = function() { confirmCancelAttendance(student.id, student.name); };
          } else if (student.name && isAdminLoggedIn) {
            seatEl.onclick = function() { promptManualAttendance(student.id, student.name); };
          }
        });

        document.getElementById('seatingDateText').innerText = `${getTodayFormatted()} 자투리 현황`;
        document.getElementById('seatingCountText').innerText = `${presentStudents}명 / ${totalStudents}명`;
      }).getAllStatus();
    }


    function updateNightSeatingData() {
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
        if (!data) return;

        let totalStudents = 0;
        let t1Present = 0;
        let t2Present = 0;

        data.forEach(function(student) {
          if (!student.seat) return;

          const seatEl = document.getElementById(`seat-${student.seat}`);
          const nameEl = document.getElementById(`name-${student.seat}`);
          const timeEl = document.getElementById(`time-${student.seat}`);
          const t1El = document.getElementById(`seat-${student.seat}-t1`);
          const t2El = document.getElementById(`seat-${student.seat}-t2`);
          if (!seatEl || !nameEl || !t1El || !t2El) return;

          nameEl.innerText = student.name || '-';
          applyGrade2NameColor_(nameEl, student.id);

          const t1Time = student.t1 && student.t1.time ? student.t1.time : '';
          const t2Time = student.t2 && student.t2.time ? student.t2.time : '';
          let timeText = '';
          if (t1Time && t2Time && t1Time !== t2Time) timeText = `1타임 ${t1Time} / 2타임 ${t2Time}`;
          else if (t1Time || t2Time) timeText = t1Time || t2Time;
          if (timeEl) timeEl.innerText = timeText;

          seatEl.classList.remove('seat-occupied', 'seat-special');
          seatEl.onclick = null;
          seatEl.oncontextmenu = null;
          seatEl.title = '';

          const states = ['empty', 'off', 'absent', 'present', 'late', 'extra', 'early'];
          states.forEach(function(s) {
            t1El.classList.remove('night-state-' + s);
            t2El.classList.remove('night-state-' + s);
          });

          const t1State = student.t1 && student.t1.state ? student.t1.state : 'off';
          const t2State = student.t2 && student.t2.state ? student.t2.state : 'off';
          t1El.classList.add('night-state-' + t1State);
          t2El.classList.add('night-state-' + t2State);

          const isT1CountTarget = !['off'].includes(t1State);
          const isT2CountTarget = !['off'].includes(t2State);

          if (student.name && String(student.name).trim() !== '' && (isT1CountTarget || isT2CountTarget)) {
            totalStudents++;
          }

          if (t1State === 'present' || t1State === 'late') t1Present++;
          if (t2State === 'present' || t2State === 'late') t2Present++;

          if (student.name && isAdminLoggedIn) {
            seatEl.onclick = function() { promptManualAttendance(student.id, student.name, t1State, t2State); };
            seatEl.oncontextmenu = function(e) {
              e.preventDefault();
              promptManualAttendance(student.id, student.name, t1State, t2State);
              return false;
            };
            seatEl.title = '탭: 출석 상황 수정';
          }
        });

        document.getElementById('seatingDateText').innerHTML = `<span class="night-title-line">${getTodayFormatted()} 야간자율학습 현황</span>`;
        document.getElementById('seatingCountText').innerHTML = `<span class="night-count-line">1타임 ${t1Present}명 / 2타임 ${t2Present}명</span>`;

        if (!document.getElementById('nightLegend')) {
          const wrapper = document.getElementById('seatingMapWrapper');
          const legend = document.createElement('div');
          legend.id = 'nightLegend';
          legend.className = 'night-legend';
          legend.innerHTML = `
            <span class="night-legend-item"><span class="night-legend-color night-state-present"></span>출석</span>
            <span class="night-legend-item"><span class="night-legend-color night-state-absent"></span>미출석</span>
            <span class="night-legend-item"><span class="night-legend-color night-state-late"></span>지각</span>
            <span class="night-legend-item"><span class="night-legend-color night-state-off"></span>미신청</span>
          `;
          wrapper.parentElement.appendChild(legend);
        }
      }).getNightStatus();
    }

    function loadNightAbsenceStatus() {
      if (!isAdminLoggedIn || adminMode !== 'night') return;
      const titleEl = document.getElementById('nightAbsenceTitleText');
      if (titleEl) titleEl.innerText = `${getTodayFormatted()} 미출결 현황`;
      const body = document.getElementById('nightAbsenceBody');
      const countText = document.getElementById('nightAbsenceCountText');
      body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty">데이터 계산 중...</td></tr>';
      if (countText) countText.innerHTML = '<span class="night-count-line">미출결 인원 계산 중...</span>';

      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(rows) {
          rows = rows || [];
          const uniqueIds = new Set(rows.map(function(r) { return String(r.id || '').trim(); }).filter(Boolean));
          if (countText) countText.innerHTML = `<span class="night-count-line">미출결 인원 ${uniqueIds.size}명</span>`;

          if (rows.length === 0) {
            body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty">미출결 학생이 없습니다.</td></tr>';
            return;
          }

          const sortedRows = [...rows].sort(function(a, b) {
            const idCompare = String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true });
            if (idCompare !== 0) return idCompare;
            return String(a.seat || '').localeCompare(String(b.seat || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true });
          });

          body.innerHTML = sortedRows.map(function(r) {
            return `<tr>
              <td>${escapeHtml(r.seat)}</td>
              <td>${escapeHtml(r.id)}</td>
              <td><strong class="${grade2NameClass_(r.id).trim()}">${escapeHtml(r.name)}</strong></td>
              <td class="text-danger fw-bold night-absence-date">${escapeHtml(r.dateTime)}</td>
            </tr>`;
          }).join('');
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
          if (countText) countText.innerText = '미출결 인원 계산 실패';
          body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty">데이터를 불러오지 못했습니다.</td></tr>';
        })
        .getNightAbsenceStatus();
    }



    function loadNightSupervisorSchedule(forceReload) {
      const panel = document.getElementById('nightSupervisorPanel');
      const head = document.getElementById('nightSupervisorHead');
      const body = document.getElementById('nightSupervisorBody');
      if (!panel || !head || !body) return;
      if (!isAdminLoggedIn || adminMode !== 'night') return;
      if (supervisorScheduleLoaded && !forceReload) return;

      head.innerHTML = `
        <tr>
          <th class="night-supervisor-row-label">구분</th>
          <th>확인 중</th>
        </tr>
      `;
      body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="2" class="muted-empty">확인 중입니다.</td></tr>';

      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
          supervisorScheduleLoaded = true;

          if (!res || res.ok === false) {
            head.innerHTML = `
              <tr>
                <th class="night-supervisor-row-label">구분</th>
                <th>불러오기 실패</th>
              </tr>
            `;
            body.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="2" class="muted-empty">${escapeHtml((res && res.message) || '감독 일정 정보를 불러오지 못했습니다.')}</td></tr>`;
            return;
          }

          const items = res.items || [];
          if (!items.length) {
            head.innerHTML = `
              <tr>
                <th class="night-supervisor-row-label">구분</th>
                <th>일정 없음</th>
              </tr>
            `;
            body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="2" class="muted-empty">표시할 일정이 없습니다.</td></tr>';
            return;
          }

          head.innerHTML = `
            <tr>
              <th class="night-supervisor-row-label">구분</th>
              ${items.map(item => `<th>${escapeHtml(item.date)}</th>`).join('')}
            </tr>
          `;

          body.innerHTML = `
            <tr>
              <th class="night-supervisor-row-label">총괄</th>
              ${items.map(item => `<td><span class="night-supervisor-name">${escapeHtml(item.general || '없음')}</span></td>`).join('')}
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <th class="night-supervisor-row-label">3학년</th>
              ${items.map(item => {
                const value = item.grade3 || '없음';
                const cls = value === '없음' ? 'night-supervisor-empty' : 'night-supervisor-name';
                return `<td><span class="${cls}">${escapeHtml(value)}</span></td>`;
              }).join('')}
            </tr>
          `;
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
          head.innerHTML = `
            <tr>
              <th class="night-supervisor-row-label">구분</th>
              <th>오류</th>
            </tr>
          `;
          body.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="2" class="muted-empty">감독 일정 오류: ${escapeHtml(err && err.message ? err.message : err)}</td></tr>`;
        })
        .getNightSupervisorSchedule();
    }

    function manualRefreshSeating() {
      document.getElementById('seatingCountText').innerText = '새로고침 중...';
      updateSeatingData();
      if (adminMode === 'night') {
        loadNightAbsenceStatus();
      }
    }

    // 📌 스크롤바 동기화 로직 (오류 수정됨)
    function setupLinkedScrollbar(contentEl, sliderEl) {
      if (!contentEl || !sliderEl) return;

      const updateSliderRange = () => {
        const max = Math.max(0, contentEl.scrollWidth - contentEl.clientWidth);
        sliderEl.max = max;

        if (sliderEl.id === 'seatingScrollbar' && adminMode === 'jaturi' && max > 0 && !contentEl.dataset.jaturiScrollbarPositioned) {
          const aisle = contentEl.querySelector('.center-aisle');
          const target = aisle
            ? Math.round(aisle.offsetLeft + (aisle.offsetWidth / 2) - (contentEl.clientWidth / 2))
            : Math.round(max * 0.5);
          const clampedTarget = Math.max(0, Math.min(max, target));
          contentEl.scrollLeft = clampedTarget;
          sliderEl.value = clampedTarget;
          contentEl.dataset.jaturiScrollbarPositioned = 'true';
        } else if (sliderEl.id === 'seatingScrollbar' && adminMode === 'night' && max > 0 && !contentEl.dataset.nightScrollbarPositioned) {
          const target = Math.round(max * 0.5);
          contentEl.scrollLeft = target;
          sliderEl.value = target;
          contentEl.dataset.nightScrollbarPositioned = 'true';
        } else {
          sliderEl.value = Math.min(Number(sliderEl.value || 0), max);
        }

        sliderEl.style.display = max > 0 ? 'block' : 'none';
      };

      if (!contentEl.dataset.scrollLinked) {
        contentEl.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
          sliderEl.value = contentEl.scrollLeft;
        });
        sliderEl.addEventListener('input', function() {
          contentEl.scrollLeft = Number(sliderEl.value || 0);
        });
        contentEl.dataset.scrollLinked = 'true';
      }

      if (!contentEl.dataset.dragScrollLinked) {
        let isDown = false;
        let startX = 0;
        let startScrollLeft = 0;
        let moved = false;

        contentEl.addEventListener('pointerdown', function(e) {
          if (e.pointerType === 'mouse' && e.button !== 0) return;
          isDown = true;
          moved = false;
          startX = e.clientX;
          startScrollLeft = contentEl.scrollLeft;
          contentEl.dataset.draggingScroll = 'false';
          contentEl.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
        });

        contentEl.addEventListener('pointermove', function(e) {
          if (!isDown) return;
          const dx = e.clientX - startX;
          if (Math.abs(dx) > 5) {
            moved = true;
            contentEl.dataset.draggingScroll = 'true';
            contentEl.scrollLeft = startScrollLeft - dx;
            sliderEl.value = contentEl.scrollLeft;
            e.preventDefault();
          }
        });

        const finishDrag = function(e) {
          if (!isDown) return;
          isDown = false;
          try { contentEl.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId); } catch (_) {}
          setTimeout(function() {
            contentEl.dataset.draggingScroll = 'false';
          }, moved ? 80 : 0);
        };

        contentEl.addEventListener('pointerup', finishDrag);
        contentEl.addEventListener('pointercancel', finishDrag);

        contentEl.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
          if (contentEl.dataset.draggingScroll === 'true') {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
          }
        }, true);

        contentEl.dataset.dragScrollLinked = 'true';
      }

      updateSliderRange();
    }

    function refreshHorizontalScrollbars() {
      // DOM이 안정화된 후 계산하도록 딜레이 추가
      setTimeout(() => {
        setupLinkedScrollbar(document.getElementById('seatingMapWrapper'), document.getElementById('seatingScrollbar'));
        setupLinkedScrollbar(document.getElementById('cumulativeTableWrapper'), document.getElementById('cumulativeScrollbar'));
      }, 150);
    }


    function isClassAdmin_() {
      return currentIntegratedUser && currentIntegratedUser.role === 'admin';
    }

    function updateAdminLogoutButton_() {
      const btn = document.getElementById('adminLogoutBtn');
      if (!btn) return;
      const show = !!isAdminLoggedIn;
      btn.style.display = show ? 'inline-flex' : 'none';
      btn.classList.toggle('admin-hidden', !show);
    }

    function adminLogout() {
      if (autoRefreshTimer) {
        clearInterval(autoRefreshTimer);
        autoRefreshTimer = null;
      }
      isAdminLoggedIn = false;
      currentIntegratedUser = null;
      currentIntegratedPassword = '';
      selectedWungjiCourse = null;
      classUploadAnalyses = [];
      classAttendanceActionMap = {};
      supervisorScheduleLoaded = false;
      adminMode = 'jaturi';
      try { wdDayWungjiReset_(); } catch (_) {}

      const loginSection = document.getElementById('adminLoginSection');
      const dashboardSection = document.getElementById('adminDashboardSection');
      const loginResult = document.getElementById('adminLoginResult');
      const adminPw = document.getElementById('adminPw');
      const floatingModeSwitchBtn = document.getElementById('floatingModeSwitchBtn');
      if (loginSection) loginSection.style.display = 'block';
      if (dashboardSection) dashboardSection.style.display = 'none';
      if (loginResult) loginResult.innerText = '';
      if (adminPw) adminPw.value = '';
      if (floatingModeSwitchBtn) floatingModeSwitchBtn.style.display = 'none';
      updateAdminLogoutButton_();

      const adminTab = document.getElementById('admin-tab');
      if (adminTab) {
        try {
          if (window.bootstrap && bootstrap.Tab) new bootstrap.Tab(adminTab).show();
          else adminTab.click();
        } catch (_) {
          adminTab.click();
        }
      }
      window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
    }

    function setAdminModeUi_() {
      const floatingModeSwitchBtn = document.getElementById('floatingModeSwitchBtn');
      const legacyPanels = document.getElementById('legacyDashboardPanels');
      const classPanel = document.getElementById('classDashboardPanel');
      const isClass = adminMode === 'class';
      if (legacyPanels) legacyPanels.style.display = isClass ? 'none' : 'block';
      if (classPanel) classPanel.style.display = isClass ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (floatingModeSwitchBtn) {
        const nextText = adminMode === 'jaturi' ? '일과 중으로 이동' : adminMode === 'class' ? '야간자습으로 이동' : '자투리로 이동';
        floatingModeSwitchBtn.innerText = nextText;
        floatingModeSwitchBtn.style.display = isAdminLoggedIn ? 'block' : 'none';
      }
      updateAdminLogoutButton_();
      if (isClass) {
        const adminTeacherRow = document.getElementById('classAdminTeacherRow');
        const adminSettings = document.getElementById('classAdminSettingsPanel');
        const classLiveStatusPanel = document.getElementById('classLiveStatusPanel');
        const classScheduleTitle = document.getElementById('classScheduleTitle');
        const isAdmin = isClassAdmin_();
        if (adminTeacherRow) adminTeacherRow.style.display = isAdmin ? 'block' : 'none';
        if (adminSettings) adminSettings.style.display = isAdmin ? 'block' : 'none';
        if (classLiveStatusPanel) {
          classLiveStatusPanel.style.display = isAdmin ? 'block' : 'none';
          classLiveStatusPanel.hidden = !isAdmin;
          classLiveStatusPanel.classList.toggle('admin-hidden', !isAdmin);
        }
        if (classScheduleTitle) classScheduleTitle.innerText = isAdmin ? '오늘 시간표' : '내 시간표';
        return;
      }
      if (adminMode === 'night') {
        document.getElementById('seatingDateText').innerHTML = `<span class="night-title-line">${getTodayFormatted()} 야간자율학습 현황</span>`;
        document.getElementById('seatingCountText').innerHTML = `<span class="night-count-line">1타임 0명 / 2타임 0명</span>`;
        const nightAbsenceTitleEl = document.getElementById('nightAbsenceTitleText');
        if (nightAbsenceTitleEl) nightAbsenceTitleEl.innerText = `${getTodayFormatted()} 미출결 현황`;
      } else {
        document.getElementById('seatingDateText').innerText = `${getTodayFormatted()} 자투리 현황`;
        document.getElementById('seatingCountText').innerText = '(데이터 확인 중...)';
      }
      document.getElementById('jaturiRankPanels').style.display = adminMode === 'night' ? 'none' : '';
      document.getElementById('nightAbsencePanel').style.display = adminMode === 'night' ? 'block' : 'none';
      const nightSupervisorPanel = document.getElementById('nightSupervisorPanel');
      if (nightSupervisorPanel) nightSupervisorPanel.style.display = adminMode === 'night' ? 'block' : 'none';
      const cumulativePanel = document.getElementById('cumulativePanel');
      if (cumulativePanel) cumulativePanel.style.display = adminMode === 'night' ? 'none' : '';
    }

    function resetSeatingAreaForMode_() {
      seatingLayoutRendered = false;
      document.getElementById('seatingChartArea').innerHTML = '';
      const legend = document.getElementById('nightLegend');
      if (legend) legend.remove();
      const mapWrapper = document.getElementById('seatingMapWrapper');
      if (mapWrapper) {
        delete mapWrapper.dataset.nightCentered;
        delete mapWrapper.dataset.jaturiScrollbarPositioned;
        delete mapWrapper.dataset.nightScrollbarPositioned;
        mapWrapper.scrollLeft = 0;
      }
      const scrollbar = document.getElementById('seatingScrollbar');
      if (scrollbar) scrollbar.value = 0;
    }

    function startAdminAutoRefresh_() {
      if (autoRefreshTimer) return;
      autoRefreshTimer = setInterval(function() {
        if (adminMode === 'class') {
          wdDayWungjiRefresh_();
        } else {
          updateSeatingData();
          if (adminMode === 'night') loadNightAbsenceStatus();
          else loadPublicTop10();
        }
      }, 300000);
    }

    function switchAdminMode() {
      if (!isAdminLoggedIn) return;
      adminMode = adminMode === 'jaturi' ? 'class' : adminMode === 'class' ? 'night' : 'jaturi';
      setAdminModeUi_();
      if (adminMode === 'class') {
        wdDayWungjiEnterFromIntegratedLogin_(currentIntegratedUser);
        return;
      }
      resetSeatingAreaForMode_();
      renderSeatingLayout();
      updateSeatingData();
      if (adminMode === 'night') {
        loadNightSupervisorSchedule();
        loadNightAbsenceStatus();
      } else {
        loadCumulativeStatus();
        loadPublicTop10();
      }
    }

    function adminLogin(mode) {
      const userId = document.getElementById('adminId').value.trim();
      const pw = document.getElementById('adminPw').value;
      adminMode = mode || 'jaturi';
      const resultDiv = document.getElementById('adminLoginResult');
      const dateEl = document.getElementById('classScheduleDate');
      const loginDateKey = dateEl ? (dateEl.value || toLocalDateKey_(new Date())) : toLocalDateKey_(new Date());
      if (dateEl && !dateEl.value) dateEl.value = loginDateKey;
      resultDiv.innerText = '확인 중...';
      const success = function(auth, initialSchedule) {
        if (!auth || !auth.ok) {
          resultDiv.innerText = '❌ ' + (auth && auth.message ? auth.message : '로그인에 실패했습니다.');
          return;
        }
        currentIntegratedUser = auth;
        currentIntegratedPassword = pw;
        try { if (userId) localStorage.setItem(ADMIN_LOGIN_ID_KEY, userId); } catch (_) {}
        isAdminLoggedIn = true;
        document.getElementById('adminLoginSection').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('adminDashboardSection').style.display = 'block';
        setAdminModeUi_();
        startAdminAutoRefresh_();
        if (adminMode === 'class') {
          wdDayWungjiEnterFromIntegratedLogin_(auth);
          return;
        }
        resetSeatingAreaForMode_();
        renderSeatingLayout();
        updateSeatingData();
        if (adminMode === 'night') {
          loadNightSupervisorSchedule();
          loadNightAbsenceStatus();
        } else {
          loadCumulativeStatus();
        }
        if (!autoRefreshTimer) autoRefreshTimer = setInterval(function() {
          if (adminMode === 'class') {
            wdDayWungjiRefresh_();
          } else {
            updateSeatingData();
            if (adminMode === 'night') loadNightAbsenceStatus();
            else loadPublicTop10();
          }
        }, 300000);
      };
      if (adminMode === 'class') {
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(bundle) {
          if (!bundle || !bundle.ok) {
            const auth = bundle && bundle.auth ? bundle.auth : { ok:false, message:'로그인에 실패했습니다.' };
            success(auth, null);
            return;
          }
          success(bundle.auth, bundle.schedule || null);
        }).withFailureHandler(function(error) {
          resultDiv.innerText = '❌ ' + (error && error.message ? error.message : '로그인에 실패했습니다.');
        }).loginIntegratedFast(userId, pw, adminMode, loginDateKey, '');
      } else {
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(auth) { success(auth, null); })
          .withFailureHandler(function(error) { resultDiv.innerText = '❌ ' + (error && error.message ? error.message : '로그인에 실패했습니다.'); })
          .authenticateIntegratedUser(userId, pw, adminMode);
      }
    }


    const wdDayState_ = {
      user:null,
      selectedCourse:null,
      teacherStudents:[],
      adminPeriod:null,
      adminStudents:[],
      modalStudent:null,
      writeQueue:Promise.resolve(),
      writeVersion:{}
    };

    function wdDayWungjiReset_() {
      wdDayState_.user = null;
      wdDayState_.selectedCourse = null;
      wdDayState_.teacherStudents = [];
      wdDayState_.adminStudents = [];
      wdDayState_.modalStudent = null;
      wdDayState_.writeQueue = Promise.resolve();
      wdDayState_.writeVersion = {};
      wdDayWungjiShowScreen_('wdLoadingScreen');
      const loading = document.getElementById('wdLoadingText');
      if (loading) loading.textContent = '로그인 정보를 확인하고 있습니다.';
      wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdTeacherSeatMap', [], 'teacher');
      wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdAdminSeatMap', [], 'admin');
    }

    function wdDayWungjiCallGas_(fn, ...args) {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(resolve).withFailureHandler(reject)[fn](...args);
      });
    }

    function wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(value) {
      return String(value == null ? '' : value)
        .replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;')
        .replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/'/g,'&#039;');
    }

    function wdDayWungjiShowScreen_(id) {
      document.querySelectorAll('#wdApp .wdScreen').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('wdActive'));
      const target = document.getElementById(id);
      if (target) target.classList.add('wdActive');
    }

    function wdDayWungjiShowToast_(message) {
      const el = document.getElementById('wdToast');
      if (!el) return;
      el.textContent = message || '';
      el.classList.add('wdActiveToast');
      clearTimeout(wdDayWungjiShowToast_.timer);
      wdDayWungjiShowToast_.timer = setTimeout(() => el.classList.remove('wdActiveToast'), 1600);
    }

    function wdDayWungjiEnqueueWrite_(task) {
      const run = wdDayState_.writeQueue.then(task, task);
      wdDayState_.writeQueue = run.catch(() => {});
      return run;
    }

    function wdDayWungjiNextWriteVersion_(key) {
      const k = String(key || '');
      wdDayState_.writeVersion[k] = (wdDayState_.writeVersion[k] || 0) + 1;
      return wdDayState_.writeVersion[k];
    }

    function wdDayWungjiCurrentWriteVersion_(key) {
      return wdDayState_.writeVersion[String(key || '')] || 0;
    }

    async function wdDayWungjiEnterFromIntegratedLogin_(auth) {
      wdDayWungjiReset_();
      const loading = document.getElementById('wdLoadingText');
      if (!auth || !auth.ok) {
        if (loading) loading.textContent = '로그인 정보를 찾지 못했습니다.';
        return;
      }
      try {
        if (loading) loading.textContent = '일과 중 웅지실 데이터를 불러오는 중입니다.';
        const loginName = auth.role === 'admin' ? 'admin' : auth.id;
        const res = await wdDayWungjiCallGas_('wdLogin', loginName);
        if (!res || !res.ok) throw new Error((res && res.message) || '일과 중 웅지실 로그인에 실패했습니다.');
        wdDayState_.user = res;
        if (res.role === 'admin') wdDayWungjiShowAdmin_(res);
        else wdDayWungjiShowTeacher_(res);
      } catch (err) {
        if (loading) loading.textContent = err && err.message ? err.message : String(err || '일과 중 웅지실을 불러오지 못했습니다.');
        wdDayWungjiShowScreen_('wdLoadingScreen');
      }
    }

    function wdDayWungjiRefresh_() {
      if (!wdDayState_.user) return;
      if (wdDayState_.user.role === 'admin') {
        wdDayWungjiLoadAdminPeriod_(wdDayState_.adminPeriod || Number(wdDayState_.user.currentPeriod || 1));
        return;
      }
      if (wdDayState_.selectedCourse) wdDayWungjiSelectCourse_(wdDayState_.selectedCourse, null, true);
    }

    function wdDayWungjiShowTeacher_(user) {
      wdDayWungjiShowScreen_('wdTeacherScreen');
      const dateText = document.getElementById('wdTeacherDateText');
      if (dateText) dateText.textContent = `${user.dateKey || ''} ${user.dayLabel || ''}`;
      wdDayWungjiRenderCourses_(user.schedule && user.schedule.courses || []);
      const selected = document.getElementById('wdSelectedCourseText');
      const list = document.getElementById('wdStudentList');
      const bulk = document.getElementById('wdBulkBtn');
      if (selected) selected.textContent = '교시를 선택하세요.';
      if (list) list.innerHTML = '<div class="wdEmpty">교시를 선택하세요.</div>';
      if (bulk) bulk.disabled = true;
      wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdTeacherSeatMap', [], 'teacher');
    }

    function wdDayWungjiRenderCourses_(courses) {
      const el = document.getElementById('wdCourseList');
      if (!el) return;
      if (!courses.length) {
        el.innerHTML = '<div class="wdEmpty">오늘 표시할 수업이 없습니다.</div>';
        return;
      }
      el.innerHTML = courses.map((c, idx) => `
        <button type="button" class="wdCard" data-wd-course-idx="${idx}">
          <div class="wdCourseTop"><span class="wdPeriodPill">${Number(c.period)}교시</span><span class="wdCountPill${Number(c.activeCount||0)>0?' wdOn':''}">${c.totalCount === '' ? '선택' : Number(c.activeCount||0)+'/'+Number(c.totalCount||0)}</span></div>
          <div class="wdSubject">${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(c.subject || '-')}</div>
          <div class="wdCourseMeta">${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_((c.classGroup ? c.classGroup + '반' : '') + (c.teacher ? ' · ' + c.teacher : ''))}</div>
        </button>
      `).join('');
      el.querySelectorAll('[data-wd-course-idx]').forEach(btn => {
        btn.addEventListener('click', () => wdDayWungjiSelectCourse_(courses[Number(btn.dataset.wdCourseIdx)], btn));
      });
    }

    async function wdDayWungjiSelectCourse_(course, btn, keepSelection) {
      document.querySelectorAll('#wdCourseList .wdCard').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('wdActiveCourse'));
      if (btn) btn.classList.add('wdActiveCourse');
      else if (keepSelection && course) {
        document.querySelectorAll('#wdCourseList .wdCard').forEach(card => {
          const p = card.querySelector('.wdPeriodPill');
          const s = card.querySelector('.wdSubject');
          if (p && s && p.textContent === Number(course.period) + '교시' && s.textContent === String(course.subject || '-')) card.classList.add('wdActiveCourse');
        });
      }
      wdDayState_.selectedCourse = course;
      const selected = document.getElementById('wdSelectedCourseText');
      const list = document.getElementById('wdStudentList');
      const bulk = document.getElementById('wdBulkBtn');
      if (selected) selected.innerHTML = `<span class="wdSelectedCourseLine">${Number(course.period)}교시 ${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(course.classGroup || '')}반</span><span class="wdSelectedSubjectLine">${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(course.subject || '-')}</span>`;
      if (list) list.innerHTML = '<div class="wdEmpty">불러오는 중...</div>';
      if (bulk) bulk.disabled = true;
      wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdTeacherSeatMap', [], 'teacher');
      try {
        const res = await wdDayWungjiCallGas_('wdGetCourseStudents', { user: wdDayWungjiCompactUser_(), course });
        if (!res || !res.ok) throw new Error((res && res.message) || '명단을 불러오지 못했습니다.');
        wdDayState_.selectedCourse = res.course || course;
        wdDayState_.teacherStudents = res.students || [];
        if (bulk) bulk.disabled = !wdDayState_.teacherStudents.length;
        wdDayWungjiRenderTeacherStudents_();
        wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdTeacherSeatMap', wdDayState_.teacherStudents, 'teacher');
      } catch (err) {
        if (list) list.innerHTML = `<div class="wdEmpty">${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(err.message || String(err))}</div>`;
      }
    }

    function wdDayWungjiCompactUser_() {
      return wdDayState_.user ? { role: wdDayState_.user.role, id: wdDayState_.user.id } : null;
    }

    function wdDayWungjiRenderTeacherStudents_() {
      const el = document.getElementById('wdStudentList');
      if (!el) return;
      const rows = (wdDayState_.teacherStudents || []).slice().sort((a,b) => String(a.id).localeCompare(String(b.id),'ko',{numeric:true}));
      if (!rows.length) {
        el.innerHTML = '<div class="wdEmpty">이 교시의 이용 학생이 없습니다.</div>';
        return;
      }
      el.innerHTML = rows.map(st => `
        <button type="button" class="wdStudentCard${st.active?' wdOn':''}" data-wd-student-id="${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(st.id)}">
          <span class="wdStudentName">${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(st.name)}</span>
          <span class="wdStudentId">${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(st.id)}</span>
        </button>
      `).join('');
      el.querySelectorAll('[data-wd-student-id]').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', () => wdDayWungjiToggleTeacherStudent_(btn.dataset.wdStudentId)));
    }

    function wdDayWungjiFindTeacherStudent_(id) {
      return (wdDayState_.teacherStudents || []).find(st => String(st.id) === String(id));
    }

    function wdDayWungjiApplyTeacherStudentActive_(id, active) {
      const st = wdDayWungjiFindTeacherStudent_(id);
      if (st) st.active = !!active;
      wdDayWungjiRenderTeacherStudents_();
      wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdTeacherSeatMap', wdDayState_.teacherStudents, 'teacher');
      wdDayWungjiRefreshCourseCountLocal_();
    }

    function wdDayWungjiRefreshCourseCountLocal_() {
      if (!wdDayState_.selectedCourse) return;
      const active = (wdDayState_.teacherStudents || []).filter(s => s.active).length;
      const total = (wdDayState_.teacherStudents || []).length;
      wdDayState_.selectedCourse.activeCount = active;
      wdDayState_.selectedCourse.totalCount = total;
      document.querySelectorAll('#wdCourseList .wdCard').forEach(card => {
        const subj = card.querySelector('.wdSubject');
        const period = card.querySelector('.wdPeriodPill');
        if (!subj || !period) return;
        if (subj.textContent === wdDayState_.selectedCourse.subject && period.textContent === Number(wdDayState_.selectedCourse.period) + '교시') {
          const pill = card.querySelector('.wdCountPill');
          if (pill) {
            pill.textContent = `${active}/${total}`;
            pill.classList.toggle('wdOn', active > 0);
          }
        }
      });
    }

    async function wdDayWungjiToggleTeacherStudent_(id) {
      const st = wdDayWungjiFindTeacherStudent_(id);
      if (!st || !wdDayState_.selectedCourse) return;
      const prev = !!st.active;
      const next = !prev;
      const versionKey = `teacher:${wdDayState_.selectedCourse.period}:${wdDayState_.selectedCourse.rosterKey}:${id}`;
      const version = wdDayWungjiNextWriteVersion_(versionKey);
      const payloadStudent = Object.assign({}, st);
      const payloadCourse = Object.assign({}, wdDayState_.selectedCourse);
      wdDayWungjiApplyTeacherStudentActive_(id, next);
      wdDayWungjiEnqueueWrite_(async () => {
        try {
          const res = await wdDayWungjiCallGas_('wdTeacherToggleStudent', { user: wdDayWungjiCompactUser_(), course: payloadCourse, student: payloadStudent, nextActive: next });
          if (!res || !res.ok) throw new Error((res && res.message) || '처리 실패');
        } catch (err) {
          if (wdDayWungjiCurrentWriteVersion_(versionKey) === version) wdDayWungjiApplyTeacherStudentActive_(id, prev);
          wdDayWungjiShowToast_(err.message || String(err));
        }
      });
    }

    async function wdDayWungjiBulkMove_() {
      if (!wdDayState_.selectedCourse || !wdDayState_.teacherStudents.length) return;
      const before = wdDayState_.teacherStudents.map(s => ({ id:s.id, active:s.active }));
      const payloadCourse = Object.assign({}, wdDayState_.selectedCourse);
      const versionKey = `bulk:${payloadCourse.period}:${payloadCourse.rosterKey}`;
      const version = wdDayWungjiNextWriteVersion_(versionKey);
      wdDayState_.teacherStudents.forEach(s => {
        s.active = true;
        wdDayWungjiNextWriteVersion_(`teacher:${payloadCourse.period}:${payloadCourse.rosterKey}:${s.id}`);
      });
      wdDayWungjiRenderTeacherStudents_();
      wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdTeacherSeatMap', wdDayState_.teacherStudents, 'teacher');
      wdDayWungjiRefreshCourseCountLocal_();
      wdDayWungjiEnqueueWrite_(async () => {
        try {
          const res = await wdDayWungjiCallGas_('wdBulkSetCourseStudents', { user: wdDayWungjiCompactUser_(), course: payloadCourse });
          if (!res || !res.ok) throw new Error((res && res.message) || '처리 실패');
          wdDayWungjiShowToast_('전체 웅지실로 이동');
        } catch (err) {
          if (wdDayWungjiCurrentWriteVersion_(versionKey) === version) {
            before.forEach(x => { const st = wdDayWungjiFindTeacherStudent_(x.id); if (st) st.active = x.active; });
            wdDayWungjiRenderTeacherStudents_();
            wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdTeacherSeatMap', wdDayState_.teacherStudents, 'teacher');
            wdDayWungjiRefreshCourseCountLocal_();
          }
          wdDayWungjiShowToast_(err.message || String(err));
        }
      });
    }

    function wdDayWungjiShowAdmin_(user) {
      wdDayWungjiShowScreen_('wdAdminScreen');
      wdDayWungjiRenderPeriodButtons_(Number(user.currentPeriod || 1));
      wdDayWungjiLoadAdminPeriod_(Number(user.currentPeriod || 1));
    }

    function wdDayWungjiRenderPeriodButtons_(activePeriod) {
      const el = document.getElementById('wdPeriodBtns');
      if (!el) return;
      el.innerHTML = Array.from({length:7}, (_,i) => i+1).map(p => `<button type="button" class="wdPeriodBtn${p===activePeriod?' wdActivePeriod':''}" data-wd-period="${p}">${p}교시</button>`).join('');
      el.querySelectorAll('[data-wd-period]').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', () => wdDayWungjiLoadAdminPeriod_(Number(btn.dataset.wdPeriod))));
    }

    async function wdDayWungjiLoadAdminPeriod_(period) {
      wdDayState_.adminPeriod = period;
      document.querySelectorAll('#wdPeriodBtns .wdPeriodBtn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.toggle('wdActivePeriod', Number(btn.dataset.wdPeriod) === Number(period)));
      const sub = document.getElementById('wdAdminSubText');
      if (sub) sub.textContent = `${period}교시 불러오는 중...`;
      wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdAdminSeatMap', [], 'admin');
      try {
        const res = await wdDayWungjiCallGas_('wdGetAdminPeriodStatus', { user: wdDayWungjiCompactUser_(), period });
        if (!res || !res.ok) throw new Error((res && res.message) || '현황을 불러오지 못했습니다.');
        wdDayState_.adminPeriod = Number(res.period);
        wdDayState_.adminStudents = res.students || [];
        if (sub) sub.textContent = `${res.dateKey || ''} ${res.dayLabel || ''} ${Number(res.period)}교시 · ${Number(res.summary && res.summary.active || 0)}/${Number(res.summary && res.summary.total || 0)}`;
        wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdAdminSeatMap', wdDayState_.adminStudents, 'admin');
        wdDayWungjiRenderPeriodButtons_(Number(res.period));
      } catch (err) {
        if (sub) sub.textContent = err.message || String(err);
        wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdAdminSeatMap', [], 'admin');
      }
    }

    function wdDayWungjiFindAdminStudent_(id) {
      return (wdDayState_.adminStudents || []).find(st => String(st.id) === String(id));
    }

    function wdDayWungjiOpenAdminModal_(id) {
      const st = wdDayWungjiFindAdminStudent_(id);
      if (!st) return;
      wdDayState_.modalStudent = st;
      const title = document.getElementById('wdModalStudentName');
      const info = document.getElementById('wdModalInfo');
      if (title) title.textContent = st.name || '학생';
      if (info) info.innerHTML = `
        <div>학번: ${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(st.id || '-')}</div>
        <div>과목: ${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(st.subject || '-')}</div>
        <div>교사: ${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(st.teacher || '-')}</div>
      `;
      const absent = document.querySelector('input[name="wdAdminAction"][value="absent"]');
      if (absent) absent.checked = true;
      const modal = document.getElementById('wdAdminModal');
      if (modal) modal.classList.add('wdActiveModal');
    }

    function wdDayWungjiCloseAdminModal_() {
      const modal = document.getElementById('wdAdminModal');
      if (modal) modal.classList.remove('wdActiveModal');
      wdDayState_.modalStudent = null;
    }

    async function wdDayWungjiConfirmAdminAction_() {
      const st = wdDayState_.modalStudent;
      if (!st) return wdDayWungjiCloseAdminModal_();
      const actionEl = document.querySelector('input[name="wdAdminAction"]:checked');
      const action = actionEl ? actionEl.value : 'absent';
      const next = action === 'present';
      const prev = !!st.active;
      const payloadStudent = Object.assign({}, st);
      const payloadCourse = Object.assign({}, st.course || {});
      const versionKey = `admin:${wdDayState_.adminPeriod}:${st.id}`;
      const version = wdDayWungjiNextWriteVersion_(versionKey);
      st.active = next;
      wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdAdminSeatMap', wdDayState_.adminStudents, 'admin');
      wdDayWungjiCloseAdminModal_();
      wdDayWungjiEnqueueWrite_(async () => {
        try {
          const res = await wdDayWungjiCallGas_('wdAdminSetStudent', { user: wdDayWungjiCompactUser_(), student: payloadStudent, course: payloadCourse, action });
          if (!res || !res.ok) throw new Error((res && res.message) || '처리 실패');
          wdDayWungjiShowToast_(next ? '웅지실 입실' : '취소');
        } catch (err) {
          if (wdDayWungjiCurrentWriteVersion_(versionKey) === version) {
            const current = wdDayWungjiFindAdminStudent_(payloadStudent.id);
            if (current) current.active = prev;
            wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_('wdAdminSeatMap', wdDayState_.adminStudents, 'admin');
          }
          wdDayWungjiShowToast_(err.message || String(err));
        }
      });
    }

    function wdDayWungjiRenderSeatLayout_(areaId, rows, mode) {
      const area = document.getElementById(areaId);
      if (!area) return;
      const studentMap = {};
      (rows || []).forEach(st => { if (st.seatKey) studentMap[String(st.seatKey).replace(/\s+/g,'')] = st; });
      let html = '<div class="wdRoomContainer">';
      html += '<div class="wdOpenSection">';
      for (let block=0; block<3; block++) {
        html += '<div class="wdOpenBlock">';
        for (let n=1; n<=8; n++) html += wdDayWungjiCreateSeatBox_(`개방${block*8+n}`, studentMap);
        html += '</div>';
      }
      html += '</div>';
      html += '<div class="wdCenterSection">';
      for (let n=25; n<=28; n++) html += wdDayWungjiCreateSeatBox_(`개방${n}`, studentMap);
      html += '<div class="wdCenterLabel">중앙복도</div></div>';
      html += '<div class="wdClosedSection">';
      html += '<div class="wdClosedBlock">';
      for (let r=0; r<9; r++) {
        html += wdDayWungjiCreateSeatBox_(`폐쇄${28+r}`, studentMap);
        html += wdDayWungjiCreateSeatBox_(`폐쇄${19+r}`, studentMap);
      }
      html += '</div><div class="wdClosedBlock">';
      for (let r=0; r<9; r++) {
        html += wdDayWungjiCreateSeatBox_(`폐쇄${10+r}`, studentMap);
        html += wdDayWungjiCreateSeatBox_(`폐쇄${1+r}`, studentMap);
      }
      html += '</div></div></div>';
      area.innerHTML = html;
      area.querySelectorAll('.wdSeatBox[data-wd-student-id]').forEach(el => {
        const id = el.dataset.wdStudentId;
        el.addEventListener('click', () => mode === 'admin' ? wdDayWungjiOpenAdminModal_(id) : wdDayWungjiToggleTeacherStudent_(id));
      });
    }

    function wdDayWungjiCreateSeatBox_(seatName, studentMap) {
      const key = String(seatName).replace(/\s+/g,'');
      const st = studentMap[key];
      const classes = ['wdSeatBox'];
      if (st) classes.push('wdClickable');
      if (st && st.active) classes.push('wdOn');
      const attrs = st ? ` data-wd-student-id="${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(st.id)}" title="${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_([st.id, st.name, st.subject, st.teacher].filter(Boolean).join(' '))}"` : '';
      return `<div class="${classes.join(' ')}"${attrs}><div class="wdSeatLabel">${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(seatName)}</div>${st ? `<div class="wdSeatName">${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(st.name)}</div><div class="wdSeatStudentId">${wdDayWungjiEscapeHtml_(st.id || '')}</div>` : '<div class="wdSeatName">-</div>'}</div>`;
    }


    function toLocalDateKey_(date) {
      const y = date.getFullYear();
      const m = String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
      const d = String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
      return `${y}-${m}-${d}`;
    }

    function setClassDateToday() {
      document.getElementById('classScheduleDate').value = toLocalDateKey_(new Date());
      loadClassSchedule();
    }

    function shiftClassDate(delta) {
      const input = document.getElementById('classScheduleDate');
      const base = input.value ? new Date(input.value + 'T12:00:00') : new Date();
      base.setDate(base.getDate() + Number(delta || 0));
      input.value = toLocalDateKey_(base);
      loadClassSchedule();
    }

    function callGasPromise_(name, ...args) {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(resolve).withFailureHandler(err => reject(new Error(err && err.message ? err.message : String(err))))[name](...args);
      });
    }

    function splitSubjectLabel_(subject) {
      const text = String(subject || '').trim();
      if (text.length <= 5) return escapeHtml(text);
      return escapeHtml(text.slice(0, 5)) + '<br>' + escapeHtml(text.slice(5));
    }

    function renderClassSchedule_(res) {
      const teacherSelect = document.getElementById('classTeacherSelect');
      if (currentIntegratedUser && currentIntegratedUser.role === 'admin' && (!teacherSelect.options.length || teacherSelect.dataset.loaded !== 'true')) {
        teacherSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">교사를 선택하세요</option>' + (res.teachers || []).map(t => `<option value="${escapeHtml(t)}">${escapeHtml(t)}</option>`).join('');
        teacherSelect.dataset.loaded = 'true';
      }
      if (teacherSelect && res.teacher) teacherSelect.value = res.teacher;
      const teacherName = res.teacher || '교사 미선택';
      document.getElementById('classScheduleTitle').innerText = `${res.date}(${res.dayLabel || '-'}) ${teacherName} 시간표`;
      const body = document.getElementById('classScheduleBody');
      let html = '';
      (res.periods || []).forEach(p => {
        if (!p.courses || !p.courses.length) {
          html += `<tr><td><strong>${p.period}</strong></td><td colspan="3" class="text-muted">수업 없음</td></tr>`;
          return;
        }
        p.courses.forEach(c => {
          const btnClass = c.rosterRegistered ? 'class-course-btn' : 'class-course-btn unregistered';
          const rosterText = c.rosterState === 'applicantMissing' ? '신청자 미등록' : c.rosterState === 'subjectMissing' ? '출석부 미등록' : `${c.rosterCount}명`;
          html += `<tr>
            <td><strong>${p.period}</strong></td>
            <td><button class="${btnClass}" type="button" onclick='openWungjiCourse(${JSON.stringify(res.date)},${p.period},${JSON.stringify(c.rosterKey)})'><span class="class-subject-label">${splitSubjectLabel_(c.subject)}</span></button></td>
            <td>${c.classGroup}반</td>
            <td>${rosterText}</td>
          </tr>`;
        });
      });
      body.innerHTML = html || '<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty">표시할 시간표가 없습니다.</td></tr>';
    }

    async function loadClassSchedule() {
      if (!currentIntegratedUser) return;
      const dateInput = document.getElementById('classScheduleDate');
      if (!dateInput.value) dateInput.value = toLocalDateKey_(new Date());
      const teacherSelect = document.getElementById('classTeacherSelect');
      const inspectTeacher = currentIntegratedUser.role === 'admin' ? teacherSelect.value : currentIntegratedUser.id;
      const body = document.getElementById('classScheduleBody');
      body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty"><div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm me-2"></div>시간표를 불러오는 중입니다...</td></tr>';
      try {
        const res = await callGasPromise_('getTeacherWungjiSchedule', currentIntegratedUser.id, currentIntegratedPassword, dateInput.value, inspectTeacher);
        if (currentIntegratedUser.role === 'admin' && !inspectTeacher && res.teachers && res.teachers.length) {
          teacherSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">교사를 선택하세요</option>' + res.teachers.map(t => `<option value="${escapeHtml(t)}">${escapeHtml(t)}</option>`).join('');
          teacherSelect.dataset.loaded = 'true';
          teacherSelect.value = res.teachers[0];
          return loadClassSchedule();
        }
        renderClassSchedule_(res);
        if (!isClassAdmin_()) autoOpenCurrentTeacherCourse_(res);
      } catch (err) {
        body.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty text-danger">${escapeHtml(err.message)}</td></tr>`;
      }
    }

    async function autoOpenCurrentTeacherCourse_(scheduleRes) {
      if (!currentIntegratedUser || isClassAdmin_()) return;
      const dateInput = document.getElementById('classScheduleDate');
      const selectedDate = dateInput && dateInput.value ? dateInput.value : '';
      if (!selectedDate) return;
      try {
        const res = await callGasPromise_('getCurrentWungjiAttendanceStatus', currentIntegratedUser.id, currentIntegratedPassword);
        if (!res || !res.ok || !res.active || res.date !== selectedDate || !res.courses || !res.courses.length) return;
        const firstCourse = res.courses[0];
        if (!firstCourse || !firstCourse.rosterKey) return;
        const sameSelection = selectedWungjiCourse && selectedWungjiCourse.date === res.date && Number(selectedWungjiCourse.period) === Number(res.period) && selectedWungjiCourse.rosterKey === firstCourse.rosterKey;
        if (sameSelection) return;
        openWungjiCourse(res.date, Number(res.period), firstCourse.rosterKey, { skipScroll: true });
      } catch (_) {
        // 현재 교시 자동 선택에 실패해도 시간표 조회 자체는 유지합니다.
      }
    }

    function registerClassAttendanceAction_(student) {
      if (!student) return '';
      const key = [student.date || '', student.period || '', student.rosterKey || '', student.id || '', Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7)].join('|');
      classAttendanceActionMap[key] = student;
      return key;
    }


    function getClassSeatStateClass_(status) {
      if (status === '출석' || status === '웅지실') return 'class-seat-present';
      if (status === '수업참석') return 'class-seat-class';
      return 'class-seat-absent';
    }

    function getClassStatusBadgeClass_(status) {
      if (status === '출석' || status === '웅지실') return 'status-present';
      if (status === '수업참석') return 'status-class';
      return 'status-absent';
    }

    function getClassStatusDisplay_(status) {
      if (status === '출석' || status === '웅지실') return '웅지실';
      return status || '미로그인';
    }

    function getClassAttendanceCountHtml_(res) {
      const present = Number(res && res.presentCount || 0);
      const classCount = Number(res && res.classCount || 0);
      const absent = Number(res && res.absentCount || 0);
      return `<span class="class-total-count">웅지실 ${present}명</span> / <span class="status-class">수업참석 ${classCount}명</span> / <span class="class-missing-count">미로그인 ${absent}명</span>`;
    }

    function getWungjiRowDataAttrs_(student) {
      if (!student) return '';
      return `data-wungji-student-id="${escapeHtml(student.id || '')}" data-wungji-date="${escapeHtml(student.date || '')}" data-wungji-period="${escapeHtml(String(student.period || ''))}" data-wungji-roster-key="${escapeHtml(student.rosterKey || '')}"`;
    }

    function formatManualTime4ToDisplay_(time4) {
      const digits = String(time4 || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
      if (digits.length < 4) return '';
      return digits.slice(0, 2) + ':' + digits.slice(2, 4);
    }

    function updateClassCountBadgesFromRows_() {
      [['classLiveAttendanceBody', 'classLiveStatusSub'], ['classAttendanceBody', 'classAttendanceSub']].forEach(function(pair) {
        const body = document.getElementById(pair[0]);
        const sub = document.getElementById(pair[1]);
        if (!body || !sub) return;
        const rows = Array.from(body.querySelectorAll('tr[data-wungji-student-id]'));
        if (!rows.length) return;
        let present = 0, classAttend = 0, absent = 0;
        rows.forEach(function(tr) {
          const badge = tr.querySelector('.class-status-cell span');
          const text = badge ? badge.textContent.trim() : '';
          if (text === '출석' || text === '웅지실') present++;
          else if (text === '수업참석') classAttend++;
          else absent++;
        });
        const presentEl = sub.querySelector('.class-total-count');
        const classEl = sub.querySelector('.status-class');
        const absentEl = sub.querySelector('.class-missing-count');
        if (presentEl) presentEl.textContent = '웅지실 ' + present + '명';
        if (classEl) classEl.textContent = '수업참석 ' + classAttend + '명';
        if (absentEl) absentEl.textContent = '미로그인 ' + absent + '명';
      });
    }

    function optimisticUpdateWungjiAttendanceUi_(student, action, time4, mode) {
      if (!student) return;
      const newStatus = action === 'absent' ? '미로그인' : (mode === 'class' ? '수업참석' : '출석');
      const displayTime = action === 'absent' ? '' : formatManualTime4ToDisplay_(time4);
      const rowSelector = `tr[data-wungji-student-id="${CSS.escape(String(student.id || ''))}"][data-wungji-date="${CSS.escape(String(student.date || ''))}"][data-wungji-period="${CSS.escape(String(student.period || ''))}"][data-wungji-roster-key="${CSS.escape(String(student.rosterKey || ''))}"]`;
      document.querySelectorAll(rowSelector).forEach(function(tr) {
        const timeCell = tr.querySelector('.class-login-cell');
        const statusCell = tr.querySelector('.class-status-cell');
        if (timeCell) timeCell.textContent = displayTime || '-';
        if (statusCell) statusCell.innerHTML = `<span class="${getClassStatusBadgeClass_(newStatus)}">${escapeHtml(getClassStatusDisplay_(newStatus))}</span>`;
      });
      const seatSelector = `.class-seat-box[data-wungji-student-id="${CSS.escape(String(student.id || ''))}"][data-wungji-date="${CSS.escape(String(student.date || ''))}"][data-wungji-period="${CSS.escape(String(student.period || ''))}"][data-wungji-roster-key="${CSS.escape(String(student.rosterKey || ''))}"]`;
      document.querySelectorAll(seatSelector).forEach(function(box) {
        box.classList.remove('class-seat-present', 'class-seat-class', 'class-seat-absent');
        box.classList.add(getClassSeatStateClass_(newStatus));
        let timeEl = box.querySelector('.class-seat-time');
        if (!timeEl) {
          timeEl = document.createElement('div');
          timeEl.className = 'class-seat-time';
          box.appendChild(timeEl);
        }
        timeEl.textContent = displayTime || '';
      });
      Object.keys(classAttendanceActionMap || {}).forEach(function(key) {
        const item = classAttendanceActionMap[key];
        if (!item) return;
        if (String(item.id || '') === String(student.id || '') && String(item.date || '') === String(student.date || '') && String(item.period || '') === String(student.period || '') && String(item.rosterKey || '') === String(student.rosterKey || '')) {
          item.status = newStatus;
          item.loginTime = displayTime;
        }
      });
      updateClassCountBadgesFromRows_();
    }

    function showWungjiAttendanceEdit_(student, callback) {
      document.getElementById('wungjiEditTitle').innerText = `${student.name} 학생 출석상황 변경` + (student.courseLabel ? ` (${student.courseLabel})` : '');
      const timeInput = document.getElementById('wungjiEditTimeInput');
      timeInput.value = normalizeTimeForManualInput4_(student.loginTime) || getCurrentTime4_();
      document.querySelectorAll('input[name="wungjiEditMode"]').forEach(function(el) { el.checked = false; });
      const defaultMode = student.status === '수업참석' ? 'class' : ((student.status === '출석' || student.status === '웅지실') ? 'wungji' : 'wungji');
      const target = document.querySelector('input[name="wungjiEditMode"][value="' + defaultMode + '"]');
      if (target) target.checked = true;
      wungjiEditCallback = callback;
      if (!wungjiEditModal && window.bootstrap && bootstrap.Modal) {
        wungjiEditModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('wungjiEditModal'));
      }
      if (wungjiEditModal) {
        wungjiEditModal.show();
        setTimeout(function() { timeInput.focus(); timeInput.select(); }, 200);
      } else {
        showMessage('출석상황 변경 창을 여는 중 문제가 발생했습니다. 화면을 새로고침한 뒤 다시 시도하세요.');
      }
    }

    function createClassSeatBox_(seatName, studentMap) {
      const student = studentMap[seatName];
      const stateClass = !student ? 'class-seat-empty' : getClassSeatStateClass_(student.status);
      const actionKey = student ? registerClassAttendanceAction_(student) : '';
      const clickableAttrs = student ? ` role="button" tabindex="0" onclick="openWungjiAttendanceEditByKey_('${escapeHtml(actionKey)}')" onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter'||event.key===' '){event.preventDefault();openWungjiAttendanceEditByKey_('${escapeHtml(actionKey)}');}"` : '';
      const title = student ? [student.id, student.name, getClassStatusDisplay_(student.status), student.loginTime || '', student.courseLabel || student.subject || ''].filter(Boolean).join(' ') : seatName;
      const dataAttrs = student ? getWungjiRowDataAttrs_(student) : '';
      return `<div class="class-seat-box ${stateClass}${student ? ' class-seat-clickable' : ''}" title="${escapeHtml(title)}" ${dataAttrs}${clickableAttrs}>
        <div class="seat-label">${escapeHtml(seatName)}</div>
        <div class="seat-name">${student ? escapeHtml(student.name) : '-'}</div>
        <div class="class-seat-time">${student && student.loginTime ? escapeHtml(student.loginTime) : ''}</div>
      </div>`;
    }

    function syncClassSeatScrollbar_(wrapperId, sliderId) {
      const wrapper = document.getElementById(wrapperId || 'classSeatMapWrapper');
      const slider = document.getElementById(sliderId || 'classSeatScrollbar');
      if (!wrapper || !slider) return;
      const max = Math.max(0, wrapper.scrollWidth - wrapper.clientWidth);
      slider.max = String(Math.max(1, Math.round(max)));
      slider.value = String(Math.min(max, wrapper.scrollLeft));
      slider.disabled = max <= 0;
      if (!wrapper.dataset.scrollSyncBound) {
        slider.addEventListener('input', function() { wrapper.scrollLeft = Number(slider.value || 0); });
        wrapper.addEventListener('scroll', function() { slider.value = String(Math.round(wrapper.scrollLeft)); }, { passive:true });
        wrapper.dataset.scrollSyncBound = 'true';
      }
    }

    function renderClassSeatingLayout_(rows, areaId, wrapperId, sliderId) {
      const area = document.getElementById(areaId || 'classSeatingChartArea');
      if (!area) return;
      const studentMap = {};
      (rows || []).forEach(row => { if (row.seatKey) studentMap[row.seatKey] = row; });
      let html = '<div class="class-room-container">';
      html += '<div class="class-open-section">';
      for (let block = 0; block < 3; block++) {
        html += '<div class="class-open-block">';
        for (let n = 1; n <= 8; n++) html += createClassSeatBox_(`개방${block * 8 + n}`, studentMap);
        html += '</div>';
      }
      html += '</div>';
      html += '<div class="class-center-section">';
      for (let n = 25; n <= 28; n++) html += createClassSeatBox_(`개방${n}`, studentMap);
      html += '<div class="class-center-label">중앙복도</div></div>';
      html += '<div class="class-closed-section">';
      html += '<div class="class-closed-block">';
      for (let r = 0; r < 9; r++) {
        html += createClassSeatBox_(`폐쇄${28 + r}`, studentMap);
        html += createClassSeatBox_(`폐쇄${19 + r}`, studentMap);
      }
      html += '</div>';
      html += '<div class="class-closed-block">';
      for (let r = 0; r < 9; r++) {
        html += createClassSeatBox_(`폐쇄${10 + r}`, studentMap);
        html += createClassSeatBox_(`폐쇄${1 + r}`, studentMap);
      }
      html += '</div></div></div>';
      area.innerHTML = html;
      requestAnimationFrame(function() { syncClassSeatScrollbar_(wrapperId || 'classSeatMapWrapper', sliderId || 'classSeatScrollbar'); });
    }

    function getCurrentTime4_() {
      const now = new Date();
      return String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0') + String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
    }

    function normalizeTimeForManualInput4_(value) {
      const digits = String(value || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
      return digits.length >= 4 ? digits.slice(0, 4) : '';
    }

    function openWungjiAttendanceEditByKey_(key) {
      const student = classAttendanceActionMap[key];
      if (!student) return showMessage('학생 정보를 다시 불러와 주세요.');
      showWungjiAttendanceEdit_(student, function(result) {
        updateWungjiAttendanceFromUi_(student, result.action, result.time, result.mode);
      });
    }

    function updateWungjiAttendanceFromUi_(student, action, time4, mode) {
      const payload = {
        date: student.date,
        period: student.period,
        rosterKey: student.rosterKey,
        studentId: student.id,
        action: action,
        mode: mode || 'wungji',
        time: time4 || ''
      };
      optimisticUpdateWungjiAttendanceUi_(student, action, time4, mode || 'wungji');
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
          showMessage(result || '처리되었습니다.');
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
          showMessage('오류 발생: ' + (error && error.message ? error.message : String(error || '처리 오류')) + '\n화면을 다시 불러옵니다.');
          if (isClassAdmin_()) loadCurrentWungjiStatus();
          if (selectedWungjiCourse) refreshSelectedClassAttendance();
        })
        .updateWungjiAttendanceState(currentIntegratedUser.id, currentIntegratedPassword, payload);
    }

    async function loadCurrentWungjiStatus() {
      if (!currentIntegratedUser || adminMode !== 'class') return;
      const titleEl = document.getElementById('classLiveStatusTitle');
      const subEl = document.getElementById('classLiveStatusSub');
      const bodyEl = document.getElementById('classLiveAttendanceBody');
      if (titleEl) titleEl.innerText = '일과 중 웅지실 현황';
      if (subEl) subEl.innerText = '현재 교시를 확인 중입니다.';
      if (bodyEl) bodyEl.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="muted-empty"><div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm me-2"></div>현황을 불러오는 중입니다...</td></tr>';
      renderClassSeatingLayout_([], 'classLiveSeatingChartArea', 'classLiveSeatMapWrapper', 'classLiveSeatScrollbar');
      try {
        const res = await callGasPromise_('getCurrentWungjiAttendanceStatus', currentIntegratedUser.id, currentIntegratedPassword);
        if (!res || !res.ok) throw new Error(res && res.message ? res.message : '현황을 불러오지 못했습니다.');
        if (!res.active) {
          titleEl.innerText = `${res.titleLabel || getTodayFormatted()} 일과 중 웅지실 현황`;
          subEl.innerText = res.message || '현재 표시할 수업이 없습니다.';
          bodyEl.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" class="muted-empty">${escapeHtml(res.message || '현재 표시할 수업이 없습니다.')}</td></tr>`;
          renderClassSeatingLayout_([], 'classLiveSeatingChartArea', 'classLiveSeatMapWrapper', 'classLiveSeatScrollbar');
          return;
        }
        const rows = (res.rows || []).slice();
        titleEl.innerText = `${res.titleLabel} 일과 중 웅지실 현황`;
        const courseText = (res.courses || []).map(c => `${c.subject} ${c.classGroup}반`).join(' / ');
        subEl.innerHTML = `<span class="class-attendance-date-line">${Number(res.period)}교시 ${escapeHtml(res.startTime || '')}~${escapeHtml(res.endTime || '')}</span><span class="class-attendance-count-line">${getClassAttendanceCountHtml_(res)}</span>${courseText ? `<span class="class-live-course-line">${escapeHtml(courseText)}</span>` : ''}`;
        bodyEl.innerHTML = rows.map(r => {
          const key = registerClassAttendanceAction_(r);
          return `<tr ${getWungjiRowDataAttrs_(r)}><td><strong>${escapeHtml(r.seatKey || '-')}</strong></td><td>${escapeHtml(r.id)}</td><td><button type="button" class="class-name-link" onclick="openWungjiAttendanceEditByKey_('${escapeHtml(key)}')">${escapeHtml(r.name)}</button></td><td>${escapeHtml(r.courseLabel || '-')}</td><td class="class-login-cell">${escapeHtml(r.loginTime || '-')}</td><td class="class-status-cell"><span class="${getClassStatusBadgeClass_(r.status)}">${escapeHtml(getClassStatusDisplay_(r.status))}</span></td></tr>`;
        }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="6" class="muted-empty">이 교시의 웅지실 이용 학생이 없습니다.</td></tr>';
        renderClassSeatingLayout_(rows, 'classLiveSeatingChartArea', 'classLiveSeatMapWrapper', 'classLiveSeatScrollbar');
      } catch (err) {
        subEl.innerText = err.message;
        bodyEl.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" class="muted-empty text-danger">${escapeHtml(err.message)}</td></tr>`;
        renderClassSeatingLayout_([], 'classLiveSeatingChartArea', 'classLiveSeatMapWrapper', 'classLiveSeatScrollbar');
      }
    }

    async function openWungjiCourse(date, period, rosterKey, options) {
      selectedWungjiCourse = { date, period, rosterKey };
      const panel = document.getElementById('classAttendancePanel');
      const seatPanel = document.getElementById('classSeatPanel');
      const seatSubEl = document.getElementById('classSeatSub');
      const titleEl = document.getElementById('classAttendanceTitle');
      const subEl = document.getElementById('classAttendanceSub');
      options = options || {};
      panel.style.display = 'block';
      if (seatPanel) seatPanel.style.display = 'block';
      titleEl.innerText = '출석 현황';
      subEl.innerText = `${date} ${period}교시`;
      document.getElementById('classAttendanceBody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="muted-empty"><div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm me-2"></div>출석 현황을 불러오는 중입니다...</td></tr>';
      document.getElementById('classRecentSessions').innerHTML = '';
      renderClassSeatingLayout_([]);
      if (!options.skipScroll) panel.scrollIntoView({ behavior:'smooth', block:'start' });
      try {
        const res = await callGasPromise_('getWungjiAttendanceDetail', currentIntegratedUser.id, currentIntegratedPassword, selectedWungjiCourse);
        if (!res.ok) {
          titleEl.innerText = res.message || '명렬표 미등록';
          subEl.innerText = res.message || '해당 수업의 웅지실 이용 학생 명단이 아직 등록되지 않았습니다.';
          document.getElementById('classAttendanceBody').innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" class="muted-empty">${escapeHtml(res.message || '명렬표 미등록')}</td></tr>`;
          if (seatSubEl) seatSubEl.innerText = '표시할 좌석 정보가 없습니다.';
          renderClassSeatingLayout_([]);
          return;
        }
        const sortedRows = sortClassRowsBySeat_(res.rows || []);
        const totalCount = sortedRows.length;
        titleEl.innerText = `${res.titleLabel || formatClassDateShort_(res.date)} 일과 중 웅지실 현황`;
        subEl.innerHTML = `<span class="class-attendance-date-line">${Number(res.period)}교시 ${escapeHtml(res.startTime || '')}~${escapeHtml(res.endTime || '')}</span><span class="class-attendance-count-line">${getClassAttendanceCountHtml_(res)}</span><span class="class-live-course-line">${escapeHtml(res.courseLabel || (res.course.subject + ' ' + res.course.classGroup + '반'))}</span>`;
        if (seatSubEl) seatSubEl.innerHTML = `<span class="class-attendance-date-line">${escapeHtml(res.titleLabel || formatClassDateShort_(res.date))} · ${Number(res.period)}교시 · ${escapeHtml(res.courseLabel || (res.course.subject + ' ' + res.course.classGroup + '반'))}</span>`;
        document.getElementById('classAttendanceBody').innerHTML = sortedRows.map(r => {
          const row = Object.assign({ date: res.date, period: Number(res.period), rosterKey: selectedWungjiCourse.rosterKey, subject: res.course.subject, classGroup: res.course.classGroup, teacher: res.course.teacher, courseLabel: res.course.subject + ' ' + res.course.classGroup + '반' }, r);
          const key = registerClassAttendanceAction_(row);
          return `<tr ${getWungjiRowDataAttrs_(row)}><td><strong>${escapeHtml(row.seatKey || '-')}</strong></td><td>${escapeHtml(row.id)}</td><td><button type="button" class="class-name-link" onclick="openWungjiAttendanceEditByKey_('${escapeHtml(key)}')">${escapeHtml(row.name)}</button></td><td>${escapeHtml(row.courseLabel || '-')}</td><td class="class-login-cell">${escapeHtml(row.loginTime || '-')}</td><td class="class-status-cell"><span class="${getClassStatusBadgeClass_(row.status)}">${escapeHtml(getClassStatusDisplay_(row.status))}</span></td></tr>`;
        }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="6" class="muted-empty">이 수업의 웅지실 이용 학생이 없습니다.</td></tr>';
        document.getElementById('classRecentSessions').innerHTML = (res.recent || []).map(s => `<button class="recent-session-card" type="button" onclick='openWungjiCourse(${JSON.stringify(s.date)},${s.period},${JSON.stringify(rosterKey)})'><strong>${escapeHtml(s.label)}</strong><span>웅지실 ${s.present}명 · 미로그인 ${s.absent}명 · 총 ${s.total}명</span></button>`).join('');
        renderClassSeatingLayout_(sortedRows.map(r => Object.assign({ date: res.date, period: Number(res.period), rosterKey: selectedWungjiCourse.rosterKey, subject: res.course.subject, classGroup: res.course.classGroup, teacher: res.course.teacher, courseLabel: res.course.subject + ' ' + res.course.classGroup + '반' }, r)));
      } catch (err) {
        document.getElementById('classAttendanceBody').innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" class="muted-empty text-danger">${escapeHtml(err.message)}</td></tr>`;
        if (seatSubEl) seatSubEl.innerText = '좌석 현황을 불러오지 못했습니다.';
        renderClassSeatingLayout_([]);
      }
    }

    function refreshSelectedClassAttendance() {
      if (selectedWungjiCourse) openWungjiCourse(selectedWungjiCourse.date, selectedWungjiCourse.period, selectedWungjiCourse.rosterKey);
    }

    function readWungjiFileAsArrayBuffer_(file) {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = e => resolve(e.target.result);
        reader.onerror = () => reject(new Error('파일을 읽지 못했습니다.'));
        reader.readAsArrayBuffer(file);
      });
    }

    function parseWungjiWorkbookBuffer_(buffer, displayName) {
      const wb = XLSX.read(buffer, { type:'array', cellDates:false, raw:false });
      const sheets = wb.SheetNames.map(name => ({
        name,
        rows:XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(wb.Sheets[name], { header:1, raw:false, defval:'', blankrows:true })
      }));
      return { fileName:displayName, sheets };
    }

    function isWungjiWorkbookName_(name) {
      return /\.(xlsx|xls)$/i.test(String(name || '')) && !/(^|\/)~\$/i.test(String(name || ''));
    }

    function isWungjiZipName_(name) {
      return /\.zip$/i.test(String(name || ''));
    }

    async function collectWungjiWorkbooks_(inputFiles) {
      const workbooks = [];
      const errors = [];
      for (const file of inputFiles) {
        try {
          if (isWungjiZipName_(file.name)) {
            const zip = await JSZip.loadAsync(await readWungjiFileAsArrayBuffer_(file));
            const entries = Object.values(zip.files).filter(entry =>
              !entry.dir && isWungjiWorkbookName_(entry.name) && !/(^|\/)__MACOSX\//i.test(entry.name)
            );
            if (!entries.length) {
              errors.push({ fileName:file.name, error:'ZIP 안에 XLS/XLSX 파일이 없습니다.' });
              continue;
            }
            for (const entry of entries) {
              try {
                const buffer = await entry.async('arraybuffer');
                workbooks.push(parseWungjiWorkbookBuffer_(buffer, `${file.name} > ${entry.name}`));
              } catch (err) {
                errors.push({ fileName:`${file.name} > ${entry.name}`, error:err.message || String(err) });
              }
            }
          } else if (isWungjiWorkbookName_(file.name)) {
            workbooks.push(parseWungjiWorkbookBuffer_(await readWungjiFileAsArrayBuffer_(file), file.name));
          } else {
            errors.push({ fileName:file.name, error:'지원하지 않는 파일 형식입니다.' });
          }
        } catch (err) {
          errors.push({ fileName:file.name, error:err.message || String(err) });
        }
      }
      return { workbooks, errors };
    }

    async function analyzeClassRosterFiles() {
      const files = Array.from(document.getElementById('classRosterFiles').files || []);
      if (!files.length) return setClassUploadStatus_('엑셀 또는 ZIP 파일을 선택하세요.', true);
      classUploadAnalyses = [];
      document.getElementById('classAnalyzeUploadBtn').disabled = true;
      document.getElementById('classApplyUploadBtn').disabled = true;
      setClassUploadStatus_('선택한 파일을 확인하고 있습니다.');
      try {
        const collected = await collectWungjiWorkbooks_(files);
        collected.errors.forEach(x => classUploadAnalyses.push({ fileName:x.fileName, ok:false, fatalError:x.error, items:[] }));
        if (!collected.workbooks.length) {
          renderClassUploadPreview_();
          return setClassUploadStatus_('분석할 XLS/XLSX 파일이 없습니다.', true);
        }
        for (let i = 0; i < collected.workbooks.length; i++) {
          const workbook = collected.workbooks[i];
          try {
            setClassUploadStatus_(`${i + 1}/${collected.workbooks.length} ${workbook.fileName} 분석 중...`);
            const analysis = await callGasPromise_('analyzeWungjiWorkbook', { mode:'subjectRoster', uploaderId:currentIntegratedUser.id, password:currentIntegratedPassword, fileName:workbook.fileName, sheets:workbook.sheets });
            classUploadAnalyses.push(analysis);
          } catch (err) {
            classUploadAnalyses.push({ fileName:workbook.fileName, ok:false, fatalError:err.message, items:[] });
          }
        }
        renderClassUploadPreview_();
        document.getElementById('classApplyUploadBtn').disabled = !classUploadAnalyses.some(a => !a.fatalError && (a.items || []).some(x => x.ok));
        setClassUploadStatus_(`분석 완료: 선택 ${files.length}개, 엑셀 ${collected.workbooks.length}개. 내용을 확인한 뒤 적용하세요.`);
      } finally {
        document.getElementById('classAnalyzeUploadBtn').disabled = false;
      }
    }

    function renderClassUploadPreview_() {
      const body = document.getElementById('classUploadPreviewBody');
      let html = '';
      classUploadAnalyses.forEach(a => {
        if (a.fatalError) {
          html += `<tr><td>${escapeHtml(a.fileName)}</td><td colspan="5">-</td><td class="text-danger fw-bold">${escapeHtml(a.fatalError)}</td></tr>`;
          return;
        }
        (a.items || []).forEach(item => {
          const excluded = Number(item.excludedDelegated || 0) + Number(item.excludedMissing || 0);
          html += `<tr><td>${escapeHtml(a.fileName)}</td><td>${escapeHtml(item.subject || '-')}</td><td>${item.classGroup ? item.classGroup + '반' : '-'}</td><td>${escapeHtml(item.teacher || '-')}</td><td>${item.studentCount || 0}</td><td>${excluded}</td><td class="${item.ok ? 'text-success' : 'text-danger'} fw-bold">${item.ok ? '정상' : escapeHtml(item.error || '오류')}</td></tr>`;
        });
      });
      body.innerHTML = html || '<tr><td colspan="7" class="muted-empty">분석 결과가 없습니다.</td></tr>';
      document.getElementById('classUploadPreviewWrap').style.display = 'block';
    }

    async function applyClassRosterFiles() {
      const targets = classUploadAnalyses.filter(a => !a.fatalError && (a.items || []).some(x => x.ok));
      if (!targets.length) return setClassUploadStatus_('적용할 정상 출석부가 없습니다.', true);
      document.getElementById('classApplyUploadBtn').disabled = true;
      document.getElementById('classAnalyzeUploadBtn').disabled = true;
      const messages = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < targets.length; i++) {
        try {
          setClassUploadStatus_(`${i + 1}/${targets.length} ${targets[i].fileName} 적용 중...`);
          const res = await callGasPromise_('applyWungjiAnalysis', { uploaderId:currentIntegratedUser.id, password:currentIntegratedPassword, analysis:targets[i] });
          messages.push(res.message || '적용 완료');
        } catch (err) { messages.push(`${targets[i].fileName}: ${err.message}`); }
      }
      setClassUploadStatus_(messages.join('\n'));
      document.getElementById('classAnalyzeUploadBtn').disabled = false;
      loadClassSchedule();
    }

    function setClassUploadStatus_(message, error) {
      const el = document.getElementById('classUploadStatus');
      el.innerText = message;
      el.className = 'result-box ' + (error ? 'text-danger' : 'text-primary');
    }

    async function loadWungjiAdminConfig() {
