      if (!currentIntegratedUser || currentIntegratedUser.role !== 'admin') return;
      const dateEl = document.getElementById('dateTimeOverrideDate');
      if (!dateEl.value) dateEl.value = document.getElementById('classScheduleDate').value || toLocalDateKey_(new Date());
      try {
        const res = await callGasPromise_('getWungjiAdminConfig', currentIntegratedUser.id, currentIntegratedPassword, dateEl.value);
        renderPeriodTimeGrid_('defaultPeriodTimeGrid', res.defaultRanges, 'defaultTime');
        renderPeriodTimeGrid_('datePeriodTimeGrid', res.dateRanges, 'dateTime');
        ['swapDateA','swapDateB','dayMapDate'].forEach(id => { const el=document.getElementById(id); if(el && !el.value) el.value=res.date; });
        setAdminSettingStatus_('관리자 설정을 불러왔습니다.');
      } catch (err) { setAdminSettingStatus_(err.message, true); }
    }

    function renderPeriodTimeGrid_(containerId, ranges, prefix) {
      const el = document.getElementById(containerId);
      ranges = ranges || {};
      el.innerHTML = Array.from({length:7}, (_,i) => i+1).map(p => {
        const item = ranges[p] || ranges[String(p)] || {};
        return `<div class="period-time-item">
          <div class="period-time-title">${p}교시</div>
          <div class="period-time-pair">
            <div class="period-time-field"><label>시작 시간</label><input type="time" class="form-control" id="${prefix}${p}Start" value="${escapeHtml(item.start || '')}"></div>
            <div class="period-time-field"><label>종료 시간</label><input type="time" class="form-control" id="${prefix}${p}End" value="${escapeHtml(item.end || '')}"></div>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    function collectPeriodTimes_(prefix) {
      const result = {};
      for (let p=1;p<=7;p++) result[p]={start:document.getElementById(prefix+p+'Start').value,end:document.getElementById(prefix+p+'End').value};
      return result;
    }

    function setAdminSettingStatus_(message,error){ const el=document.getElementById('classAdminSettingStatus'); el.innerText=message; el.className='result-box '+(error?'text-danger':'text-primary'); }


    function buildStatsData(data) {
      const reversedDates = [...(data.dates || [])].reverse();
      const statsData = [];

      (data.records || []).forEach(function(r) {
        let totalMins = 0;
        let attendCount = 0;

        reversedDates.forEach(function(d) {
          const time = r.attendance[d.full] || '-';
          if (time !== '-') {
            const parts = time.split(':');
            if (parts.length === 2) {
              totalMins += parseInt(parts[0], 10) * 60 + parseInt(parts[1], 10);
              attendCount++;
            }
          }
        });

        let avgStr = '-';
        let avgMins = Infinity;

        if (attendCount > 0) {
          avgMins = totalMins / attendCount;
          const avgH = Math.floor(avgMins / 60);
          const avgM = Math.floor(avgMins % 60);
          avgStr = `${String(avgH).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(avgM).padStart(2, '0')}`;
        }

        statsData.push({
          seat: r.seat,
          id: r.rawId,
          name: r.rawName,
          sixDayScore: r.sixDayScore || 0,
          avgMins: avgMins,
          avgStr: avgStr,
          attendCount: attendCount
        });
      });

      return statsData;
    }

    function renderPublicTop10(data) {
      const body = document.getElementById('publicTop10Body');
      const statsData = buildStatsData(data);

      const top10 = [...statsData]
        .filter(x => x.attendCount > 0)
        .sort((a, b) => (b.sixDayScore - a.sixDayScore) || (a.avgMins - b.avgMins))
        .slice(0, 15);

      if (top10.length === 0) {
        body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="muted-empty">데이터가 없습니다.</td></tr>';
        return;
      }

      let html = '';
      top10.forEach(function(x, i) {
        html += `
          <tr>
            <td><span class="rank-badge">${i + 1}</span></td>
            <td>${x.id}</td>
            <td><strong>${x.name}</strong></td>
            <td class="text-primary fw-bold">${x.avgStr}</td>
            <td class="fw-bold">${x.sixDayScore}</td>
          </tr>
        `;
      });

      body.innerHTML = html;
    }


    function applyPublicPanelOrder() {
      const nightPanel = document.getElementById('publicPreviousNightAbsencePanel');
      const top10Panel = document.getElementById('publicTop10Panel');
      if (!nightPanel || !top10Panel) return;

      const todayDate = new Date().getDate();
      if (todayDate % 2 === 0) {
        nightPanel.style.order = '2';
        top10Panel.style.order = '3';
      } else {
        top10Panel.style.order = '2';
        nightPanel.style.order = '3';
      }
    }

    function loadPublicPreviousNightAbsenceStatus() {
      const title = document.getElementById('publicPreviousNightAbsenceTitle');
      const body = document.getElementById('publicPreviousNightAbsenceBody');
      if (!title || !body) return;

      title.innerHTML = '<span>시행일 확인 중</span><br><span>미출결 현황</span>';
      body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty"><div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm me-2"></div>데이터를 불러오는 중입니다...</td></tr>';

      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
          res = res || {};
          const dateLabel = res.dateLabel || '최근';
          const rows = res.rows || [];
          title.innerHTML = dateLabel ? `${escapeHtml(dateLabel)}<br>미출결 현황(${rows.length}명)` : `미출결 현황(${rows.length}명)`;

          if (res.ok === false) {
            body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty">데이터를 불러오지 못했습니다.</td></tr>';
            return;
          }

          if (!rows.length) {
            if (res.message) {
              body.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty">${escapeHtml(res.message)}</td></tr>`;
            } else {
              body.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="4" class="public-night-success">🎉🎊👏 축하합니다! ✨🎈🏆<br>${escapeHtml(dateLabel)} 미출결자가 없습니다! 🎉🎊👏</td></tr>`;
            }
            return;
          }

          const sortedRows = [...rows].sort(function(a, b) {
            const idCompare = String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true });
            if (idCompare !== 0) return idCompare;
            return String(a.seat || '').localeCompare(String(b.seat || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true });
          });

          body.innerHTML = sortedRows.map(function(r) {
            return `<tr>
              <td>${escapeHtml(r.seat)}</td>
              <td>${escapeHtml(r.id)}</td>
              <td><strong class="${grade2NameClass_(r.id).trim()}">${escapeHtml(r.name)}</strong></td>
              <td class="text-danger fw-bold night-absence-date">${escapeHtml(r.dateTime)}</td>
            </tr>`;
          }).join('');
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function() {
          title.innerHTML = '<span>시행일 확인 실패</span><br><span>미출결 현황</span>';
          body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="muted-empty">데이터를 불러오지 못했습니다.</td></tr>';
        })
        .getPreviousNightAbsenceStatus();
    }

    function loadPublicTop10() {
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
          renderPublicTop10(data || { dates: [], records: [] });
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function() {
          document.getElementById('publicTop10Body').innerHTML =
            '<tr><td colspan="5" class="muted-empty">데이터를 불러오지 못했습니다.</td></tr>';
        })
        .getCumulativeStatus();
    }

    function loadCumulativeStatus() {
      if (!isAdminLoggedIn) return;

      const body = document.getElementById('cumulativeBody');
      body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="10" class="muted-empty"><div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm me-2"></div>데이터를 계산하여 불러오는 중입니다...</td></tr>';

      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
        const header = document.getElementById('cumulativeHeader');
        const reversedDates = [...(data.dates || [])].reverse();

        let headerHtml = `<tr>
          <th class="sticky-col-1">좌석</th>
          <th class="sticky-col-2">학번</th>
          <th class="sticky-col-3">이름</th>
          <th class="table-warning text-danger">총점</th>`;
        reversedDates.forEach(d => { headerHtml += `<th>${d.display}</th>`; });
        headerHtml += `</tr>`;
        header.innerHTML = headerHtml;

        if (!data.records || data.records.length === 0) {
          body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="10" class="muted-empty">등록된 학생 데이터가 없습니다.</td></tr>';
          document.getElementById('top10ArrivalBody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="muted-empty">데이터가 없습니다.</td></tr>';
          document.getElementById('bottom10ScoreBody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="muted-empty">데이터가 없습니다.</td></tr>';
          return;
        }

        let bodyHtml = '';
        const statsData = buildStatsData(data);

        data.records.forEach(function(r) {
          bodyHtml += `<tr>
            <td class="text-muted sticky-col-1">${r.seat}</td>
            <td class="text-muted sticky-col-2">${r.rawId}</td>
            <td class="sticky-col-3"><strong>${r.rawName}</strong></td>
            <td class="table-warning fw-bold text-danger fs-6">${r.totalScore}</td>`;

          reversedDates.forEach(function(d) {
            const time = r.attendance[d.full] || '-';
            const cellStyle = (time === '-') ? 'text-muted opacity-50' : 'fw-bold text-primary';
            bodyHtml += `<td class="${cellStyle}">${time}</td>`;
          });

          bodyHtml += `</tr>`;
        });

        body.innerHTML = bodyHtml;

        // 📌 테이블이 완전히 렌더링 된 후 (시간차를 넉넉하게 둠) 스크롤바와 틀고정 위치 재계산
        setTimeout(function() {
          const th1 = header.querySelector('.sticky-col-1');
          const th2 = header.querySelector('.sticky-col-2');
          if (th1 && th2) {
            const w1 = th1.getBoundingClientRect().width;
            const w2 = th2.getBoundingClientRect().width;
            document.querySelectorAll('.sticky-col-2').forEach(el => el.style.left = w1 + 'px');
            document.querySelectorAll('.sticky-col-3').forEach(el => el.style.left = (w1 + w2) + 'px');
          }
          refreshHorizontalScrollbars();
        }, 200);

        const top10 = [...statsData]
          .filter(x => x.attendCount > 0)
          .sort((a, b) => (b.sixDayScore - a.sixDayScore) || (a.avgMins - b.avgMins))
          .slice(0, 15);

        let top10Html = '';
        top10.forEach(function(x, i) {
          top10Html += `<tr>
            <td>${i + 1}</td>
            <td>${x.id}</td>
            <td>${x.name}</td>
            <td class="text-primary fw-bold">${x.avgStr}</td>
            <td class="fw-bold">${x.sixDayScore}</td>
          </tr>`;
        });
        if (top10.length === 0) top10Html = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="muted-empty">데이터가 없습니다.</td></tr>';
        document.getElementById('top10ArrivalBody').innerHTML = top10Html;

        const bottom10 = [...statsData]
          .sort((a, b) => (a.sixDayScore - b.sixDayScore) || (a.avgMins - b.avgMins))
          .slice(0, 10);

        let bottom10Html = '';
        bottom10.forEach(function(x, i) {
          bottom10Html += `<tr>
            <td>${i + 1}</td>
            <td>${x.id}</td>
            <td>${x.name}</td>
            <td>${x.avgStr}</td>
            <td class="text-danger fw-bold">${x.sixDayScore}</td>
          </tr>`;
        });
        if (bottom10.length === 0) bottom10Html = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="muted-empty">데이터가 없습니다.</td></tr>';
        document.getElementById('bottom10ScoreBody').innerHTML = bottom10Html;
      }).getCumulativeStatus();
    }
  </script>
  <button class="floating-mode-switch" id="floatingModeSwitchBtn" type="button" onclick="switchAdminMode()">야간자습으로 이동</button>
</body>
</html>

<code4>
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <base target="_top">
  <meta charset="utf-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
  <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/xlsx@0.18.5/dist/xlsx.full.min.js"></script>
  <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/jszip@3.10.1/dist/jszip.min.js"></script>
  <style>
    :root { --primary:#2957ff; --line:#e5eaf2; --muted:#6b7684; --bg:#f4f7fb; }
    * { box-sizing:border-box; }
    body { margin:0; padding:20px; font-family:'Apple SD Gothic Neo','Noto Sans KR',sans-serif; color:#17212f; background:var(--bg); }
    .card { background:#fff; border:1px solid var(--line); border-radius:18px; padding:18px; margin-bottom:14px; }
    h1 { font-size:1.25rem; margin:0 0 14px; }
    .grid { display:grid; grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr; gap:10px; }
    label { display:block; font-size:.86rem; font-weight:800; margin-bottom:6px; }
    input, button { width:100%; min-height:44px; border-radius:12px; border:1px solid #dce4ef; padding:9px 12px; font-size:.95rem; }
    button { border:0; background:var(--primary); color:#fff; font-weight:900; cursor:pointer; }
    button.secondary { background:#fff; color:#17212f; border:1px solid var(--line); }
    button:disabled { opacity:.55; cursor:not-allowed; }
    .help { color:var(--muted); font-size:.82rem; margin-top:8px; line-height:1.5; }
    .status { font-weight:800; min-height:24px; margin-top:10px; white-space:pre-line; }
    .table-wrap { overflow:auto; max-height:330px; border:1px solid var(--line); border-radius:14px; }
    table { width:100%; border-collapse:collapse; background:#fff; font-size:.84rem; }
    th, td { border-bottom:1px solid var(--line); padding:9px 8px; text-align:center; white-space:nowrap; }
    th { position:sticky; top:0; background:#f7f9fc; z-index:1; }
    .ok { color:#16803f; font-weight:900; }
    .error { color:#c44141; font-weight:900; }
    .actions { display:grid; grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr; gap:10px; margin-top:12px; }
    @media(max-width:600px){ .grid,.actions{grid-template-columns:1fr;} body{padding:12px;} }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="card">
    <h1><?= dialogTitle ?></h1>
    <div class="grid">
      <div>
        <label>아이디</label>
        <input id="userId" value="admin" autocomplete="username">
      </div>
      <div>
        <label>비밀번호</label>
        <input id="password" type="password" inputmode="numeric" autocomplete="current-password" value="17752">
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:12px;">
      <label>엑셀 또는 ZIP 파일 선택</label>
      <input id="files" type="file" accept=".xlsx,.xls,.zip" multiple>
      <div class="help">엑셀 파일 여러 개 또는 ZIP 파일을 함께 선택할 수 있습니다. ZIP 안의 XLS/XLSX 파일을 자동으로 풀어 분석합니다.</div>
    </div>
    <div class="actions">
      <button id="analyzeBtn" type="button" onclick="analyzeFiles()">파일 분석</button>
      <button id="applyBtn" class="secondary" type="button" onclick="applyAll()" disabled>분석 결과 적용</button>
    </div>
    <div class="status" id="status"></div>
  </div>

  <div class="card" id="previewCard" style="display:none;">
    <div class="table-wrap">
      <table>
        <thead><tr><th>파일</th><th>과목/구분</th><th>수업반</th><th>담당교사</th><th>학생</th><th>제외</th><th>결과</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody id="previewBody"></tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  </div>

<script>
  const uploadMode = '<?= uploadMode ?>';
  let analyses = [];

  function escapeHtml(value) {
    return String(value == null ? '' : value).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/'/g,'&#039;');
  }

  function readFileAsArrayBuffer(file) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = e => resolve(e.target.result);
      reader.onerror = () => reject(new Error('파일을 읽지 못했습니다.'));
      reader.readAsArrayBuffer(file);
    });
  }

  function parseWorkbookBuffer(buffer, displayName) {
    const wb = XLSX.read(buffer, { type:'array', cellDates:false, raw:false });
    const sheets = wb.SheetNames.map(name => ({
      name,
      rows: XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(wb.Sheets[name], { header:1, raw:false, defval:'', blankrows:true })
    }));
    return { fileName:displayName, sheets };
  }

  function isWorkbookName(name) {
    return /\.(xlsx|xls)$/i.test(String(name || '')) && !/(^|\/)~\$/i.test(String(name || ''));
  }

  function isZipName(name) {
    return /\.zip$/i.test(String(name || ''));
  }

  async function collectWorkbooks(inputFiles) {
    const workbooks = [];
    const errors = [];

    for (const file of inputFiles) {
      try {
        if (isZipName(file.name)) {
          const zip = await JSZip.loadAsync(await readFileAsArrayBuffer(file));
          const entries = Object.values(zip.files).filter(entry =>
            !entry.dir && isWorkbookName(entry.name) && !/(^|\/)__MACOSX\//i.test(entry.name)
          );
          if (!entries.length) {
            errors.push({ fileName:file.name, error:'ZIP 안에 XLS/XLSX 파일이 없습니다.' });
            continue;
          }
          for (const entry of entries) {
            try {
              const buffer = await entry.async('arraybuffer');
              workbooks.push(parseWorkbookBuffer(buffer, `${file.name} > ${entry.name}`));
            } catch (err) {
              errors.push({ fileName:`${file.name} > ${entry.name}`, error:err.message || String(err) });
            }
          }
        } else if (isWorkbookName(file.name)) {
          workbooks.push(parseWorkbookBuffer(await readFileAsArrayBuffer(file), file.name));
        } else {
          errors.push({ fileName:file.name, error:'지원하지 않는 파일 형식입니다.' });
        }
      } catch (err) {
        errors.push({ fileName:file.name, error:err.message || String(err) });
      }
    }
    return { workbooks, errors };
  }

  function callServer(functionName, payload) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(resolve).withFailureHandler(err => reject(new Error(err && err.message ? err.message : String(err))))[functionName](payload);
    });
  }

  async function analyzeFiles() {
    const fileInput = document.getElementById('files');
    const files = Array.from(fileInput.files || []);
    const userId = document.getElementById('userId').value.trim();
    const password = document.getElementById('password').value;
    if (!files.length) return setStatus('엑셀 또는 ZIP 파일을 선택하세요.', true);
    analyses = [];
    document.getElementById('analyzeBtn').disabled = true;
    document.getElementById('applyBtn').disabled = true;
    setStatus('선택한 파일을 확인하고 있습니다...');

    try {
      const collected = await collectWorkbooks(files);
      collected.errors.forEach(x => analyses.push({ mode:uploadMode, fileName:x.fileName, ok:false, fatalError:x.error, items:[] }));
      if (!collected.workbooks.length) {
        renderPreview();
        setStatus('분석할 XLS/XLSX 파일이 없습니다.', true);
        return;
      }
      for (let i = 0; i < collected.workbooks.length; i++) {
        const workbook = collected.workbooks[i];
        try {
          setStatus(`${i + 1}/${collected.workbooks.length} ${workbook.fileName} 분석 중...`);
          const analysis = await callServer('analyzeWungjiWorkbook', { mode:uploadMode, uploaderId:userId, password, fileName:workbook.fileName, sheets:workbook.sheets });
          analyses.push(analysis);
        } catch (err) {
          analyses.push({ mode:uploadMode, fileName:workbook.fileName, ok:false, fatalError:err.message, items:[] });
        }
      }
      renderPreview();
      const applicable = analyses.some(a => a.ok !== false || (a.items || []).some(x => x.ok));
      document.getElementById('applyBtn').disabled = !applicable;
      setStatus(`분석 완료: 선택 ${files.length}개, 엑셀 ${collected.workbooks.length}개`);
    } finally {
      document.getElementById('analyzeBtn').disabled = false;
    }
  }

  function renderPreview() {
    const body = document.getElementById('previewBody');
    let html = '';
    analyses.forEach(a => {
      if (a.fatalError) {
        html += `<tr><td>${escapeHtml(a.fileName)}</td><td colspan="5">-</td><td class="error">${escapeHtml(a.fatalError)}</td></tr>`;
        return;
      }
      if (a.mode === 'subjectRoster') {
        (a.items || []).forEach(item => {
          const excluded = Number(item.excludedDelegated || 0) + Number(item.excludedMissing || 0);
          html += `<tr><td>${escapeHtml(a.fileName)}</td><td>${escapeHtml(item.subject || '-')}</td><td>${item.classGroup ? item.classGroup + '반' : '-'}</td><td>${escapeHtml(item.teacher || '-')}</td><td>${item.studentCount || 0}</td><td>${excluded}</td><td class="${item.ok ? 'ok' : 'error'}">${item.ok ? '정상' : escapeHtml(item.error || '오류')}</td></tr>`;
        });
      } else if (a.mode === 'applicantRoster') {
        const s = a.summary || {};
        const excluded = Number(s.excludedMissing || 0) + Number(s.excludedWithdrawn || 0) + Number(s.invalidSeatCount || 0);
        const detail = a.ok
          ? `정상 · 개방 ${Number(s.openCount || 0)}명 / 폐쇄 ${Number(s.closedCount || 0)}명`
          : escapeHtml((a.errors || []).slice(0, 2).join(' / ') || '좌석 또는 학생 정보를 확인하세요.');
        html += `<tr><td>${escapeHtml(a.fileName)}</td><td>${escapeHtml(s.title || '신청자 명렬표')}</td><td>-</td><td>-</td><td>${Number(s.studentCount || 0)}</td><td>${excluded}</td><td class="${a.ok ? 'ok' : 'error'}">${detail}</td></tr>`;
      } else {
        const s = a.summary || {};
        const count = s.studentCount || s.recordCount || 0;
        const excluded = Number(s.excludedDelegated || 0) + Number(s.excludedWithdrawn || 0);
        html += `<tr><td>${escapeHtml(a.fileName)}</td><td>${escapeHtml(s.title || a.mode)}</td><td>-</td><td>-</td><td>${count}</td><td>${excluded}</td><td class="${a.ok ? 'ok' : 'error'}">${a.ok ? '정상' : '확인 필요'}</td></tr>`;
      }
    });
    body.innerHTML = html || '<tr><td colspan="7">분석 결과가 없습니다.</td></tr>';
    document.getElementById('previewCard').style.display = 'block';
  }

  async function applyAll() {
    const userId = document.getElementById('userId').value.trim();
    const password = document.getElementById('password').value;
    const targets = analyses.filter(a => !a.fatalError && (a.ok !== false || (a.items || []).some(x => x.ok)));
    if (!targets.length) return setStatus('적용할 정상 분석 결과가 없습니다.', true);
    document.getElementById('applyBtn').disabled = true;
    document.getElementById('analyzeBtn').disabled = true;
    const messages = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < targets.length; i++) {
      try {
        setStatus(`${i + 1}/${targets.length} ${targets[i].fileName} 적용 중...`);
        const res = await callServer('applyWungjiAnalysis', { uploaderId:userId, password, analysis:targets[i] });
        messages.push(res.message || '적용 완료');
      } catch (err) {
        messages.push(`${targets[i].fileName}: ${err.message}`);
      }
    }
    setStatus(messages.join('\n'));
    document.getElementById('analyzeBtn').disabled = false;
  }

  function setStatus(message, error) {
    const el = document.getElementById('status');
    el.textContent = message;
    el.className = 'status ' + (error ? 'error' : '');
  }
</script>
</body>
</html>


<code5>
/**
 * 일과 중 웅지실 출석 모듈
 * 기존 자투리/야간 모듈과 분리하여 같은 웹앱 안에서 동작합니다.
 */
const WUNGJI_PASSWORD = '17752';
const WUNGJI_SETTINGS_SHEET = '웅지실 설정';
const WUNGJI_FULL_ROSTER_SHEET = '웅지실 전체명렬';
const WUNGJI_APPLICANT_ROSTER_SHEET = '웅지실 신청자명렬';
const WUNGJI_TIMETABLE_SHEET = '웅지실 시간표';
const WUNGJI_TEACHER_SUBJECT_SHEET = '교사-과목';
const WUNGJI_SUBJECT_ROSTER_SHEET = '웅지실 과목명렬';
const WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_LOG_SHEET = '웅지실 출석로그';
const WUNGJI_OVERRIDE_SHEET = '웅지실 시간표변경';
const WUNGJI_DATE_TIME_SHEET = '웅지실 교시시간변경';
const WUNGJI_UPLOAD_LOG_SHEET = '웅지실 업로드로그';
const WUNGJI_ERROR_LOG_SHEET = '웅지실 오류로그';
const WUNGJI_WEEKLY_CUMULATIVE_PREFIX = '일과통계';
const WUNGJI_WEEKLY_STAT_START_DATE = '2026-07-07';
const WUNGJI_WEEKLY_CUMULATIVE_BASE_HEADERS = ['학번', '이름'];
const WUNGJI_STATUS_PRESENT = '출석';
const WUNGJI_STATUS_CLASS = '수업참석';
const WUNGJI_STATUS_ABSENT = '미로그인';
const WUNGJI_CLASS_MARK_PREFIX = '(수)';

const WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS = ['', '월', '화', '수', '목', '금'];
const WUNGJI_DEFAULT_PERIOD_TIMES = {
  1: '09:05',
  2: '10:05',
  3: '11:05',
  4: '12:05',
  5: '13:55',
  6: '14:55',
  7: '15:55'
};

const WUNGJI_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS = {
  1: '윤혜영,유제호',
  2: '이진순,유미란',
  3: '노석완,박소연',
  4: '홍상호,이석찬',
  5: '장현,오중석',
  6: '고승범,김낙은',
  7: '이주현,이기모',
  8: '김희정,김대기'
};

const WUNGJI_CACHE_PREFIX = 'w7_';
const WUNGJI_STATIC_CACHE_SECONDS = 21600;
const WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS = 600;
const WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_CACHE_SECONDS = 900;
let WUNGJI_REVISION_MEMO = '';

function getWungjiEffectiveTeacherName_(teacher, dateKey) {
  const name = String(teacher || '').replace(/\s+/g, '').trim();
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date());
  if (name === '박소연' && date && date >= '2026-08-01') return '김진범';
  return name;
}

function getWungjiTeacherAliasForMatch_(teacher) {
  const name = String(teacher || '').replace(/\s+/g, '').trim();
  if (name === '김진범') return '박소연';
  return name;
}

function getWungjiEffectiveTeacherListForDate_(teacherList, dateKey) {
  const list = normalizeWungjiTeacherList_(teacherList).split(',').map(t => getWungjiEffectiveTeacherName_(t, dateKey)).filter(Boolean);
  const unique = {};
  list.forEach(t => unique[t] = true);
  return Object.keys(unique).sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'ko')).join(',');
}

function getWungjiSpecialFridayTeachersForClass_(classNo, dateKey) {
  return getWungjiEffectiveTeacherListForDate_(WUNGJI_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS[Number(classNo)] || '', dateKey);
}

function getWungjiStudentClassNo_(studentId) {
  const id = String(studentId || '').replace(/\D/g, '');
  if (id.length >= 3) return Number(id.charAt(1)) || 0;
  return 0;
}

function getWungjiEffectiveStudentName_(studentId, name) {
  const id = normalizeWungjiStudentId_(studentId);
  const cleaned = cleanWungjiStudentName_(name);
  if (id === '3409') return '이서령';
  return cleaned;
}

function makeWungjiSpecialFridayRosterKey_(classGroup) {
  return 'SPECIAL_FRIDAY_CREATIVE|' + Number(classGroup || 0);
}

function isWungjiSpecialFridayRosterKey_(rosterKey) {
  return String(rosterKey || '').indexOf('SPECIAL_FRIDAY_CREATIVE|') === 0;
}

function getWungjiSpecialFridayClassFromRosterKey_(rosterKey) {
  const m = String(rosterKey || '').match(/^SPECIAL_FRIDAY_CREATIVE\|(\d+)$/);
  return m ? Number(m[1]) : 0;
}

function getWungjiRevision_() {
  if (WUNGJI_REVISION_MEMO) return WUNGJI_REVISION_MEMO;
  WUNGJI_REVISION_MEMO = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('WUNGJI_DATA_REVISION') || '1';
  return WUNGJI_REVISION_MEMO;
}

function bumpWungjiRevision_() {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const next = String((Number(props.getProperty('WUNGJI_DATA_REVISION')) || 1) + 1);
  props.setProperty('WUNGJI_DATA_REVISION', next);
  WUNGJI_REVISION_MEMO = next;
  try { CacheService.getScriptCache().remove(WUNGJI_CACHE_PREFIX + 'teacher_names'); } catch (_) {}
  return next;
}

function wungjiHash_(value) {
  const bytes = Utilities.computeDigest(Utilities.DigestAlgorithm.MD5, String(value || ''), Utilities.Charset.UTF_8);
  return bytes.map(b => (b & 255).toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('').slice(0, 20);
}

function getWungjiCacheJson_(key) {
  try {
    const raw = CacheService.getScriptCache().get(WUNGJI_CACHE_PREFIX + key);
    return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null;
  } catch (_) {
    return null;
  }
}

function putWungjiCacheJson_(key, value, seconds) {
  try {
    const raw = JSON.stringify(value);
    if (raw.length < 95000) CacheService.getScriptCache().put(WUNGJI_CACHE_PREFIX + key, raw, seconds || WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
  } catch (_) {}
  return value;
}

function removeWungjiCache_(key) {
  try { CacheService.getScriptCache().remove(WUNGJI_CACHE_PREFIX + key); } catch (_) {}
}

function getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_(name, suffix) {
  return getWungjiRevision_() + '_' + name + (suffix ? '_' + suffix : '');
}


function ensureWungjiCoreSheets_() {
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_SETTINGS_SHEET, ['설정키', '설정값', '설명'], false);
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_FULL_ROSTER_SHEET, ['학번', '이름', '반', '번호', '원본표기', '업로드일시'], false);
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_APPLICANT_ROSTER_SHEET, ['버전', '현재버전', '업로드일시', '학번', '이름', '좌석형태', '좌석번호', '좌석키', '사용여부', '원본파일'], false);
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_TIMETABLE_SHEET, ['요일번호', '요일', '교시', '수업반', '과목명', '과목키', '담당교사', '원본'], false);
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_TEACHER_SUBJECT_SHEET, ['과목명', '교사명'], false);
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_SUBJECT_ROSTER_SHEET, ['명렬키', '버전', '현재버전', '업로드일시', '담당교사', '과목명', '과목키', '수업반', '학번', '이름', '사용여부', '제외사유', '원본파일', '원본시트'], false);
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_LOG_SHEET, ['기록키', '날짜', '요일', '교시', '수업반', '과목명', '과목키', '담당교사', '명렬키', '학번', '이름', '로그인시간', '상태', '처리구분'], true);
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_OVERRIDE_SHEET, ['날짜', '유형', '기준요일', '수업반', '교시', '과목명', '과목키', '담당교사', '수정일시'], false);
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_DATE_TIME_SHEET, ['날짜', '교시', '시작시간', '종료시간', '수정일시'], false);
  migrateWungjiDateTimeSheet_();
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_UPLOAD_LOG_SHEET, ['업로드일시', '업로더', '구분', '파일명', '처리결과', '상세'], true);
  ensureWungjiSheet_(WUNGJI_ERROR_LOG_SHEET, ['발생일시', '구분', '학번', '내용', '상세'], true);
  applyWungjiStudentNameAliases_();
  seedWungjiSettings_();
  ensureWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetForDate_(new Date(), false);
}

function ensureWungjiSheet_(name, headers, hidden) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name) || ss.insertSheet(name);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() === 0) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
  } else {
    const current = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, Math.max(headers.length, sheet.getLastColumn())).getDisplayValues()[0];
    const mismatch = headers.some((h, i) => current[i] !== h);
    if (mismatch) sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
  }
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#eef3ff');
  if (hidden) {
    try { sheet.hideSheet(); } catch (_) {}
  }
  return sheet;
}

function applyWungjiStudentNameAliases_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const targets = [
    { sheet: WUNGJI_FULL_ROSTER_SHEET, idCol: 1, nameCol: 2 },
    { sheet: WUNGJI_APPLICANT_ROSTER_SHEET, idCol: 4, nameCol: 5 },
    { sheet: WUNGJI_SUBJECT_ROSTER_SHEET, idCol: 9, nameCol: 10 },
    { sheet: WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_LOG_SHEET, idCol: 10, nameCol: 11 }
  ];
  let changed = false;
  targets.forEach(t => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(t.sheet);
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;
    const rowCount = sheet.getLastRow() - 1;
    const ids = sheet.getRange(2, t.idCol, rowCount, 1).getDisplayValues();
    const names = sheet.getRange(2, t.nameCol, rowCount, 1).getDisplayValues();
    let localChanged = false;
    const out = names.map((r, i) => {
      const id = normalizeWungjiStudentId_(ids[i][0]);
      const next = getWungjiEffectiveStudentName_(id, r[0]);
      if (next && next !== r[0]) {
        localChanged = true;
        changed = true;
        return [next];
      }
      return [r[0]];
    });
    if (localChanged) sheet.getRange(2, t.nameCol, rowCount, 1).setValues(out);
  });
  if (changed) {
    bumpWungjiRevision_();
  }
}

function seedWungjiSettings_() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_SETTINGS_SHEET);
  const existing = {};
  if (sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getDisplayValues().forEach(r => {
      if (r[0]) existing[String(r[0]).trim()] = r[1];
    });
  }
  const rows = [];
  Object.keys(WUNGJI_DEFAULT_PERIOD_TIMES).forEach(p => {
    const startKey = 'PERIOD_' + p + '_START';
    const endKey = 'PERIOD_' + p + '_END';
    const start = WUNGJI_DEFAULT_PERIOD_TIMES[p];
    if (!existing[startKey]) rows.push([startKey, start, p + '교시 기본 시작시간']);
    if (!existing[endKey]) rows.push([endKey, addWungjiMinutes_(start, 50), p + '교시 기본 종료시간']);
  });
  if (!existing.CLASS_DURATION_MINUTES) rows.push(['CLASS_DURATION_MINUTES', '50', '기존 설정 호환용 수업 시간(분)']);
  if (!existing.ATTENDANCE_EARLY_MINUTES) rows.push(['ATTENDANCE_EARLY_MINUTES', '3', '시작 전 QR 출석 허용 시간(분)']);
  if (!existing.ATTENDANCE_LATE_MINUTES) rows.push(['ATTENDANCE_LATE_MINUTES', '9', '시작 후 출석 허용 시간(분)']);
  if (!existing.ATTENDANCE_RESET_BEFORE_BELL_MINUTES) rows.push(['ATTENDANCE_RESET_BEFORE_BELL_MINUTES', '5', '종 치기 전 다음 교시 현황으로 전환할 시간(분)']);
  if (!existing.WUNGJI_STATS_START_DATE) rows.push(['WUNGJI_STATS_START_DATE', WUNGJI_WEEKLY_STAT_START_DATE, '일과통계 첫 운영 시작일']);
  if (rows.length) sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, rows.length, 3).setValues(rows);
  enforceWungjiAttendanceTimingSettings_(sheet);
}

function enforceWungjiAttendanceTimingSettings_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_SETTINGS_SHEET);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;
  const fixed = {
    ATTENDANCE_EARLY_MINUTES: ['3', '시작 전 QR 출석 허용 시간(분)'],
    ATTENDANCE_LATE_MINUTES: ['9', '시작 후 출석 허용 시간(분)'],
    ATTENDANCE_RESET_BEFORE_BELL_MINUTES: ['5', '종 치기 전 다음 교시 현황으로 전환할 시간(분)']
  };
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, Math.max(3, sheet.getLastColumn())).getValues();
  const found = {};
  values.forEach((row, i) => {
    const key = String(row[0] || '').trim();
    if (!fixed[key]) return;
    found[key] = true;
    sheet.getRange(i + 2, 2, 1, 2).setValues([fixed[key]]);
  });
  const missing = Object.keys(fixed).filter(k => !found[k]).map(k => [k].concat(fixed[k]));
  if (missing.length) sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, missing.length, 3).setValues(missing);
}



function migrateWungjiDateTimeSheet_() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_DATE_TIME_SHEET);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;
  const rowCount = sheet.getLastRow() - 1;
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, rowCount, Math.max(5, sheet.getLastColumn())).getValues();
  const output = values.map(row => {
    const date = row[0];
    const period = row[1];
    const start = normalizeWungjiTime_(row[2]);
    const oldModified = row[3] instanceof Date ? row[3] : null;
    const possibleEnd = oldModified ? '' : normalizeWungjiTime_(row[3]);
    const modified = row[4] || oldModified || new Date();
    const end = possibleEnd || (start ? addWungjiMinutes_(start, 50) : '');
    return [date, period, start, end, modified];
  });
  sheet.getRange(2, 1, rowCount, 5).setValues(output);
  if (sheet.getLastColumn() > 5) sheet.getRange(2, 6, rowCount, sheet.getLastColumn() - 5).clearContent();
}

function showWungjiFullRosterUploadDialog() {
  showWungjiUploadDialog_('fullRoster', '3학년 전체 명렬표 업로드');
}

}

  showWungjiUploadDialog_('timetable', '3학년 시간표 업로드');
}

  showWungjiUploadDialog_('subjectRoster', '과목별 웅지실 출석부 업로드');
}

function showWungjiUploadDialog_(mode, title) {
  const template = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('upload');
  template.uploadMode = mode;
  template.dialogTitle = title;
  const html = template.evaluate().setWidth(900).setHeight(650);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, title);
}

function authenticateIntegratedUser(userId, password, mode) {
  const id = String(userId || '').trim();
  if (!id || String(password || '') !== WUNGJI_PASSWORD) {
    return { ok: false, message: '아이디 또는 비밀번호가 올바르지 않습니다.' };
  }
  if (id.toLowerCase() === 'admin') {
    return { ok: true, role: 'admin', id: 'admin', displayName: '관리자', mode: mode || 'jaturi' };
  }
  const teachers = getWungjiTeacherNames_();
  if (teachers.indexOf(id) === -1) {
    return { ok: false, message: '등록된 교사 아이디가 아닙니다. 시간표 또는 교사-과목 탭을 확인하세요.' };
  }
  return { ok: true, role: 'teacher', id: id, displayName: id + ' 선생님', mode: mode || 'jaturi' };
}


function loginIntegratedFast(userId, password, mode, dateKey, inspectTeacher) {
  const auth = authenticateIntegratedUser(userId, password, mode);
  if (!auth.ok) return { ok: false, auth: auth };
  if (String(mode || '') !== 'class') return { ok: true, auth: auth };
  let target = auth.role === 'admin' ? String(inspectTeacher || '').trim() : auth.id;
  if (auth.role === 'admin' && !target) {
    const teachers = getWungjiTeacherNames_();
    target = teachers.length ? teachers[0] : '';
  }
  const schedule = getTeacherWungjiSchedule(userId, password, dateKey || new Date(), target);
  return { ok: true, auth: auth, schedule: schedule };
}

function verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, requireAdmin) {
  const auth = authenticateIntegratedUser(userId, password, 'class');
  if (!auth.ok) throw new Error(auth.message);
  if (requireAdmin && auth.role !== 'admin') throw new Error('관리자만 사용할 수 있는 기능입니다.');
  return auth;
}

function getWungjiTeacherNames_() {
  const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_('teacher_names');
  if (cached) return cached;
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(WUNGJI_TEACHER_SUBJECT_SHEET);
  const names = {};
  if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 2, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getDisplayValues().forEach(r => {
      String(r[0] || '').split(',').map(x => x.trim()).filter(Boolean).forEach(x => names[x] = true);
    });
  }
  Object.keys(WUNGJI_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS).forEach(k => {
    WUNGJI_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS[k].split(',').forEach(x => {
      const name = String(x || '').trim();
      if (name) names[name] = true;
      const changed = getWungjiEffectiveTeacherName_(name, '2026-08-01');
      if (changed) names[changed] = true;
    });
  });
  return putWungjiCacheJson_('teacher_names', Object.keys(names).sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'ko')), WUNGJI_STATIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function analyzeWungjiWorkbook(request) {
  ensureWungjiCoreSheets_();
  request = request || {};
  const mode = String(request.mode || 'subjectRoster');
  const requireAdmin = mode !== 'subjectRoster';
  const auth = verifyWungjiCredentials_(request.uploaderId || 'admin', request.password || '', requireAdmin);
  const payload = sanitizeWorkbookPayload_(request);
  let analysis;
  if (mode === 'fullRoster') analysis = analyzeWungjiFullRoster_(payload);
  else if (mode === 'applicantRoster') analysis = analyzeWungjiApplicantRoster_(payload);
  else if (mode === 'timetable') analysis = analyzeWungjiTimetable_(payload);
  else analysis = analyzeWungjiSubjectRosters_(payload, auth);
  analysis.mode = mode;
  analysis.fileName = payload.fileName;
  analysis.uploader = auth.id;
  return analysis;
}

function sanitizeWorkbookPayload_(request) {
  const sheets = (request.sheets || []).map(s => ({
    name: String(s.name || 'Sheet1').slice(0, 100),
    rows: (s.rows || []).slice(0, 3000).map(row => (row || []).slice(0, 100).map(v => String(v == null ? '' : v).slice(0, 1000)))
  }));
  if (!sheets.length) throw new Error('읽을 수 있는 시트가 없습니다.');
  return { fileName: String(request.fileName || '업로드파일').slice(0, 250), sheets: sheets };
}

function applyWungjiAnalysis(request) {
  ensureWungjiCoreSheets_();
  request = request || {};
  const analysis = request.analysis || {};
  const mode = String(analysis.mode || request.mode || 'subjectRoster');
  const auth = verifyWungjiCredentials_(request.uploaderId || analysis.uploader || 'admin', request.password || '', mode !== 'subjectRoster');
  let result;
  if (mode === 'fullRoster') result = applyWungjiFullRoster_(analysis, auth);
  else if (mode === 'applicantRoster') result = applyWungjiApplicantRoster_(analysis, auth);
  else if (mode === 'timetable') result = applyWungjiTimetable_(analysis, auth);
  else result = applyWungjiSubjectRosters_(analysis, auth);
  bumpWungjiRevision_();
  refreshWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetForDate_(new Date());
  appendWungjiUploadLog_(auth.id, mode, analysis.fileName || '', result.ok ? '완료' : '오류', result.message || '');
  return result;
}

function analyzeWungjiFullRoster_(payload) {
  const extracted = [];
  let excludedDelegated = 0;
  let excludedWithdrawn = 0;
  payload.sheets.forEach(s => {
    extractWungjiStudentsFromSheet_(s.rows).forEach(st => {
      if (st.delegated) { excludedDelegated++; return; }
      if (st.id === '3728') { excludedWithdrawn++; return; }
      extracted.push(st);
    });
  });
  const unique = {};
  extracted.forEach(st => unique[st.id] = st);
  const students = Object.keys(unique).sort().map(id => unique[id]);
  if (!students.length) throw new Error('전체 명렬표에서 학생을 찾지 못했습니다.');
  return {
    ok: true,
    students: students,
    summary: {
      title: '전체 명렬표',
      studentCount: students.length,
      excludedDelegated: excludedDelegated,
      excludedWithdrawn: excludedWithdrawn
    }
  };
}

function applyWungjiFullRoster_(analysis, auth) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_FULL_ROSTER_SHEET);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() > 1) sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 6).clearContent();
  const now = new Date();
  const rows = (analysis.students || []).map(st => [st.id, st.name, st.classNo, st.number, st.rawName || st.name, now]);
  if (!rows.length) throw new Error('적용할 학생이 없습니다.');
  sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, 6).setValues(rows);
  bumpWungjiRevision_();
  reconcileWungjiSubjectRostersWithFullRoster_();
  reconcileWungjiApplicantRosterWithFullRoster_();
  return { ok: true, message: '전체 명렬표 ' + rows.length + '명을 적용했습니다.', count: rows.length };
}


function analyzeWungjiApplicantRoster_(payload) {
  const fullRoster = getWungjiFullRosterMap_();
  if (!Object.keys(fullRoster).length) throw new Error('먼저 3학년 전체 명렬표를 업로드하세요.');

  const applicants = {};
  const seatOwners = {};
  const errors = [];
  let excludedMissing = 0;
  let excludedWithdrawn = 0;
  let correctedNames = 0;
  let invalidSeatCount = 0;
  let recognizedSheetCount = 0;

  payload.sheets.forEach(sheetData => {
    const rows = sheetData.rows || [];
    let headerRow = -1;
    let idCol = -1;
    let nameCol = -1;
    let seatTypeCol = -1;
    let seatNoCol = -1;

    for (let r = 0; r < Math.min(rows.length, 40); r++) {
      const headers = (rows[r] || []).map(v => normalizeWungjiHeader_(v));
      headers.forEach((h, c) => {
        if (h === '학번') idCol = c;
        if (h === '이름' || h === '성명') nameCol = c;
        if (h === '희망좌석' || h === '좌석형태' || h === '좌석구분') seatTypeCol = c;
        if (h === '좌석번호' || h === '번호') seatNoCol = c;
      });
      if (idCol >= 0 && nameCol >= 0 && seatTypeCol >= 0 && seatNoCol >= 0) {
        headerRow = r;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (headerRow < 0) return;
    recognizedSheetCount++;

    for (let r = headerRow + 1; r < rows.length; r++) {
      const row = rows[r] || [];
      const id = normalizeWungjiStudentId_(row[idCol]);
      if (!id) continue;
      if (id === '3728') { excludedWithdrawn++; continue; }

      const canonical = fullRoster[id];
      if (!canonical) {
        excludedMissing++;
        continue;
      }

      const rawName = cleanWungjiStudentName_(row[nameCol]);
      if (rawName && rawName !== canonical.name) correctedNames++;

      const seatType = normalizeWungjiSeatType_(row[seatTypeCol]);
      const seatNumber = parseSmallInteger_(row[seatNoCol]);
      if (!isValidWungjiSeat_(seatType, seatNumber)) {
        invalidSeatCount++;
        errors.push(sheetData.name + ' ' + (r + 1) + '행: ' + id + ' ' + canonical.name + ' 학생의 좌석이 올바르지 않습니다.');
        continue;
      }

      const seatKey = makeWungjiSeatKey_(seatType, seatNumber);
      if (applicants[id]) {
        errors.push(id + ' ' + canonical.name + ' 학생이 신청자 명렬표에 두 번 이상 있습니다.');
        continue;
      }
      if (seatOwners[seatKey]) {
        errors.push(seatKey + ' 좌석이 ' + seatOwners[seatKey] + ' 학생과 ' + canonical.name + ' 학생에게 중복 배정되었습니다.');
        continue;
      }

      applicants[id] = {
        id: id,
        name: canonical.name,
        classNo: canonical.classNo,
        number: canonical.number,
        seatType: seatType,
        seatNumber: seatNumber,
        seatKey: seatKey
      };
      seatOwners[seatKey] = canonical.name;
    }
  });

  const list = Object.keys(applicants).sort().map(id => applicants[id]);
  if (!recognizedSheetCount) throw new Error('신청자 명렬표의 학번·이름·희망좌석·좌석번호 열을 찾지 못했습니다.');
  if (!list.length) throw new Error('신청자 명렬표에서 적용할 학생을 찾지 못했습니다.');

  return {
    ok: errors.length === 0,
    applicants: list,
    errors: errors,
    summary: {
      title: '일과 중 웅지실 신청자 명렬표',
      studentCount: list.length,
      openCount: list.filter(x => x.seatType === '개방형').length,
      closedCount: list.filter(x => x.seatType === '폐쇄형').length,
      excludedMissing: excludedMissing,
      excludedWithdrawn: excludedWithdrawn,
      correctedNames: correctedNames,
      invalidSeatCount: invalidSeatCount,
      errorCount: errors.length
    }
  };
}

function applyWungjiApplicantRoster_(analysis, auth) {
  if (!analysis.ok && (analysis.errors || []).length) {
    throw new Error('좌석 중복 또는 잘못된 좌석이 있어 적용할 수 없습니다. 분석 결과를 확인하세요.');
  }
  const applicants = analysis.applicants || [];
  if (!applicants.length) throw new Error('적용할 신청자가 없습니다.');

  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_APPLICANT_ROSTER_SHEET);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    const currentValues = sheet.getRange(2, 2, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getDisplayValues();
    const updates = currentValues.map(r => [String(r[0]) === 'Y' ? 'N' : r[0]]);
    sheet.getRange(2, 2, updates.length, 1).setValues(updates);
  }

  const version = Utilities.getUuid();
  const now = new Date();
  const rows = applicants.map(st => [
    version, 'Y', now, st.id, st.name, st.seatType, st.seatNumber, st.seatKey, 'Y', analysis.fileName || ''
  ]);
  sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, rows.length, 10).setValues(rows);
  return {
    ok: true,
    message: '일과 중 웅지실 신청자 ' + rows.length + '명과 좌석을 적용했습니다.',
    studentCount: rows.length
  };
}


function analyzeWungjiTimetable_(payload) {
  const records = [];
  payload.sheets.forEach(s => {
    const rows = s.rows || [];
    let headerRow = -1;
    let periodCol = -1;
    let dateCol = -1;
    const classCols = {};
    for (let r = 0; r < Math.min(rows.length, 30); r++) {
      const row = rows[r] || [];
      row.forEach((value, c) => {
        const text = String(value || '').replace(/\s+/g, '');
        if (text === '교시') periodCol = c;
        if (text === '일자') dateCol = c;
        const m = text.match(/^([1-8])\(3학년[1-8]반\)$/);
        if (m) classCols[c] = Number(m[1]);
      });
      if (periodCol >= 0 && Object.keys(classCols).length >= 4) { headerRow = r; break; }
    }
    if (headerRow < 0) return;
    let currentDay = 0;
    for (let r = headerRow + 1; r < rows.length; r++) {
      const row = rows[r] || [];
      const rowText = row.join(' ');
      const dayMatch = rowText.match(/\(([월화수목금])요일\)/) || rowText.match(/([월화수목금])요일/);
      if (dayMatch) currentDay = dayLabelToNumber_(dayMatch[1]);
      const period = parseInt(String(row[periodCol] || '').replace(/\.0$/, ''), 10);
      if (!currentDay || !(period >= 1 && period <= 7)) continue;
      Object.keys(classCols).forEach(colText => {
        const col = Number(colText);
        const classGroup = classCols[col];
        const cell = String(row[col] || '').trim();
        if (!cell) return;
        const parsed = parseWungjiCourseCell_(cell);
        if (!parsed.subject || !parsed.teacher) return;
        records.push({
          dayNo: currentDay,
          dayLabel: WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS[currentDay],
          period: period,
          classGroup: classGroup,
          subject: parsed.subject,
          subjectKey: normalizeWungjiSubjectKey_(parsed.subject),
          teacher: normalizeWungjiTeacherList_(parsed.teacher),
          raw: cell
        });
      });
    }
  });
  if (!records.length) throw new Error('시간표 형식을 분석하지 못했습니다.');
  const map = {};
  records.forEach(x => map[x.dayNo + '|' + x.period + '|' + x.classGroup] = x);
  Object.keys(WUNGJI_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS).forEach(classNo => {
    [5, 6, 7].forEach(period => {
      const rec = {
        dayNo: 5,
        dayLabel: '금',
        period: period,
        classGroup: Number(classNo),
        subject: '창의적 체험활동',
        subjectKey: normalizeWungjiSubjectKey_('창의적 체험활동'),
        teacher: normalizeWungjiTeacherList_(WUNGJI_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS[classNo]),
        raw: '창의적 체험활동(' + WUNGJI_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS[classNo] + ')'
      };
      map[rec.dayNo + '|' + rec.period + '|' + rec.classGroup] = rec;
    });
  });
  const finalRecords = Object.keys(map).map(k => map[k]).sort((a, b) => a.dayNo - b.dayNo || a.period - b.period || a.classGroup - b.classGroup);
  return { ok: true, records: finalRecords, summary: { title: '3학년 시간표', recordCount: finalRecords.length } };
}

function applyWungjiTimetable_(analysis, auth) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_TIMETABLE_SHEET);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() > 1) sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).clearContent();
  const rows = (analysis.records || []).map(x => [x.dayNo, x.dayLabel, x.period, x.classGroup, x.subject, x.subjectKey, x.teacher, x.raw]);
  if (!rows.length) throw new Error('적용할 시간표가 없습니다.');
  sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, 8).setValues(rows);
  bumpWungjiRevision_();
  rebuildWungjiTeacherSubjectSheet_();
  return { ok: true, message: '시간표 ' + rows.length + '건을 적용했습니다.', count: rows.length };
}


function analyzeWungjiSubjectRosters_(payload, auth) {
  const fullRoster = getWungjiFullRosterMap_();
  if (!Object.keys(fullRoster).length) throw new Error('먼저 3학년 전체 명렬표를 업로드하세요.');
  const assignments = getWungjiAssignments_();
  if (!assignments.length) throw new Error('먼저 3학년 시간표를 업로드하세요.');
  const grouped = {};
  const skippedSheets = [];
  payload.sheets.forEach(sheetData => {
    const rawStudents = extractWungjiStudentsFromSheet_(sheetData.rows);
    if (!rawStudents.length) { skippedSheets.push(sheetData.name); return; }
    const metadata = inferWungjiRosterMetadata_(payload.fileName, sheetData.name, sheetData.rows, rawStudents, assignments, auth);
    if (!metadata.ok) {
      const key = 'ERROR|' + sheetData.name;
      grouped[key] = grouped[key] || { ok: false, fileName: payload.fileName, sheetName: sheetData.name, error: metadata.message, students: [] };
      return;
    }
    const rosterKey = makeWungjiRosterKey_(metadata.teacher, metadata.subjectKey, metadata.classGroup);
    if (!grouped[rosterKey]) {
      grouped[rosterKey] = {
        ok: true,
        rosterKey: rosterKey,
        teacher: metadata.teacher,
        subject: metadata.subject,
        subjectKey: metadata.subjectKey,
        classGroup: metadata.classGroup,
        fileName: payload.fileName,
        sheetNames: [],
        students: {},
        excludedDelegated: 0,
        excludedMissing: 0,
        correctedNames: 0
      };
    }
    const item = grouped[rosterKey];
    item.sheetNames.push(sheetData.name);
    rawStudents.forEach(st => {
      if (st.delegated || st.id === '3728') { item.excludedDelegated++; return; }
      const canonical = fullRoster[st.id];
      if (!canonical) { item.excludedMissing++; return; }
      if (canonical.name !== st.name) item.correctedNames++;
      item.students[st.id] = { id: st.id, name: canonical.name, classNo: canonical.classNo, number: canonical.number };
    });
  });
  const items = Object.keys(grouped).map(key => {
    const g = grouped[key];
    if (!g.ok) return g;
    g.students = Object.keys(g.students).sort().map(id => g.students[id]);
    g.studentCount = g.students.length;
    g.sheetName = g.sheetNames.join(', ');
    delete g.sheetNames;
    return g;
  });
  if (!items.length) throw new Error('학생 명렬을 분석할 수 있는 시트가 없습니다.');
  const errors = items.filter(x => !x.ok).length;
  return {
    ok: errors === 0,
    items: items,
    skippedSheets: skippedSheets,
    summary: {
      title: payload.fileName,
      rosterCount: items.filter(x => x.ok).length,
      errorCount: errors,
      studentCount: items.filter(x => x.ok).reduce((sum, x) => sum + x.studentCount, 0)
    }
  };
}

function applyWungjiSubjectRosters_(analysis, auth) {
  const validItems = (analysis.items || []).filter(x => x.ok);
  if (!validItems.length) throw new Error('적용할 출석부가 없습니다.');
  const assignments = getWungjiAssignments_();
  validItems.forEach(item => {
    if (auth.role !== 'admin' && !teacherListContains_(item.teacher, auth.id)) {
      throw new Error(auth.id + ' 선생님에게 배정된 출석부만 업로드할 수 있습니다.');
    }
    const permitted = assignments.some(a => a.subjectKey === item.subjectKey && Number(a.classGroup) === Number(item.classGroup) && teacherListContains_(a.teacher, auth.id === 'admin' ? item.teacher.split(',')[0] : auth.id));
    if (auth.role !== 'admin' && !permitted) throw new Error('시간표에 배정되지 않은 과목 또는 수업반입니다.');
  });
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_SUBJECT_ROSTER_SHEET);
  const now = new Date();
  const oldValues = sheet.getLastRow() > 1 ? sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 14).getValues() : [];
  const keysToReplace = {};
  validItems.forEach(item => keysToReplace[item.rosterKey] = true);
  oldValues.forEach((row, idx) => {
    if (keysToReplace[String(row[0] || '')] && String(row[2] || '') === 'Y') {
      sheet.getRange(idx + 2, 3).setValue('N');
    }
  });
  const appendRows = [];
  validItems.forEach(item => {
    const version = Utilities.getUuid();
    (item.students || []).forEach(st => {
      appendRows.push([
        item.rosterKey, version, 'Y', now, item.teacher, item.subject, item.subjectKey,
        Number(item.classGroup), st.id, st.name, 'Y', '', item.fileName || analysis.fileName || '', item.sheetName || ''
      ]);
    });
  });
  if (appendRows.length) sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, appendRows.length, 14).setValues(appendRows);
  return { ok: true, message: validItems.length + '개 출석부, 학생 ' + appendRows.length + '명을 적용했습니다.', rosterCount: validItems.length, studentCount: appendRows.length };
}


function extractWungjiStudentsFromSheet_(rows) {
  rows = rows || [];
  const descriptors = [];

  for (let r = 0; r < Math.min(rows.length, 200); r++) {
    const normalized = (rows[r] || []).map(v => normalizeWungjiHeader_(v));
    const nameCols = [];
    normalized.forEach((h, c) => {
      if (h === '성명' || h === '이름') nameCols.push(c);
    });
    if (!nameCols.length) continue;

    nameCols.forEach((nameCol, idx) => {
      const leftBoundary = idx === 0 ? 0 : Math.floor((nameCols[idx - 1] + nameCol) / 2) + 1;
      const rightBoundary = idx === nameCols.length - 1 ? normalized.length - 1 : Math.floor((nameCol + nameCols[idx + 1]) / 2);
      let idCol = -1, gradeCol = -1, classCol = -1, numberCol = -1;
      for (let c = leftBoundary; c <= rightBoundary; c++) {
        const h = normalized[c];
        if (h === '학번') idCol = c;
        if (h === '학년') gradeCol = c;
        if (h === '반') classCol = c;
        if (h === '번호') numberCol = c;
      }
      if (idCol >= 0 || (classCol >= 0 && numberCol >= 0)) {
        descriptors.push({ headerRow: r, leftBoundary, rightBoundary, idCol, gradeCol, classCol, numberCol, nameCol });
      }
    });
  }

  if (!descriptors.length) return [];
  const resultMap = {};

  descriptors.forEach(desc => {
    let blankRun = 0;
    for (let r = desc.headerRow + 1; r < rows.length; r++) {
      const row = rows[r] || [];
      const segment = row.slice(desc.leftBoundary, desc.rightBoundary + 1);
      const segmentText = segment.join(' ').trim();
      const normalizedSegment = segment.map(v => normalizeWungjiHeader_(v));
      if (normalizedSegment.some(h => h === '성명' || h === '이름')) break;
      if (!segmentText) {
        blankRun++;
        if (blankRun > 10) break;
        continue;
      }
      blankRun = 0;

      let id = '';
      if (desc.idCol >= 0) id = normalizeWungjiStudentId_(row[desc.idCol]);
      if (!id) {
        for (let c = desc.leftBoundary; c <= desc.rightBoundary; c++) {
          const candidate = normalizeWungjiStudentId_(row[c]);
          if (candidate) { id = candidate; break; }
        }
      }

      let classNo = parseSmallInteger_(desc.classCol >= 0 ? row[desc.classCol] : '');
      let number = parseSmallInteger_(desc.numberCol >= 0 ? row[desc.numberCol] : '');
      const grade = parseSmallInteger_(desc.gradeCol >= 0 ? row[desc.gradeCol] : '3') || 3;
      if (!id && grade === 3 && classNo >= 1 && classNo <= 8 && number >= 1 && number <= 99) {
        id = '3' + String(classNo) + String(number).padStart(2, '0');
      }
      if (!id) continue;
      if (!classNo) classNo = Number(id.charAt(1));
      if (!number) number = Number(id.slice(2));

      let rawName = String(row[desc.nameCol] || '').trim();
      if (!rawName) {
        rawName = segment.map(v => String(v || '').trim()).find(v => /^[가-힣]{2,5}(?:\s*\([^)]*\))?$/.test(v)) || '';
      }
      if (!rawName) continue;
      const delegated = /\(\s*위탁\s*\)/.test(rawName) || /\(\s*위탁\s*\)/.test(segmentText);
      const name = getWungjiEffectiveStudentName_(id, rawName);
      if (!name) continue;
      resultMap[id] = { id, name, rawName, classNo, number, delegated };
    }
  });

  return Object.keys(resultMap).sort().map(id => resultMap[id]);
}

function inferWungjiRosterMetadata_(fileName, sheetName, rows, students, assignments, auth) {
  const topText = (rows || []).slice(0, 20).map(r => (r || []).join(' ')).join(' ');
  const combined = [fileName, sheetName, topText].join(' ');
  const combinedKey = normalizeWungjiSubjectKey_(combined);
  const subjectKeys = {};
  assignments.forEach(a => subjectKeys[a.subjectKey] = a.subject);
  const matchingKeys = Object.keys(subjectKeys).filter(k => k && combinedKey.indexOf(k) >= 0).sort((a, b) => b.length - a.length);
  let subjectKey = matchingKeys[0] || '';
  let classGroup = inferWungjiClassGroup_(combined, students);
  let explicitTeacher = inferWungjiTeacher_(combined, assignments);
  let candidates = assignments.filter(a => (!subjectKey || a.subjectKey === subjectKey) && (!classGroup || Number(a.classGroup) === Number(classGroup)));
  if (auth.role !== 'admin') candidates = candidates.filter(a => teacherListContains_(a.teacher, auth.id));
  if (explicitTeacher) candidates = candidates.filter(a => teacherListContains_(a.teacher, explicitTeacher));
  if (!subjectKey && candidates.length) {
    const distinct = {};
    candidates.forEach(a => distinct[a.subjectKey] = a);
    if (Object.keys(distinct).length === 1) subjectKey = candidates[0].subjectKey;
  }
  if (!classGroup && candidates.length) {
    const distinctClass = {};
    candidates.forEach(a => distinctClass[a.classGroup] = true);
    if (Object.keys(distinctClass).length === 1) classGroup = Number(candidates[0].classGroup);
  }
  candidates = assignments.filter(a => a.subjectKey === subjectKey && Number(a.classGroup) === Number(classGroup));
  if (auth.role !== 'admin') candidates = candidates.filter(a => teacherListContains_(a.teacher, auth.id));
  if (explicitTeacher) candidates = candidates.filter(a => teacherListContains_(a.teacher, explicitTeacher));
  const unique = {};
  candidates.forEach(a => unique[a.teacher + '|' + a.subjectKey + '|' + a.classGroup] = a);
  candidates = Object.keys(unique).map(k => unique[k]);
  if (!subjectKey) return { ok: false, message: '과목명을 인식하지 못했습니다.' };
  if (!classGroup) return { ok: false, message: '수업반을 인식하지 못했습니다.' };
  if (candidates.length === 0) return { ok: false, message: '시간표에서 해당 과목·수업반·교사를 찾지 못했습니다.' };
  if (candidates.length > 1) return { ok: false, message: '같은 과목·수업반을 담당하는 교사가 여러 명입니다. 담당 교사가 표시된 파일을 사용하거나 본인 계정으로 업로드하세요.' };
  const chosen = candidates[0];
  return { ok: true, teacher: chosen.teacher, subject: chosen.subject, subjectKey: chosen.subjectKey, classGroup: chosen.classGroup };
}

function inferWungjiClassGroup_(text, students) {
  text = String(text || '');
  let m = text.match(/3\s*학년\s*3\s*[-_]\s*([1-8])/);
  if (!m) m = text.match(/3\s*[-_]\s*([1-8])/);
  if (!m) m = text.match(/30([1-8])(?!\d)/);
  if (!m) m = text.match(/\(([1-8])\s*반\)/);
  if (!m) m = text.match(/([1-8])\s*반/);
  if (m) return Number(m[1]);
  const counts = {};
  (students || []).forEach(s => counts[s.classNo] = (counts[s.classNo] || 0) + 1);
  const keys = Object.keys(counts).sort((a, b) => counts[b] - counts[a]);
  return keys.length === 1 ? Number(keys[0]) : 0;
}

function inferWungjiTeacher_(text, assignments) {
  text = String(text || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
  let m = text.match(/담당\s*교사\s*[:：]?\s*([가-힣A-Za-z]+\s*[ABab]?)/);
  if (m) return m[1].replace(/\s+/g, '');
  const teachers = {};
  assignments.forEach(a => a.teacher.split(',').forEach(t => teachers[t.trim()] = true));
  const found = Object.keys(teachers).filter(t => t && text.replace(/\s+/g, '').indexOf(t.replace(/\s+/g, '')) >= 0);
  return found.length === 1 ? found[0] : '';
}

function getWungjiAssignments_() {
  const key = getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('assignments');
  const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_TIMETABLE_SHEET);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return [];
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getDisplayValues();
  const unique = {};
  values.forEach(r => {
    if (!r[4] || !r[6]) return;
    const item = {
      dayNo: Number(r[0]), dayLabel: r[1], period: Number(r[2]), classGroup: Number(r[3]),
      subject: r[4], subjectKey: r[5] || normalizeWungjiSubjectKey_(r[4]), teacher: normalizeWungjiTeacherList_(r[6])
    };
    unique[item.dayNo + '|' + item.period + '|' + item.classGroup + '|' + item.teacher] = item;
  });
  return putWungjiCacheJson_(key, Object.keys(unique).map(k => unique[k]), WUNGJI_STATIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function rebuildWungjiTeacherSubjectSheet_() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_TEACHER_SUBJECT_SHEET);
  const pairs = {};
  getWungjiAssignments_().forEach(a => {
    a.teacher.split(',').map(x => x.trim()).filter(Boolean).forEach(t => pairs[a.subject + '|' + t] = [a.subject, t]);
  });
  const rows = Object.keys(pairs).map(k => pairs[k]).sort((a, b) => a[1].localeCompare(b[1], 'ko') || a[0].localeCompare(b[0], 'ko'));
  if (sheet.getLastRow() > 1) sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).clearContent();
  if (rows.length) sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, 2).setValues(rows);
}


function getWungjiApplicantRostersForDates_(dateKeys) {
  const normalized = Array.from(new Set((dateKeys || []).map(d => normalizeDateKey_(d)).filter(Boolean)));
  const result = {};
  const missing = [];
  normalized.forEach(date => {
    const key = getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('applicant', date);
    const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(key);
    if (cached) result[date] = cached;
    else missing.push(date);
  });
  if (!missing.length) return result;
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_APPLICANT_ROSTER_SHEET);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) {
    missing.forEach(date => result[date] = { version:'', registered:false, students:[], map:{} });
    return result;
  }
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
  const versions = {};
  values.forEach(row => {
    const version = String(row[0] || '');
    if (!version) return;
    if (!versions[version]) versions[version] = { version:version, uploadedAt:new Date(row[2]), current:String(row[1]) === 'Y', rows:[] };
    versions[version].rows.push(row);
  });
  const list = Object.keys(versions).map(k => versions[k]).sort((a,b) => a.uploadedAt - b.uploadedAt);
  missing.forEach(date => {
    if (!list.length) {
      result[date] = { version:'', registered:false, students:[], map:{} };
      return;
    }
    let chosen = list.find(v => v.current) || list[list.length - 1];
    const target = parseWungjiDate_(date);
    target.setHours(23,59,59,999);
    const eligible = list.filter(v => v.uploadedAt <= target);
    if (eligible.length) chosen = eligible[eligible.length - 1];
    const students = chosen.rows.filter(r => String(r[8] || '') === 'Y' && String(r[3] || '') !== '3728').map(r => ({
      id:String(r[3] || ''), name:getWungjiEffectiveStudentName_(String(r[3] || ''), r[4]), seatType:String(r[5] || ''), seatNumber:Number(r[6]) || 0,
      seatKey:String(r[7] || '') || makeWungjiSeatKey_(r[5],r[6])
    })).sort((a,b) => a.id.localeCompare(b.id,'ko',{numeric:true}));
    const map = {};
    students.forEach(st => map[st.id] = st);
    result[date] = { version:chosen.version, registered:true, students:students, map:map };
    putWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('applicant', date), result[date], WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
  });
  return result;
}

function getWungjiApplicantRosterForDate_(dateKey) {
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date());
  return getWungjiApplicantRostersForDates_([date])[date] || { version:'', registered:false, students:[], map:{} };
}

function normalizeWungjiSeatType_(value) {
  const text = String(value || '').replace(/\s+/g, '').trim();
  if (text.indexOf('개방') >= 0) return '개방형';
  if (text.indexOf('폐쇄') >= 0) return '폐쇄형';
  return '';
}

function isValidWungjiSeat_(seatType, seatNumber) {
  const n = Number(seatNumber);
  if (seatType === '개방형') return n >= 1 && n <= 28;
  if (seatType === '폐쇄형') return n >= 1 && n <= 36;
  return false;
}

function makeWungjiSeatKey_(seatType, seatNumber) {
  const type = normalizeWungjiSeatType_(seatType);
  const number = Number(seatNumber) || 0;
  return type && number ? type.replace('형', '') + number : '';
}

function getWungjiFullRosterMap_() {
  const key = getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('full_roster');
  const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_FULL_ROSTER_SHEET);
  const result = {};
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return result;
  sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getDisplayValues().forEach(r => {
    const id = normalizeWungjiStudentId_(r[0]);
    if (id && id !== '3728') result[id] = {
      id: id, name: getWungjiEffectiveStudentName_(id, r[1]), classNo: Number(r[2]) || Number(id.charAt(1)), number: Number(r[3]) || Number(id.slice(2))
    };
  });
  return putWungjiCacheJson_(key, result, WUNGJI_STATIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function reconcileWungjiApplicantRosterWithFullRoster_() {
  const full = getWungjiFullRosterMap_();
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_APPLICANT_ROSTER_SHEET);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
  const names = [];
  const active = [];
  values.forEach(row => {
    const id = String(row[3] || '').trim();
    const canonical = full[id];
    names.push([canonical ? canonical.name : row[4]]);
    active.push([canonical && id !== '3728' ? String(row[8] || 'Y') : 'N']);
  });
  sheet.getRange(2, 5, names.length, 1).setValues(names);
  sheet.getRange(2, 9, active.length, 1).setValues(active);
}

function reconcileWungjiSubjectRostersWithFullRoster_() {
  const full = getWungjiFullRosterMap_();
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_SUBJECT_ROSTER_SHEET);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 14).getValues();
  const names = [];
  const active = [];
  const reasons = [];
  values.forEach(row => {
    const id = String(row[8] || '').trim();
    const canonical = full[id];
    if (!canonical || id === '3728') {
      names.push([row[9]]);
      active.push(['N']);
      reasons.push([id === '3728' ? '자퇴' : '전체 명렬표 미등록']);
    } else {
      names.push([canonical.name]);
      active.push([String(row[2]) === 'Y' ? 'Y' : row[10]]);
      reasons.push(['']);
    }
  });
  sheet.getRange(2, 10, names.length, 1).setValues(names);
  sheet.getRange(2, 11, active.length, 1).setValues(active);
  sheet.getRange(2, 12, reasons.length, 1).setValues(reasons);
}


function getWungjiPeriodStudentIndex_(dateKey, period) {
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey);
  const key = getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('period_index', date + '_' + Number(period));
  const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  const courses = getEffectiveWungjiScheduleForDate_(date).filter(x => Number(x.period) === Number(period));
  const rosters = buildWungjiRostersForKeys_(courses.map(c => c.rosterKey), date);
  const byStudent = {};
  courses.forEach(course => {
    const roster = rosters[course.rosterKey] || { students: [] };
    (roster.students || []).forEach(student => {
      if (!byStudent[student.id]) byStudent[student.id] = [];
      byStudent[student.id].push({ course: course, student: student });
    });
  });
  return putWungjiCacheJson_(key, { byStudent: byStudent }, WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function appendWungjiAttendanceRowLocked_(row, cacheKey, studentId, loginTime) {
  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(12000)) throw new Error('접속이 몰려 처리 대기 중입니다. 잠시 후 자동으로 다시 시도합니다.');
  try {
    let map = getWungjiCacheJson_(cacheKey);
    if (!map) map = getWungjiAttendanceMap_(row[1], row[3], row[8]);
    if (map[studentId]) return { duplicate: true, loginTime: map[studentId] };
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_LOG_SHEET);
    const nextRow = Math.max(2, sheet.getLastRow() + 1);
    sheet.getRange(nextRow, 1, 1, row.length).setValues([row]);
    map[studentId] = loginTime;
    putWungjiCacheJson_(cacheKey, map, WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_CACHE_SECONDS);
    removeWungjiCache_(getWungjiAttendanceRecordCacheKey_(row[1], row[3], row[8]));
    return { duplicate: false, loginTime: loginTime };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function processWungjiAttendanceById_(id, mode) {
  const studentId = normalizeWungjiStudentId_(id);
  if (!studentId) return '❌ 학번 4자리를 정확히 입력하세요.';
  const now = new Date();
  const attendanceMode = normalizeWungjiAttendanceMode_(mode);
  const periodInfo = attendanceMode === 'class' ? getCurrentWungjiDayRegistrationPeriod_(now) : getCurrentWungjiPeriod_(now);
  if (!periodInfo.ok) {
    if (attendanceMode === 'class') return '❌ 현재는 수업참석 등록 시간이 아닙니다.<br>수업참석 등록은 08:55부터 16:40까지 가능합니다.';
    return '❌ 현재는 교과 출석 등록 시간이 아닙니다.<br>QR 출석은 수업 시작 3분 전부터 시작 9분 후까지 가능합니다.';
  }
  const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(now, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const applicantRoster = getWungjiApplicantRosterForDate_(dateKey);
  if (!applicantRoster.registered) return '❌ 일과 중 웅지실 신청자 명렬표가 아직 등록되지 않았습니다.';
  const applicant = applicantRoster.map[studentId];
  if (!applicant) return '❌ 일과 중 웅지실 이용 신청자 명단에 등록되어 있지 않습니다.';
  const index = getWungjiPeriodStudentIndex_(dateKey, periodInfo.period);
  const matches = (index.byStudent && index.byStudent[studentId]) || [];
  if (matches.length === 0) return '❌ 현재 수업의 웅지실 이용 명단에 등록되어 있지 않습니다.';
  if (matches.length > 1) {
    appendWungjiErrorLog_('중복명렬', studentId, '같은 교시에 두 개 이상의 웅지실 출석부에서 발견됨', matches.map(x => x.course.subject + ' ' + x.course.classGroup + '반').join(', '));
    return '❌ 같은 교시에 두 출석부에서 학번이 중복으로 확인되었습니다. 담당 교사에게 문의하세요.';
  }
  const match = matches[0];
  const recordKey = dateKey + '|' + periodInfo.period + '|' + match.course.rosterKey + '|' + studentId;
  const timeStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, TZ, 'HH:mm');
  const dayNo = dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(now);
  const cacheKey = getWungjiAttendanceCacheKey_(dateKey, periodInfo.period, match.course.rosterKey);
  const recordMap = getWungjiAttendanceRecordMap_(dateKey, periodInfo.period, match.course.rosterKey);
  const existing = recordMap[studentId];
  if (existing && existing.time) {
    return '✅ 이미 ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(getWungjiAttendanceStatusLabel_(existing)) + '으로 등록되어 있습니다.<br>' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.student.name) + ' / ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.course.subject) + ' ' + match.course.classGroup + '반<br>좌석: ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(applicant.seatKey) + '<br>담당교사: ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.course.teacher) + '<br>최초 로그인: ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(formatWungjiTime4_(existing.time));
  }
  const status = attendanceMode === 'class' ? WUNGJI_STATUS_CLASS : WUNGJI_STATUS_PRESENT;
  const source = attendanceMode === 'class' ? '학생QR수업' : '학생QR';
  const write = appendWungjiAttendanceRowLocked_([
    recordKey, dateKey, WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS[dayNo], periodInfo.period, match.course.classGroup,
    match.course.subject, match.course.subjectKey, match.course.teacher, match.course.rosterKey,
    studentId, match.student.name, timeStr, status, source
  ], cacheKey, studentId, timeStr);
  if (write.duplicate) {
    return '✅ 이미 출석이 등록되어 있습니다.<br>' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.student.name) + ' / ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.course.subject) + ' ' + match.course.classGroup + '반<br>좌석: ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.course.seatKey || applicant.seatKey) + '<br>담당교사: ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.course.teacher) + '<br>최초 로그인: ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(formatWungjiTime4_(write.loginTime));
  }
  fastUpdateWungjiWeeklyStatCell_(dateKey, periodInfo.period, match.course, studentId, match.student.name, timeStr, status);
  const doneLabel = attendanceMode === 'class' ? '수업참석' : '출석';
  return '✅ ' + doneLabel + '이 등록되었습니다.<br>' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.student.name) + ' / ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.course.subject) + ' ' + match.course.classGroup + '반<br>좌석: ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.student.seatKey) + '<br>' + periodInfo.period + '교시 / 담당교사: ' + escapeWungjiHtml_(match.course.teacher) + '<br>로그인 시간: ' + timeStr;
}

function normalizeWungjiAttendanceMode_(mode) {
  const text = String(mode || '').toLowerCase().trim();
  return text === 'class' || text === '수업' || text === 'lesson' ? 'class' : 'wungji';
}

function getCurrentWungjiDayRegistrationPeriod_(dateObj) {
  const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const nowMinutes = dateObj.getHours() * 60 + dateObj.getMinutes() + dateObj.getSeconds() / 60;
  const dayStart = 8 * 60 + 55;
  const dayEnd = 16 * 60 + 40 + 59 / 60;
  if (nowMinutes < dayStart || nowMinutes > dayEnd) return { ok: false };
  const maxPeriod = getWungjiSchoolPeriodLimitForDate_(dateKey);
  if (!maxPeriod) return { ok: false };
  const ranges = getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey);
  const firstStart = parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(ranges[1] && ranges[1].start);
  if (firstStart >= 0 && nowMinutes < firstStart) return { ok: true, period: 1, startTime: ranges[1].start, endTime: ranges[1].end };
  for (let p = 1; p <= maxPeriod; p++) {
    const start = parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(ranges[p] && ranges[p].start);
    const end = parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(ranges[p] && ranges[p].end);
    if (start < 0 || end < 0) continue;
    if (nowMinutes >= start && nowMinutes <= end + 59 / 60) return { ok: true, period: p, startTime: ranges[p].start, endTime: ranges[p].end };
    if (p < maxPeriod) {
      const nextStart = parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(ranges[p + 1] && ranges[p + 1].start);
      if (nextStart >= 0 && nowMinutes > end && nowMinutes < nextStart) return { ok: true, period: p + 1, startTime: ranges[p + 1].start, endTime: ranges[p + 1].end };
    } else if (nowMinutes > end && nowMinutes <= dayEnd) {
      return { ok: true, period: p, startTime: ranges[p].start, endTime: ranges[p].end };
    }
  }
  return { ok: false };
}


function getWungjiQrEarlyMinutes_(settings) {
  // QR 허용 시간은 현황표 리셋 기준과 분리합니다.
  // 일과 중 웅지실 QR 출석은 수업 시작 3분 전부터 허용합니다.
  settings = settings || getWungjiSettingsMap_();
  const configured = Number(settings.ATTENDANCE_EARLY_MINUTES);
  return Math.max(3, configured || 3);
}

function getWungjiQrLateMinutes_(settings) {
  settings = settings || getWungjiSettingsMap_();
  const configured = Number(settings.ATTENDANCE_LATE_MINUTES);
  return Math.max(9, configured || 9);
}

function getWungjiResetBeforeBellMinutes_(settings) {
  settings = settings || getWungjiSettingsMap_();
  const configured = Number(settings.ATTENDANCE_RESET_BEFORE_BELL_MINUTES);
  return Math.max(5, configured || 5);
}

function getCurrentWungjiPeriod_(dateObj) {
  const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const ranges = getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey);
  const settings = getWungjiSettingsMap_();
  const early = getWungjiQrEarlyMinutes_(settings);
  const late = getWungjiQrLateMinutes_(settings);
  const nowMinutes = dateObj.getHours() * 60 + dateObj.getMinutes() + dateObj.getSeconds() / 60;
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) {
    const start = parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(ranges[p].start);
    if (nowMinutes >= start - early && nowMinutes <= start + late + 59 / 60) {
      return { ok: true, period: p, startTime: ranges[p].start, endTime: ranges[p].end, qrEarlyMinutes: early, lateMinutes: late };
    }
  }
  return { ok: false };
}

function getCurrentWungjiDisplaySession_(dateObj) {
  const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const ranges = getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey);
  const resetBeforeBell = getWungjiResetBeforeBellMinutes_(getWungjiSettingsMap_());
  const nowMinutes = dateObj.getHours() * 60 + dateObj.getMinutes() + dateObj.getSeconds() / 60;
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) {
    const start = parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(ranges[p].start);
    const nextStart = p < 7 ? parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(ranges[p + 1].start) : null;
    const end = p < 7 ? nextStart - resetBeforeBell : parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(ranges[p].end) - resetBeforeBell;
    if (nowMinutes >= start - resetBeforeBell && nowMinutes < end) {
      return { ok: true, date: dateKey, period: p, startTime: ranges[p].start, endTime: ranges[p].end, resetBeforeBell: resetBeforeBell };
    }
  }
  return { ok: false, date: dateKey, resetBeforeBell: resetBeforeBell };
}

function formatWungjiTime4_(value) {
  // v13: 교사 수동 입력창만 4자리(0915)를 받고, 저장·표시·통계는 HH:mm(09:15)로 통일합니다.
  if (value instanceof Date) return Utilities.formatDate(value, TZ, 'HH:mm');
  const text = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
  if (!text) return '';
  let m = text.match(/^(\d{1,2}):(\d{2})$/);
  if (!m) {
    const digits = text.replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
    if (digits.length >= 4) m = [null, digits.slice(0, 2), digits.slice(2, 4)];
  }
  if (!m) return text;
  const hh = Number(m[1]);
  const mm = Number(m[2]);
