  if (hh < 0 || hh > 23 || mm < 0 || mm > 59) return text;
  return String(hh).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(mm).padStart(2, '0');
}

function normalizeWungjiManualTime4_(value) {
  // 입력은 0915처럼 4자리로 받되, 실제 저장값은 09:15 형식으로 변환합니다.
  const digits = String(value == null ? '' : value).replace(/[０-９]/g, function(ch) { return String(ch.charCodeAt(0) - 65248); }).replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
  if (!/^\d{4}$/.test(digits)) throw new Error('시간은 숫자 4자리로 입력해야 합니다. 예: 0915');
  const hh = Number(digits.slice(0, 2));
  const mm = Number(digits.slice(2, 4));
  if (hh < 0 || hh > 23 || mm < 0 || mm > 59) throw new Error('올바른 시간이 아닙니다. 예: 0915');
  return String(hh).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(mm).padStart(2, '0');
}

function getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey) {
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date());
  const key = getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('period_ranges', date);
  const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  const settings = getWungjiSettingsMap_();
  const ranges = {};
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) {
    const start = normalizeWungjiTime_(settings['PERIOD_' + p + '_START'] || WUNGJI_DEFAULT_PERIOD_TIMES[p]);
    const end = normalizeWungjiTime_(settings['PERIOD_' + p + '_END']) || addWungjiMinutes_(start, Number(settings.CLASS_DURATION_MINUTES) || 50);
    ranges[p] = { start: start, end: end };
  }
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_DATE_TIME_SHEET);
  if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getDisplayValues().forEach(r => {
      const period = Number(r[1]);
      if (normalizeDateKey_(r[0]) !== date || !(period >= 1 && period <= 7)) return;
      const start = normalizeWungjiTime_(r[2]);
      const end = normalizeWungjiTime_(r[3]);
      if (start) ranges[period].start = start;
      if (end) ranges[period].end = end;
      else if (start) ranges[period].end = addWungjiMinutes_(start, 50);
    });
  }
  validateWungjiPeriodRanges_(ranges);
  return putWungjiCacheJson_(key, ranges, WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function getWungjiPeriodTimesForDate_(dateKey) {
  const ranges = getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey);
  const times = {};
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) times[p] = ranges[p].start;
  return times;
}

function validateWungjiPeriodRanges_(ranges) {
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) {
    const range = ranges[p] || {};
    const start = normalizeWungjiTime_(range.start);
    const end = normalizeWungjiTime_(range.end);
    if (!start || !end) throw new Error(p + '교시 시작·종료 시간이 올바르지 않습니다.');
    if (parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(end) <= parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(start)) throw new Error(p + '교시 종료 시간은 시작 시간보다 늦어야 합니다.');
    range.start = start;
    range.end = end;
    ranges[p] = range;
  }
  return ranges;
}

function getWungjiSettingsMap_() {
  const key = getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('settings');
  const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  const result = {};
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_SETTINGS_SHEET);
  if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getDisplayValues().forEach(r => {
      if (r[0]) result[String(r[0]).trim()] = r[1];
    });
  }
  return putWungjiCacheJson_(key, result, WUNGJI_STATIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}


function getWungjiScheduleData_() {
  const key = getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('schedule_data');
  const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  const data = { assignments: getWungjiAssignments_(), overridesByDate: {} };
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_OVERRIDE_SHEET);
  if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getDisplayValues().forEach(r => {
      const date = normalizeDateKey_(r[0]);
      if (!date) return;
      if (!data.overridesByDate[date]) data.overridesByDate[date] = [];
      data.overridesByDate[date].push(r);
    });
  }
  return putWungjiCacheJson_(key, data, WUNGJI_STATIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}

function getEffectiveWungjiDayNoForDate_(dateKey, data) {
  const date = parseWungjiDate_(dateKey);
  if (!date) return 0;
  let dayNo = dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(date);
  data = data || getWungjiScheduleData_();
  const overrides = (data.overridesByDate && data.overridesByDate[dateKey]) || [];
  const mapRow = overrides.slice().reverse().find(r => r[1] === '요일적용');
  if (mapRow && Number(mapRow[2]) >= 1 && Number(mapRow[2]) <= 5) dayNo = Number(mapRow[2]);
  return dayNo;
}

function buildEffectiveWungjiScheduleFromData_(dateKey, data) {
  const date = parseWungjiDate_(dateKey);
  if (!date) return [];
  data = data || getWungjiScheduleData_();
  const dayNo = getEffectiveWungjiDayNoForDate_(dateKey, data);
  const base = (data.assignments || []).filter(a => Number(a.dayNo) === dayNo).map(a => Object.assign({}, a));
  const byKey = {};
  base.forEach(a => byKey[a.classGroup + '|' + a.period] = a);

  // 일부 반·교시 변경 기능은 폐지했습니다.
  // 과거에 저장된 '수업없음' 또는 '수업변경' 행도 더 이상 실제 시간표에 적용하지 않습니다.
  // 금요일 5·6·7교시는 창체 시간으로 고정하되, 요일적용 변경이 있으면 변경된 요일 기준을 따릅니다.
  if (dayNo === 5) {
    Object.keys(WUNGJI_SPECIAL_FRIDAY_TEACHERS).forEach(classNo => {
      [5, 6, 7].forEach(period => {
        byKey[Number(classNo) + '|' + period] = {
          dayNo: 5,
          dayLabel: '금',
          period: period,
          classGroup: Number(classNo),
          subject: '창체',
          subjectKey: normalizeWungjiSubjectKey_('창체'),
          teacher: getWungjiSpecialFridayTeachersForClass_(classNo, dateKey),
          raw: '창체(' + getWungjiSpecialFridayTeachersForClass_(classNo, dateKey) + ')',
          isSpecialFridayCreative: true
        };
      });
    });
  }

  return Object.keys(byKey).map(k => {
    const a = byKey[k];
    if (dayNo === 5 && Number(a.period) >= 5 && Number(a.period) <= 7 && Number(a.classGroup) >= 1 && Number(a.classGroup) <= 8) {
      a.subject = '창체';
      a.subjectKey = normalizeWungjiSubjectKey_('창체');
      a.teacher = getWungjiSpecialFridayTeachersForClass_(a.classGroup, dateKey);
      a.rosterKey = makeWungjiSpecialFridayRosterKey_(a.classGroup);
      a.isSpecialFridayCreative = true;
    } else {
      const sourceTeacher = a.teacher;
      a.teacher = getWungjiEffectiveTeacherListForDate_(sourceTeacher, dateKey);
      a.rosterKey = makeWungjiRosterKey_(sourceTeacher, a.subjectKey, a.classGroup);
    }
    return a;
  }).sort((a, b) => a.period - b.period || a.classGroup - b.classGroup);
}

function getEffectiveWungjiScheduleForDate_(dateKey) {
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date());
  const key = getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('effective_schedule', date);
  const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(key);
  if (cached) return cached;
  return putWungjiCacheJson_(key, buildEffectiveWungjiScheduleFromData_(date, getWungjiScheduleData_()), WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
}


function getWungjiRosterCacheKey_(rosterKey, dateKey) {
  return getWungjiVersionedCacheKey_('roster', normalizeDateKey_(dateKey) + '_' + wungjiHash_(rosterKey));
}

function buildWungjiRostersForKeys_(rosterKeys, dateKey) {
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date());
  const result = {};
  const missing = [];
  (rosterKeys || []).filter(Boolean).forEach(rosterKey => {
    const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiRosterCacheKey_(rosterKey, date));
    if (cached) result[rosterKey] = cached;
    else missing.push(rosterKey);
  });
  if (!missing.length) return result;
  const applicantRoster = getWungjiApplicantRosterForDate_(date);
  const emptyBase = { version: '', applicantVersion: applicantRoster.version, subjectRegistered: false, applicantRegistered: applicantRoster.registered, students: [] };
  missing.slice().forEach(rosterKey => {
    if (!isWungjiSpecialFridayRosterKey_(rosterKey)) return;
    const classNo = getWungjiSpecialFridayClassFromRosterKey_(rosterKey);
    const students = (applicantRoster.students || []).filter(st => getWungjiStudentClassNo_(st.id) === classNo).map(st => Object.assign({}, st)).sort(sortWungjiStudentsBySeat_);
    result[rosterKey] = putWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiRosterCacheKey_(rosterKey, date), {
      version: 'special-friday', applicantVersion: applicantRoster.version,
      subjectRegistered: true, applicantRegistered: applicantRoster.registered, students: students
    }, WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
    const idx = missing.indexOf(rosterKey);
    if (idx >= 0) missing.splice(idx, 1);
  });
  if (!missing.length) return result;
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_SUBJECT_ROSTER_SHEET);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) {
    missing.forEach(k => result[k] = putWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiRosterCacheKey_(k, date), Object.assign({}, emptyBase), WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS));
    return result;
  }
  const wanted = {};
  missing.forEach(k => wanted[k] = true);
  const versionsByKey = {};
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 14).getValues();
  values.forEach(row => {
    const rosterKey = String(row[0] || '');
    if (!wanted[rosterKey]) return;
    const version = String(row[1] || '');
    if (!versionsByKey[rosterKey]) versionsByKey[rosterKey] = {};
    if (!versionsByKey[rosterKey][version]) versionsByKey[rosterKey][version] = { version: version, uploadedAt: new Date(row[3]), current: String(row[2]) === 'Y', rows: [] };
    versionsByKey[rosterKey][version].rows.push(row);
  });
  const targetEnd = parseWungjiDate_(date);
  targetEnd.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
  missing.forEach(rosterKey => {
    const versions = versionsByKey[rosterKey] || {};
    const list = Object.keys(versions).map(k => versions[k]).sort((a, b) => a.uploadedAt - b.uploadedAt);
    if (!list.length) {
      result[rosterKey] = Object.assign({}, emptyBase);
    } else {
      let chosen = list[0];
      list.forEach(v => { if (v.uploadedAt <= targetEnd) chosen = v; });
      const students = chosen.rows.filter(r => String(r[10] || '') === 'Y' && String(r[8] || '') !== '3728' && applicantRoster.map[String(r[8] || '')]).map(r => {
        const applicant = applicantRoster.map[String(r[8] || '')];
        return { id: String(r[8]), name: getWungjiEffectiveStudentName_(String(r[8]), r[9]), seatType: applicant.seatType, seatNumber: applicant.seatNumber, seatKey: applicant.seatKey };
      }).sort((a, b) => {
        if (a.seatType !== b.seatType) return a.seatType === '개방형' ? -1 : 1;
        return a.seatNumber - b.seatNumber;
      });
      result[rosterKey] = {
        version: chosen.version, applicantVersion: applicantRoster.version,
        subjectRegistered: true, applicantRegistered: applicantRoster.registered, students: students
      };
    }
    putWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiRosterCacheKey_(rosterKey, date), result[rosterKey], WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
  });
  return result;
}

function getWungjiRosterCountMapForDate_(rosterKeys, dateKey) {
  const rosters = buildWungjiRostersForKeys_(rosterKeys, dateKey);
  const result = {};
  Object.keys(rosters).forEach(k => {
    const roster = rosters[k];
    result[k] = {
      count: (roster.students || []).length,
      state: !roster.subjectRegistered ? 'subjectMissing' : !roster.applicantRegistered ? 'applicantMissing' : 'ready'
    };
  });
  return result;
}


function buildWungjiRosterForDates_(rosterKey, dateKeys) {
  rosterKey = String(rosterKey || '');
  const dates = Array.from(new Set((dateKeys || []).map(d => normalizeDateKey_(d)).filter(Boolean)));
  if (isWungjiSpecialFridayRosterKey_(rosterKey)) {
    const classNo = getWungjiSpecialFridayClassFromRosterKey_(rosterKey);
    const applicants = getWungjiApplicantRostersForDates_(dates);
    const specialResult = {};
    dates.forEach(date => {
      const applicant = applicants[date] || { version: '', registered: false, students: [] };
      specialResult[date] = {
        version: 'special-friday', applicantVersion: applicant.version,
        subjectRegistered: true, applicantRegistered: applicant.registered,
        students: (applicant.students || []).filter(st => getWungjiStudentClassNo_(st.id) === classNo).map(st => Object.assign({}, st)).sort(sortWungjiStudentsBySeat_)
      };
      putWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiRosterCacheKey_(rosterKey, date), specialResult[date], WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
    });
    return specialResult;
  }
  const result = {};
  const missing = [];
  dates.forEach(date => {
    const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiRosterCacheKey_(rosterKey, date));
    if (cached) result[date] = cached;
    else missing.push(date);
  });
  if (!missing.length) return result;
  const applicants = getWungjiApplicantRostersForDates_(missing);
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_SUBJECT_ROSTER_SHEET);
  const versions = {};
  if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 14).getValues().forEach(row => {
      if (String(row[0] || '') !== rosterKey) return;
      const version = String(row[1] || '');
      if (!versions[version]) versions[version] = { version:version, uploadedAt:new Date(row[3]), current:String(row[2]) === 'Y', rows:[] };
      versions[version].rows.push(row);
    });
  }
  const list = Object.keys(versions).map(k => versions[k]).sort((a,b) => a.uploadedAt - b.uploadedAt);
  missing.forEach(date => {
    const applicant = applicants[date] || { version:'', registered:false, map:{} };
    let roster;
    if (!list.length) {
      roster = { version:'', applicantVersion:applicant.version, subjectRegistered:false, applicantRegistered:applicant.registered, students:[] };
    } else {
      const target = parseWungjiDate_(date);
      target.setHours(23,59,59,999);
      let chosen = list[0];
      list.forEach(v => { if (v.uploadedAt <= target) chosen = v; });
      const students = chosen.rows.filter(r => String(r[10] || '') === 'Y' && String(r[8] || '') !== '3728' && applicant.map[String(r[8] || '')]).map(r => {
        const app = applicant.map[String(r[8] || '')];
        return { id:String(r[8]), name:getWungjiEffectiveStudentName_(String(r[8]), r[9]), seatType:app.seatType, seatNumber:app.seatNumber, seatKey:app.seatKey };
      }).sort((a,b) => {
        if (a.seatType !== b.seatType) return a.seatType === '개방형' ? -1 : 1;
        return a.seatNumber - b.seatNumber;
      });
      roster = { version:chosen.version, applicantVersion:applicant.version, subjectRegistered:true, applicantRegistered:applicant.registered, students:students };
    }
    result[date] = roster;
    putWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiRosterCacheKey_(rosterKey,date), roster, WUNGJI_DYNAMIC_CACHE_SECONDS);
  });
  return result;
}

function getWungjiRosterStudentsForDate_(rosterKey, dateKey) {
  const result = buildWungjiRostersForKeys_([String(rosterKey || '')], normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date()));
  return result[String(rosterKey || '')] || { version: '', applicantVersion: '', subjectRegistered: false, applicantRegistered: false, students: [] };
}

function getTeacherWungjiSchedule(userId, password, dateKey, inspectTeacher) {
  const auth = verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, false);
  const targetTeacher = auth.role === 'admin' ? String(inspectTeacher || '').trim() : auth.id;
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date());
  if (!targetTeacher) {
    return { ok: true, role: auth.role, teacher: '', teachers: getWungjiTeacherNames_(), date: date, periods: buildEmptyWungjiPeriods_(date) };
  }
  const ranges = getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_(date);
  const schedule = getEffectiveWungjiScheduleForDate_(date).filter(a => teacherListContains_(a.teacher, targetTeacher));
  const rosterKeys = schedule.map(a => a.rosterKey);
  const counts = getWungjiRosterCountMapForDate_(rosterKeys, date);
  const periods = [];
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) {
    const start = ranges[p].start;
    const end = ranges[p].end;
    const courses = schedule.filter(a => Number(a.period) === p).map(a => {
      const info = counts[a.rosterKey] || { count: 0, state: 'subjectMissing' };
      return {
        period: p, start: start, end: end, subject: a.subject, classGroup: a.classGroup, teacher: a.teacher,
        rosterKey: a.rosterKey, rosterCount: info.count, rosterRegistered: info.state === 'ready', rosterState: info.state
      };
    });
    periods.push({ period: p, start: start, end: end, courses: courses });
  }
  return {
    ok: true, role: auth.role, teacher: targetTeacher, teachers: auth.role === 'admin' ? getWungjiTeacherNames_() : [],
    date: date, dayLabel: WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS[dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(parseWungjiDate_(date))] || '', periods: periods
  };
}

function buildEmptyWungjiPeriods_(dateKey) {
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date());
  const ranges = getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_(date);
  const periods = [];
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) periods.push({ period: p, start: ranges[p].start, end: ranges[p].end, courses: [] });
  return periods;
}

function getWungjiAttendanceDetail(userId, password, request) {
  request = request || {};
  const auth = verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, false);
  const dateKey = normalizeDateKey_(request.date || new Date());
  const rosterKey = String(request.rosterKey || '');
  const schedule = getEffectiveWungjiScheduleForDate_(dateKey);
  const course = schedule.find(a => a.rosterKey === rosterKey && Number(a.period) === Number(request.period));
  if (!course) throw new Error('해당 날짜의 수업을 찾을 수 없습니다.');
  if (auth.role !== 'admin' && !teacherListContains_(course.teacher, auth.id)) throw new Error('본인의 수업만 조회할 수 있습니다.');
  const recentSessions = findRecentWungjiSessions_(course, dateKey, 3);
  const rosterDates = [dateKey].concat(recentSessions.map(s => s.date));
  const rosters = buildWungjiRosterForDates_(rosterKey, rosterDates);
  const roster = rosters[dateKey];
  if (!roster.subjectRegistered) return { ok: false, message: '과목별 출석부 미등록', course: course, rows: [], recent: [] };
  if (!roster.applicantRegistered) return { ok: false, message: '일과 중 웅지실 신청자 명렬표 미등록', course: course, rows: [], recent: [] };
  const sessionRequests = [{ date: dateKey, period: Number(request.period), rosterKey: rosterKey }].concat(
    recentSessions.map(s => ({ date: s.date, period: s.period, rosterKey: rosterKey }))
  );
  const maps = getWungjiAttendanceRecordMapsForSessions_(sessionRequests);
  const currentMapId = dateKey + '|' + Number(request.period) + '|' + rosterKey;
  const attendance = maps[currentMapId] || {};
  const rows = roster.students.map(st => ({
    id: st.id, name: st.name, seatType: st.seatType, seatNumber: st.seatNumber, seatKey: st.seatKey,
    loginTime: formatWungjiTime4_((attendance[st.id] && attendance[st.id].time) || ''), status: getWungjiAttendanceStatusLabel_(attendance[st.id]),
    date: dateKey, period: Number(request.period), rosterKey: rosterKey,
    subject: course.subject, classGroup: course.classGroup, teacher: course.teacher
  })).sort((a, b) => String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true }));
  const recent = recentSessions.map(session => {
    const sessionRoster = rosters[session.date] || getWungjiRosterStudentsForDate_(rosterKey, session.date);
    const map = maps[session.date + '|' + Number(session.period) + '|' + rosterKey] || {};
    const present = sessionRoster.students.filter(s => map[s.id]).length;
    return { date: session.date, label: session.label, period: session.period, present: present, absent: sessionRoster.students.length - present, total: sessionRoster.students.length };
  });
  const counts = getWungjiAttendanceStatusCounts_(rows);
  const presentCount = counts.present;
  const detailDateObj = parseWungjiDate_(dateKey);
  const detailDayLabel = WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS[dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(detailDateObj)] || '';
  const detailTitleLabel = Utilities.formatDate(detailDateObj, TZ, 'MM/dd') + '(' + detailDayLabel + ')';
  const detailRanges = getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_(dateKey);
  const detailRange = detailRanges[Number(request.period)] || { start: '', end: '' };
  return {
    ok: true, date: dateKey, dayLabel: detailDayLabel, titleLabel: detailTitleLabel,
    period: Number(request.period), startTime: detailRange.start, endTime: detailRange.end,
    course: course, courseLabel: course.subject + ' ' + course.classGroup + '반', rows: rows,
    presentCount: presentCount, classCount: counts.classAttend, absentCount: counts.absent, recent: recent
  };
}


function getCurrentWungjiAttendanceStatus(userId, password) {
  const auth = verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, false);
  const now = new Date();
  const session = getCurrentWungjiDisplaySession_(now);
  const titleLabel = Utilities.formatDate(now, TZ, 'MM/dd') + '(' + (WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS[dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(now)] || '') + ')';
  if (!session.ok) {
    return { ok: true, active: false, date: session.date, titleLabel: titleLabel, period: '', rows: [], presentCount: 0, absentCount: 0, totalCount: 0, message: '현재 표시할 일과 중 웅지실 수업이 없습니다.' };
  }
  const schedule = getEffectiveWungjiScheduleForDate_(session.date).filter(a => Number(a.period) === Number(session.period));
  const scopedSchedule = auth.role === 'admin' ? schedule : schedule.filter(a => teacherListContains_(a.teacher, auth.id));
  const rosterKeys = scopedSchedule.map(c => c.rosterKey).filter(Boolean);
  const rosters = buildWungjiRostersForKeys_(rosterKeys, session.date);
  const maps = getWungjiAttendanceRecordMapsForSessions_(scopedSchedule.map(c => ({ date: session.date, period: session.period, rosterKey: c.rosterKey }))); 
  const byStudent = {};
  scopedSchedule.forEach(course => {
    const roster = rosters[course.rosterKey] || { students: [] };
    const attendance = maps[session.date + '|' + Number(session.period) + '|' + String(course.rosterKey || '')] || {};
    (roster.students || []).forEach(st => {
      const key = st.id;
      const rawRecord = attendance[st.id] || null;
      const rawTime = rawRecord && rawRecord.time ? rawRecord.time : '';
      if (!byStudent[key]) {
        byStudent[key] = {
          id: st.id, name: st.name, seatType: st.seatType, seatNumber: st.seatNumber, seatKey: st.seatKey,
          loginTime: formatWungjiTime4_(rawTime), status: getWungjiAttendanceStatusLabel_(rawRecord),
          date: session.date, period: Number(session.period), rosterKey: course.rosterKey,
          subject: course.subject, classGroup: course.classGroup, teacher: course.teacher,
          courseLabel: course.subject + ' ' + course.classGroup + '반'
        };
      } else if (rawTime && byStudent[key].status === WUNGJI_STATUS_ABSENT) {
        byStudent[key].loginTime = formatWungjiTime4_(rawTime);
        byStudent[key].status = getWungjiAttendanceStatusLabel_(rawRecord);
        byStudent[key].rosterKey = course.rosterKey;
        byStudent[key].subject = course.subject;
        byStudent[key].classGroup = course.classGroup;
        byStudent[key].teacher = course.teacher;
        byStudent[key].courseLabel = course.subject + ' ' + course.classGroup + '반';
      }
    });
  });
  const rows = Object.keys(byStudent).map(k => byStudent[k]).sort((a, b) => {
    const at = a.seatType === '개방형' ? 0 : a.seatType === '폐쇄형' ? 1 : 2;
    const bt = b.seatType === '개방형' ? 0 : b.seatType === '폐쇄형' ? 1 : 2;
    if (at !== bt) return at - bt;
    if (Number(a.seatNumber || 0) !== Number(b.seatNumber || 0)) return Number(a.seatNumber || 0) - Number(b.seatNumber || 0);
    return String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true });
  });
  const counts = getWungjiAttendanceStatusCounts_(rows);
  const presentCount = counts.present;
  return {
    ok: true, active: true, date: session.date, titleLabel: titleLabel, period: Number(session.period),
    startTime: session.startTime, endTime: session.endTime, resetBeforeBell: session.resetBeforeBell,
    rows: rows, courses: scopedSchedule.map(c => ({ subject: c.subject, classGroup: c.classGroup, teacher: c.teacher, rosterKey: c.rosterKey })),
    presentCount: presentCount, classCount: counts.classAttend, absentCount: counts.absent, totalCount: rows.length,
    role: auth.role, teacher: auth.role === 'admin' ? '' : auth.id
  };
}

function updateWungjiAttendanceState(userId, password, request) {
  request = request || {};
  const auth = verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, false);
  const dateKey = normalizeDateKey_(request.date || new Date());
  const period = Number(request.period);
  const rosterKey = String(request.rosterKey || '');
  const studentId = normalizeWungjiStudentId_(request.studentId || request.id);
  const action = String(request.action || '').toLowerCase();
  const attendanceMode = normalizeWungjiAttendanceMode_(request.mode || request.attendanceMode || 'wungji');
  if (!dateKey || !(period >= 1 && period <= 7) || !rosterKey || !studentId) throw new Error('출석 처리에 필요한 정보가 부족합니다.');
  const schedule = getEffectiveWungjiScheduleForDate_(dateKey);
  const course = schedule.find(a => a.rosterKey === rosterKey && Number(a.period) === period);
  if (!course) throw new Error('해당 날짜의 수업을 찾을 수 없습니다.');
  if (auth.role !== 'admin' && !teacherListContains_(course.teacher, auth.id)) throw new Error('본인의 수업만 수정할 수 있습니다.');
  const roster = getWungjiRosterStudentsForDate_(rosterKey, dateKey);
  const student = (roster.students || []).find(st => st.id === studentId);
  if (!student) throw new Error('해당 학생은 이 수업의 웅지실 명단에 없습니다.');
  const recordKey = dateKey + '|' + period + '|' + rosterKey + '|' + studentId;
  const cacheKey = getWungjiAttendanceCacheKey_(dateKey, period, rosterKey);
  if (action === 'present') {
    const time4 = normalizeWungjiManualTime4_(request.time || request.loginTime || Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, 'HHmm'));
    const dayNo = dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(parseWungjiDate_(dateKey));
    const status = attendanceMode === 'class' ? WUNGJI_STATUS_CLASS : WUNGJI_STATUS_PRESENT;
    replaceWungjiAttendanceRowLocked_(recordKey, [
      recordKey, dateKey, WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS[dayNo], period, course.classGroup,
      course.subject, course.subjectKey, course.teacher, course.rosterKey,
      studentId, student.name, time4, status, auth.role === 'admin' ? '관리자수정' : '교사수정'
    ], cacheKey);
    fastUpdateWungjiWeeklyStatCell_(dateKey, period, course, studentId, student.name, time4, status);
    return '✅ ' + status + '으로 변경했습니다.\n' + student.name + ' / ' + time4;
  }
  if (action === 'absent') {
    removeWungjiAttendanceRowsLocked_(recordKey, cacheKey);
    fastUpdateWungjiWeeklyStatCell_(dateKey, period, course, studentId, student.name, '', WUNGJI_STATUS_ABSENT);
    return '✅ 출석을 취소했습니다.\n' + student.name;
  }
  throw new Error('출석, 수업참석 또는 출석취소 중 하나를 선택해야 합니다.');
}


function replaceWungjiAttendanceRowLocked_(recordKey, row, cacheKey) {
  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(12000)) throw new Error('접속이 몰려 처리 대기 중입니다. 잠시 후 다시 시도하세요.');
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_LOG_SHEET);
    if (!sheet) throw new Error('웅지실 출석로그 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.');
    deleteWungjiAttendanceRecordRows_(sheet, recordKey);
    sheet.getRange(Math.max(2, sheet.getLastRow() + 1), 1, 1, row.length).setValues([row]);
    removeWungjiCache_(cacheKey);
    removeWungjiCache_(getWungjiAttendanceRecordCacheKey_(row[1], row[3], row[8]));
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function removeWungjiAttendanceRowsLocked_(recordKey, cacheKey) {
  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(12000)) throw new Error('접속이 몰려 처리 대기 중입니다. 잠시 후 다시 시도하세요.');
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_LOG_SHEET);
    if (!sheet) throw new Error('웅지실 출석로그 시트를 찾을 수 없습니다.');
    deleteWungjiAttendanceRecordRows_(sheet, recordKey);
    removeWungjiCache_(cacheKey);
    const parts = String(recordKey || '').split('|');
    const rk = parts.length > 3 ? parts.slice(2, -1).join('|') : (parts[2] || '');
    removeWungjiCache_(getWungjiAttendanceRecordCacheKey_(parts[0], parts[1], rk));
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function deleteWungjiAttendanceRecordRows_(sheet, recordKey) {
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1 || !recordKey) return 0;
  const range = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1);
  let matches = [];
  try {
    matches = range.createTextFinder(String(recordKey)).matchEntireCell(true).findAll() || [];
  } catch (_) {
    matches = [];
  }
  if (!matches.length) return 0;
  const rows = matches.map(cell => cell.getRow()).sort((a, b) => b - a);
  rows.forEach(row => sheet.deleteRow(row));
  return rows.length;
}

function fastUpdateWungjiWeeklyStatCell_(dateKey, period, course, studentId, studentName, loginTime, status) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const name = getWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetName_(dateKey);
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (!sheet) return false;
    const week = getWungjiWeekRange_(dateKey);
    const columns = getWungjiWeeklyStatColumns_(week);
    let targetIndex = -1;
    for (let i = 0; i < columns.length; i++) {
      if (columns[i].dateKey === normalizeDateKey_(dateKey) && Number(columns[i].period) === Number(period)) {
        targetIndex = i;
        break;
      }
    }
    if (targetIndex < 0) return false;
    const col = 3 + targetIndex;
    const idText = normalizeWungjiStudentId_(studentId);
    if (!idText) return false;
    let row = 0;
    const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow >= 3) {
      const found = sheet.getRange(3, 1, lastRow - 2, 1).createTextFinder(idText).matchEntireCell(true).findNext();
      if (found) row = found.getRow();
    }
    if (!row) {
      row = Math.max(3, lastRow + 1);
      sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, 2).setValues([[idText, getWungjiEffectiveStudentName_(idText, studentName || '')]]);
      sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, Math.max(2, 2 + columns.length)).setNumberFormat('@').setHorizontalAlignment('center').setVerticalAlignment('middle');
    }
    let value = '';
    let color = '#202124';
    const normalizedStatus = String(status || '').trim();
    const timeValue = formatWungjiTime4_(loginTime || '');
    if ((normalizedStatus === WUNGJI_STATUS_PRESENT || normalizedStatus === WUNGJI_STATUS_CLASS) && timeValue) {
      value = normalizedStatus === WUNGJI_STATUS_CLASS ? WUNGJI_CLASS_MARK_PREFIX + timeValue : timeValue;
      color = '#202124';
    } else {
      value = getWungjiCourseCellText_(course || {}, dateKey);
      color = '#d93025';
    }
    sheet.getRange(row, col).setValue(value).setFontColor(color);
    return true;
  } catch (e) {
    try { appendWungjiErrorLog_('통계빠른갱신실패', studentId, String(e && e.message || e), normalizeDateKey_(dateKey) + ' ' + period); } catch (_) {}
    return false;
  }
}



function refreshCurrentWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheet() {
  return refreshWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetForDate_(new Date());
}

function refreshWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetForDate_(dateKey) {
  const sheet = rebuildWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetForDate_(dateKey);
  return sheet ? sheet.getName() : '';
}

function ensureWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetForDate_(dateKey, rebuild) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const name = getWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetName_(dateKey);
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet(name);
  if (rebuild || sheet.getLastRow() === 0) rebuildWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetForDate_(dateKey);
  return sheet;
}

function rebuildWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetForDate_(dateKey) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const week = getWungjiWeekRange_(dateKey);
  const name = getWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetName_(dateKey);
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet(name);

  const columns = getWungjiWeeklyStatColumns_(week);
  setupWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheet_(sheet, columns);
  if (!columns.length) return sheet;

  const dateKeys = week.dates.map(d => Utilities.formatDate(d, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd'));
  const applicantsByDate = getWungjiApplicantRostersForDates_(dateKeys);
  const studentsById = {};
  dateKeys.forEach(d => {
    const roster = applicantsByDate[d] || { students: [] };
    (roster.students || []).forEach(st => {
      if (!studentsById[st.id]) studentsById[st.id] = Object.assign({}, st);
    });
  });
  const students = Object.keys(studentsById).map(id => studentsById[id]).sort((a, b) => String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true }));

  const cellByStudent = {};
  const fontByStudent = {};
  students.forEach(st => {
    cellByStudent[st.id] = new Array(columns.length).fill('');
    fontByStudent[st.id] = new Array(columns.length).fill('#202124');
  });

  const columnsByDatePeriod = {};
  columns.forEach((col, idx) => columnsByDatePeriod[col.dateKey + '|' + col.period] = idx);

  dateKeys.forEach(d => {
    const maxPeriod = getWungjiSchoolPeriodLimitForDate_(d);
    if (!maxPeriod) return;
    const schedule = getEffectiveWungjiScheduleForDate_(d).filter(course => Number(course.period) >= 1 && Number(course.period) <= maxPeriod);
    if (!schedule.length) return;
    const rosters = buildWungjiRostersForKeys_(schedule.map(course => course.rosterKey), d);
    const maps = getWungjiAttendanceRecordMapsForSessions_(schedule.map(course => ({ date: d, period: course.period, rosterKey: course.rosterKey }))); 

    schedule.forEach(course => {
      const idx = columnsByDatePeriod[d + '|' + Number(course.period)];
      if (idx == null) return;
      const roster = rosters[course.rosterKey] || { students: [] };
      const attendance = maps[d + '|' + Number(course.period) + '|' + String(course.rosterKey || '')] || {};
      const missText = getWungjiCourseCellText_(course, d);
      (roster.students || []).forEach(st => {
        if (!cellByStudent[st.id]) {
          cellByStudent[st.id] = new Array(columns.length).fill('');
          fontByStudent[st.id] = new Array(columns.length).fill('#202124');
          studentsById[st.id] = Object.assign({}, st);
        }
        const attRecord = attendance[st.id] || null;
        const loginTime = formatWungjiTime4_(attRecord && attRecord.time ? attRecord.time : '');
        if (loginTime) {
          cellByStudent[st.id][idx] = getWungjiWeeklyAttendanceCellValue_(attRecord);
          fontByStudent[st.id][idx] = '#202124';
        } else if (!cellByStudent[st.id][idx]) {
          cellByStudent[st.id][idx] = missText;
          fontByStudent[st.id][idx] = '#d93025';
        } else if (!/^((\(수\))?\d{4})$/.test(String(cellByStudent[st.id][idx]))) {
          cellByStudent[st.id][idx] += ' / ' + missText;
          fontByStudent[st.id][idx] = '#d93025';
        }
      });
    });
  });

  const finalStudents = Object.keys(studentsById).map(id => studentsById[id]).sort((a, b) => String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true }));
  const values = finalStudents.map(st => [st.id, st.name].concat(cellByStudent[st.id] || new Array(columns.length).fill('')));
  const fontColors = finalStudents.map(st => ['#202124', '#202124'].concat(fontByStudent[st.id] || new Array(columns.length).fill('#202124')));

  if (values.length) {
    if (sheet.getMaxRows() < values.length + 2) sheet.insertRowsAfter(sheet.getMaxRows(), values.length + 2 - sheet.getMaxRows());
    sheet.getRange(3, 1, values.length, 2 + columns.length).setValues(values);
    sheet.getRange(3, 1, values.length, 2 + columns.length).setFontColors(fontColors);
  }
  formatWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheet_(sheet, values.length, columns);
  return sheet;
}

function setupWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheet_(sheet, columns) {
  if (!sheet) return;
  columns = columns || [];
  const totalCols = Math.max(2, 2 + columns.length);
  if (sheet.getMaxColumns() < totalCols) sheet.insertColumnsAfter(sheet.getMaxColumns(), totalCols - sheet.getMaxColumns());
  if (sheet.getMaxRows() < 2) sheet.insertRowsAfter(sheet.getMaxRows(), 2 - sheet.getMaxRows());
  try { sheet.getDataRange().breakApart(); } catch (_) {}
  sheet.clear();
  sheet.clearConditionalFormatRules();

  const header1 = ['학번', '이름'];
  const header2 = ['', ''];
  columns.forEach(col => {
    header1.push(col.dayHeader);
    header2.push(col.period + '교시');
  });
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 2, totalCols).setValues([header1, header2]);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 2, 1).merge().setValue('학번');
  sheet.getRange(1, 2, 2, 1).merge().setValue('이름');

  let startCol = 3;
  while (startCol <= totalCols) {
    const label = sheet.getRange(1, startCol).getValue();
    let endCol = startCol;
    while (endCol + 1 <= totalCols && sheet.getRange(1, endCol + 1).getValue() === label) endCol++;
    if (endCol > startCol) sheet.getRange(1, startCol, 1, endCol - startCol + 1).merge();
    startCol = endCol + 1;
  }

  sheet.setFrozenRows(2);
  sheet.setFrozenColumns(2);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 2, totalCols)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setBackground('#eaf2ff')
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle')
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, '#d9e2f3', SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);
}

function formatWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheet_(sheet, rowCount, columns) {
  if (!sheet) return;
  columns = columns || [];
  const lastRow = Math.max(2, rowCount + 2);
  const lastCol = Math.max(2, 2 + columns.length);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol)
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle')
    .setWrapStrategy(SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.WRAP)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, '#d9e2f3', SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);
  if (rowCount > 0) {
    sheet.getRange(3, 1, rowCount, lastCol).setNumberFormat('@');
  }
  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 80);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 90);
  for (let c = 3; c <= lastCol; c++) sheet.setColumnWidth(c, 120);
  try {
    if (sheet.getFilter()) sheet.getFilter().remove();
  } catch (_) {}
}

function getWungjiCourseCellText_(course, dateKey) {
  const subject = String(course.subject || '').trim() || '수업';
  const teacher = getWungjiEffectiveTeacherListForDate_(course.teacher || '', dateKey);
  return subject + '(' + teacher + ')';
}

function getWungjiWeeklyStatColumns_(week) {
  const columns = [];
  (week.dates || []).forEach(date => {
    const dateKey = Utilities.formatDate(date, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const dayNo = getEffectiveWungjiDayNoForDate_(dateKey);
    const maxPeriod = getWungjiSchoolPeriodLimitForDate_(dateKey);
    if (!maxPeriod) return;
    const dayLabel = WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS[dayNo] || '';
    const dayHeader = Utilities.formatDate(date, TZ, 'M/d') + '(' + dayLabel + ')';
    for (let p = 1; p <= maxPeriod; p++) {
      columns.push({ dateKey: dateKey, dayNo: dayNo, dayLabel: dayLabel, dayHeader: dayHeader, period: p });
    }
  });
  return columns;
}

function getWungjiWeeklyCumulativeSheetName_(dateKey) {
  const week = getWungjiWeekRange_(dateKey);
  return WUNGJI_WEEKLY_CUMULATIVE_PREFIX + '(' + formatWungjiShortDate_(week.startKey) + '~' + formatWungjiShortDate_(week.endKey) + ')';
}

function formatWungjiShortDate_(dateKey) {
  const d = parseWungjiDate_(normalizeDateKey_(dateKey));
  return d ? Utilities.formatDate(d, TZ, 'M/d') : String(dateKey || '');
}

function getWungjiWeekRange_(dateKey) {
  const base = parseWungjiDate_(normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date()));
  const day = base.getDay();
  const diffToMonday = day === 0 ? -6 : 1 - day;
  let start = new Date(base.getTime());
  start.setDate(base.getDate() + diffToMonday);
  start.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  const end = new Date(start.getTime());
  end.setDate(start.getDate() + 4);

  const settings = getWungjiSettingsMap_();
  const configuredStart = parseWungjiDate_(normalizeDateKey_(settings.WUNGJI_STATS_START_DATE || WUNGJI_WEEKLY_STAT_START_DATE));
  if (configuredStart && configuredStart > start && configuredStart <= end) {
    start = new Date(configuredStart.getTime());
    start.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  }

  const dates = [];
  const cursor = new Date(start.getTime());
  while (cursor <= end) {
    const d = new Date(cursor.getTime());
    if (d.getDay() >= 1 && d.getDay() <= 5) dates.push(d);
    cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() + 1);
  }
  return {
    start: start,
    end: end,
    startKey: Utilities.formatDate(start, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd'),
    endKey: Utilities.formatDate(end, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd'),
    dates: dates
  };
}

function getWungjiSchoolPeriodLimitForDate_(dateKey) {
  const day = getEffectiveWungjiDayNoForDate_(normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date()));
  if (day === 1 || day === 2 || day === 4) return 6;
  if (day === 3 || day === 5) return 7;
  return 0;
}

function sortWungjiStudentsBySeat_(a, b) {
  const at = a.seatType === '개방형' ? 0 : a.seatType === '폐쇄형' ? 1 : 2;
  const bt = b.seatType === '개방형' ? 0 : b.seatType === '폐쇄형' ? 1 : 2;
  if (at !== bt) return at - bt;
  if (Number(a.seatNumber || 0) !== Number(b.seatNumber || 0)) return Number(a.seatNumber || 0) - Number(b.seatNumber || 0);
  return String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''), 'ko', { numeric: true });
}

function getWungjiAttendanceCacheKey_(dateKey, period, rosterKey) {
  return 'attendance_' + normalizeDateKey_(dateKey) + '_' + Number(period) + '_' + wungjiHash_(rosterKey);
}

function getWungjiAttendanceRecordCacheKey_(dateKey, period, rosterKey) {
  return 'attendance_records_' + normalizeDateKey_(dateKey) + '_' + Number(period) + '_' + wungjiHash_(rosterKey);
}

function getWungjiAttendanceRecordMapsForSessions_(sessions) {
  const result = {};
  const missing = [];
  (sessions || []).forEach(s => {
    const id = normalizeDateKey_(s.date) + '|' + Number(s.period) + '|' + String(s.rosterKey || '');
    const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiAttendanceRecordCacheKey_(s.date, s.period, s.rosterKey));
    if (cached) result[id] = cached;
    else missing.push({ id: id, date: normalizeDateKey_(s.date), period: Number(s.period), rosterKey: String(s.rosterKey || '') });
  });
  if (!missing.length) return result;
  const wanted = {};
  missing.forEach(s => { wanted[s.id] = s; result[s.id] = {}; });
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_LOG_SHEET);
  if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    const rows = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 14).getDisplayValues();
    rows.forEach(r => {
      const id = normalizeDateKey_(r[1]) + '|' + Number(r[3]) + '|' + String(r[8] || '');
      if (!wanted[id]) return;
      const studentId = String(r[9] || '');
      if (!studentId || result[id][studentId]) return;
      const status = String(r[12] || WUNGJI_STATUS_PRESENT).trim() || WUNGJI_STATUS_PRESENT;
      result[id][studentId] = { time: formatWungjiTime4_(r[11] || ''), status: status, source: String(r[13] || '') };
    });
  }
  missing.forEach(s => putWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiAttendanceRecordCacheKey_(s.date, s.period, s.rosterKey), result[s.id], WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_CACHE_SECONDS));
  return result;
}

function getWungjiAttendanceRecordMap_(dateKey, period, rosterKey) {
  const id = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey) + '|' + Number(period) + '|' + String(rosterKey || '');
  return getWungjiAttendanceRecordMapsForSessions_([{ date: dateKey, period: period, rosterKey: rosterKey }])[id] || {};
}

function getWungjiAttendanceStatusLabel_(recordOrTime) {
  if (!recordOrTime) return WUNGJI_STATUS_ABSENT;
  if (typeof recordOrTime === 'string') return recordOrTime ? WUNGJI_STATUS_PRESENT : WUNGJI_STATUS_ABSENT;
  const status = String(recordOrTime.status || '').trim();
  if (status === WUNGJI_STATUS_CLASS) return WUNGJI_STATUS_CLASS;
  if (recordOrTime.time) return WUNGJI_STATUS_PRESENT;
  return WUNGJI_STATUS_ABSENT;
}

function getWungjiAttendanceStatusCounts_(rows) {
  const result = { present: 0, classAttend: 0, absent: 0 };
  (rows || []).forEach(r => {
    if (r.status === WUNGJI_STATUS_PRESENT) result.present++;
    else if (r.status === WUNGJI_STATUS_CLASS) result.classAttend++;
    else result.absent++;
  });
  return result;
}

function getWungjiWeeklyAttendanceCellValue_(record) {
  if (!record || !record.time) return '';
  return getWungjiAttendanceStatusLabel_(record) === WUNGJI_STATUS_CLASS ? WUNGJI_CLASS_MARK_PREFIX + formatWungjiTime4_(record.time) : formatWungjiTime4_(record.time);
}

function getWungjiAttendanceMapsForSessions_(sessions) {
  const result = {};
  const missing = [];
  (sessions || []).forEach(s => {
    const id = normalizeDateKey_(s.date) + '|' + Number(s.period) + '|' + String(s.rosterKey || '');
    const cached = getWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiAttendanceCacheKey_(s.date, s.period, s.rosterKey));
    if (cached) result[id] = cached;
    else missing.push({ id: id, date: normalizeDateKey_(s.date), period: Number(s.period), rosterKey: String(s.rosterKey || '') });
  });
  if (!missing.length) return result;
  const wanted = {};
  missing.forEach(s => wanted[s.id] = s);
  missing.forEach(s => result[s.id] = {});
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_LOG_SHEET);
  if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    const rows = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 14).getDisplayValues();
    rows.forEach(r => {
      const id = normalizeDateKey_(r[1]) + '|' + Number(r[3]) + '|' + String(r[8] || '');
      if (!wanted[id]) return;
      const studentId = String(r[9] || '');
      if (studentId && !result[id][studentId]) result[id][studentId] = r[11];
    });
  }
  missing.forEach(s => putWungjiCacheJson_(getWungjiAttendanceCacheKey_(s.date, s.period, s.rosterKey), result[s.id], WUNGJI_ATTENDANCE_CACHE_SECONDS));
  return result;
}

function getWungjiAttendanceMap_(dateKey, period, rosterKey) {
  const id = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey) + '|' + Number(period) + '|' + String(rosterKey || '');
  return getWungjiAttendanceMapsForSessions_([{ date: dateKey, period: period, rosterKey: rosterKey }])[id] || {};
}

function findRecentWungjiSessions_(course, dateKey, count) {
  const result = [];
  const cursor = parseWungjiDate_(dateKey);
  const data = getWungjiScheduleData_();
  for (let i = 0; i < 120 && result.length < count; i++) {
    const key = Utilities.formatDate(cursor, TZ, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const match = buildEffectiveWungjiScheduleFromData_(key, data).find(a => a.rosterKey === course.rosterKey);
    if (match) result.push({
      date: key, period: match.period,
      label: Utilities.formatDate(cursor, TZ, 'M/d') + '(' + WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS[dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(cursor)] + ') ' + match.period + '교시'
    });
    cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() - 1);
  }
  return result;
}

function getWungjiAdminConfig(userId, password, dateKey) {
  verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, true);
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey || new Date());
  return {
    ok: true,
    date: date,
    defaultRanges: getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_('1900-01-01'),
    dateRanges: getWungjiPeriodRangesForDate_(date),
    teachers: getWungjiTeacherNames_(),
    subjects: getWungjiSubjects_(),
    overrides: getWungjiOverridesForDate_(date),
    applicantCount: getWungjiApplicantRosterForDate_(date).students.length
  };
}

function getWungjiSubjects_() {
  const map = {};
  getWungjiAssignments_().forEach(a => map[a.subjectKey] = a.subject);
  return Object.keys(map).map(k => ({ key: k, name: map[k] })).sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name, 'ko'));
}

function getWungjiOverridesForDate_(dateKey) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_OVERRIDE_SHEET);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return [];
  return sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getDisplayValues().filter(r => normalizeDateKey_(r[0]) === dateKey).map(r => ({ date: normalizeDateKey_(r[0]), type: r[1], baseDay: Number(r[2]) || 0, classGroup: Number(r[3]) || 0, period: Number(r[4]) || 0, subject: r[5], subjectKey: r[6], teacher: r[7] }));
}

function saveWungjiDefaultTimes(userId, password, ranges) {
  verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, true);
  ranges = normalizeWungjiPeriodRangeInput_(ranges);
  validateWungjiPeriodRanges_(ranges);
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_SETTINGS_SHEET);
  const values = sheet.getLastRow() > 1 ? sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 3).getValues() : [];
  const rowMap = {};
  values.forEach((r, i) => rowMap[String(r[0])] = i + 2);
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) {
    const pairs = [
      ['PERIOD_' + p + '_START', ranges[p].start, p + '교시 기본 시작시간'],
      ['PERIOD_' + p + '_END', ranges[p].end, p + '교시 기본 종료시간']
    ];
    pairs.forEach(item => {
      if (rowMap[item[0]]) sheet.getRange(rowMap[item[0]], 2, 1, 2).setValues([[item[1], item[2]]]);
      else sheet.appendRow(item);
    });
  }
  bumpWungjiRevision_();
  return { ok: true, message: '기본 교시 시작·종료 시간을 저장했습니다.' };
}

function saveWungjiDateTimes(userId, password, dateKey, ranges) {
  verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, true);
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey);
  if (!date) throw new Error('날짜를 선택하세요.');
  ranges = normalizeWungjiPeriodRangeInput_(ranges);
  validateWungjiPeriodRanges_(ranges);
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_DATE_TIME_SHEET);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getDisplayValues();
    for (let i = values.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) if (normalizeDateKey_(values[i][0]) === date) sheet.deleteRow(i + 2);
  }
  const now = new Date();
  const rows = [];
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) rows.push([date, p, ranges[p].start, ranges[p].end, now]);
  sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, rows.length, 5).setValues(rows);
  bumpWungjiRevision_();
  return { ok: true, message: date + ' 교시별 시작·종료 시간을 저장했습니다.' };
}

function normalizeWungjiPeriodRangeInput_(ranges) {
  const result = {};
  ranges = ranges || {};
  for (let p = 1; p <= 7; p++) {
    const item = ranges[p] || ranges[String(p)] || {};
    if (typeof item === 'string') result[p] = { start: item, end: addWungjiMinutes_(item, 50) };
    else result[p] = { start: item.start, end: item.end };
  }
  return result;
}


function clearWungjiDateTimes(userId, password, dateKey) {
  verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, true);
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey);
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_DATE_TIME_SHEET);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getDisplayValues();
    for (let i = values.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) if (normalizeDateKey_(values[i][0]) === date) sheet.deleteRow(i + 2);
  }
  bumpWungjiRevision_();
  return { ok: true, message: date + '의 단축수업 설정을 삭제했습니다.' };
}


function saveWungjiDayMap(userId, password, dateKey, dayNo) {
  verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, true);
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey);
  dayNo = Number(dayNo);
  if (!date || !(dayNo >= 1 && dayNo <= 5)) throw new Error('날짜와 적용 요일을 확인하세요.');
  deleteWungjiOverrides_(date, '요일적용');
  SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_OVERRIDE_SHEET).appendRow([date, '요일적용', dayNo, '', '', '', '', '', new Date()]);
  bumpWungjiRevision_();
  return { ok: true, message: date + '에 ' + WUNGJI_DAY_LABELS[dayNo] + '요일 시간표를 적용했습니다.' };
}


function swapWungjiDates(userId, password, dateA, dateB) {
  verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, true);
  dateA = normalizeDateKey_(dateA); dateB = normalizeDateKey_(dateB);
  const a = parseWungjiDate_(dateA), b = parseWungjiDate_(dateB);
  if (!a || !b) throw new Error('교환할 두 날짜를 선택하세요.');
  const dayA = dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(a), dayB = dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(b);
  if (!(dayA >= 1 && dayA <= 5 && dayB >= 1 && dayB <= 5)) throw new Error('평일 날짜를 선택하세요.');
  deleteWungjiOverrides_(dateA, '요일적용');
  deleteWungjiOverrides_(dateB, '요일적용');
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_OVERRIDE_SHEET);
  sheet.appendRow([dateA, '요일적용', dayB, '', '', '', '', '', new Date()]);
  sheet.appendRow([dateB, '요일적용', dayA, '', '', '', '', '', new Date()]);
  bumpWungjiRevision_();
  return { ok: true, message: dateA + '와 ' + dateB + '의 요일 시간표를 맞교환했습니다.' };
}


function clearWungjiOverridesForDate(userId, password, dateKey) {
  verifyWungjiCredentials_(userId, password, true);
  const date = normalizeDateKey_(dateKey);
  deleteWungjiOverrides_(date);
  bumpWungjiRevision_();
  return { ok: true, message: date + '의 시간표 변경을 모두 삭제했습니다.' };
}


function deleteWungjiOverrides_(dateKey, type, classGroup, period) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_OVERRIDE_SHEET);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;
  const rows = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getDisplayValues();
  for (let i = rows.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    const r = rows[i];
    if (normalizeDateKey_(r[0]) !== dateKey) continue;
    if (type && r[1] !== type) continue;
    if (classGroup && Number(r[3]) !== Number(classGroup)) continue;
    if (period && Number(r[4]) !== Number(period)) continue;
    sheet.deleteRow(i + 2);
  }
}

function appendWungjiUploadLog_(uploader, type, fileName, result, detail) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_UPLOAD_LOG_SHEET);
  sheet.appendRow([new Date(), uploader, type, fileName, result, detail]);
}

function appendWungjiErrorLog_(type, id, content, detail) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(WUNGJI_ERROR_LOG_SHEET);
  sheet.appendRow([new Date(), type, id, content, detail]);
}

function parseWungjiCourseCell_(cell) {
  const text = String(cell || '').replace(/\n/g, ' ').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
  const m = text.match(/^(.*)\(([^()]*)\)\s*$/);
  if (!m) return { subject: '', teacher: '' };
  return { subject: m[1].trim(), teacher: m[2].replace(/\s+/g, '').trim() };
}

function normalizeWungjiSubjectKey_(value) {
  return String(value || '')
    .replace(/Ⅰ/g, '1').replace(/Ⅱ/g, '2').replace(/Ⅲ/g, '3').replace(/Ⅳ/g, '4')
    .replace(/\bIV\b/gi, '4').replace(/\bIII\b/gi, '3').replace(/\bII\b/gi, '2').replace(/\bI\b/gi, '1')
    .replace(/\s+/g, '').replace(/[·ㆍ.,:：()\[\]{}_-]/g, '').toLowerCase();
}

function normalizeWungjiTeacherList_(value) {
  const list = String(value || '').replace(/[，、/]/g, ',').split(',').map(x => x.replace(/\s+/g, '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
  const unique = {};
  list.forEach(x => unique[x] = true);
  return Object.keys(unique).sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'ko')).join(',');
}

function teacherListContains_(teacherList, teacher) {
  const target = getWungjiTeacherAliasForMatch_(teacher);
  return normalizeWungjiTeacherList_(teacherList).split(',').map(t => getWungjiTeacherAliasForMatch_(t)).indexOf(target) >= 0;
}

function makeWungjiRosterKey_(teacher, subjectKey, classGroup) {
  return normalizeWungjiTeacherList_(teacher) + '|' + normalizeWungjiSubjectKey_(subjectKey) + '|' + Number(classGroup);
}

function normalizeWungjiHeader_(value) {
  return String(value || '').replace(/\s+/g, '').replace(/[.:：]/g, '');
}

function normalizeWungjiStudentId_(value) {
  const text = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim().replace(/\.0$/, '');
  return /^3[1-8]\d{2}$/.test(text) ? text : '';
}

function cleanWungjiStudentName_(value) {
  return String(value || '').replace(/\(\s*공동\s*\)/g, '').replace(/\(\s*위탁\s*\)/g, '').replace(/\s+/g, '').trim();
}

function parseSmallInteger_(value) {
  const m = String(value == null ? '' : value).match(/\d+/);
  return m ? Number(m[0]) : 0;
}

function dayLabelToNumber_(label) {
  return { '월': 1, '화': 2, '수': 3, '목': 4, '금': 5 }[label] || 0;
}

function dayLabelToNumberFromDate_(date) {
  const day = date.getDay();
  return day >= 1 && day <= 5 ? day : 0;
}

function parseWungjiDate_(value) {
  const key = normalizeDateKey_(value);
  const m = key.match(/^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})$/);
  if (!m) return null;
  return new Date(Number(m[1]), Number(m[2]) - 1, Number(m[3]), 12, 0, 0);
}

function normalizeWungjiTime_(value) {
  if (value instanceof Date) return Utilities.formatDate(value, TZ, 'HH:mm');
  const text = String(value || '').trim();
  let m = text.match(/^(\d{1,2}):(\d{2})$/);
  if (!m) m = text.match(/^(\d{2})(\d{2})$/);
  if (!m) return '';
  const h = Number(m[1]), min = Number(m[2]);
  if (h < 0 || h > 23 || min < 0 || min > 59) return '';
  return String(h).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(min).padStart(2, '0');
}

function parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(value) {
  const t = normalizeWungjiTime_(value);
  if (!t) return -1;
  const p = t.split(':').map(Number);
  return p[0] * 60 + p[1];
}

function addWungjiMinutes_(time, minutes) {
  const total = parseWungjiTimeMinutes_(time) + Number(minutes || 0);
  return String(Math.floor(total / 60) % 24).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(total % 60).padStart(2, '0');
}

function escapeWungjiHtml_(value) {
  return String(value == null ? '' : value).replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/'/g, '&#039;');
}
